// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/main.c

/*
 * main.c — CLI entry point for NC AI.
 *
 * The NC AI engine: a purpose-built AI for generating NC language code.
 * Supports code generation, document-driven generation, model training,
 * tokenization, and provider bridging.
 *
 * Part of NC AI by DevHeal Labs AI.
 */

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdbool.h>

#include "nc_model.h"
#include "nc_tokenizer.h"
#include "nc_generate.h"
#include "nc_training.h"
#include "nc_dataset.h"
#include "nc_ai_bridge.h"

#define NC_AI_VERSION "0.1.0"
#define NC_AI_NAME    "NC AI"

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Forward declarations
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static void print_help(void);
static void print_version(void);
static int  cmd_generate(int argc, char **argv);
static int  cmd_doc(int argc, char **argv);
static int  cmd_train(int argc, char **argv);
static int  cmd_bridge(int argc, char **argv);
static int  cmd_tokenize(int argc, char **argv);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Help text
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static void print_help(void) {
    printf("\n");
    printf("  %s v%s — AI Engine for NC Language\n", NC_AI_NAME, NC_AI_VERSION);
    printf("  by DevHeal Labs AI\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Usage:\n");
    printf("    nc-ai <command> [options]\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Commands:\n");
    printf("    generate <description>          Generate NC backend code\n");
    printf("    generate --ui <description>     Generate NC UI code\n");
    printf("    generate --full <description>   Generate both backend + UI\n");
    printf("    doc <spec.md>                   Generate project from document\n");
    printf("    doc <spec.md> --output <dir>    Generate with custom output\n");
    printf("    train                           Train model on NC examples\n");
    printf("    train --data <dir>              Train on custom data directory\n");
    printf("    bridge --list                   List available AI providers\n");
    printf("    bridge --set <provider>         Set active provider\n");
    printf("    tokenize <text>                 Tokenize text into tokens\n");
    printf("    version                         Show version\n");
    printf("    help                            Show this help message\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Examples:\n");
    printf("    nc-ai generate \"a blog service\"\n");
    printf("    nc-ai generate --ui \"a portfolio page\"\n");
    printf("    nc-ai generate --full \"a todo app\"\n");
    printf("    nc-ai doc blog_spec.md --output ./my-blog\n");
    printf("    nc-ai train --data ./examples/\n");
    printf("    nc-ai bridge --set openai\n");
    printf("\n");
}

static void print_version(void) {
    printf("%s v%s\n", NC_AI_NAME, NC_AI_VERSION);
    printf("Built with: C11, no external dependencies\n");
    printf("By DevHeal Labs AI\n");
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Command: generate
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int cmd_generate(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc < 1) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: 'generate' requires a description.\n");
        fprintf(stderr, "Usage: nc-ai generate [--ui|--full] <description>\n");
        return 1;
    }

    /* Parse flags */
    bool gen_ui   = false;
    bool gen_full = false;
    const char *description = NULL;

    for (int i = 0; i < argc; i++) {
        if (strcmp(argv[i], "--ui") == 0) {
            gen_ui = true;
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--full") == 0) {
            gen_full = true;
        } else if (argv[i][0] != '-') {
            description = argv[i];
        }
    }

    if (!description) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: no description provided.\n");
        return 1;
    }

    printf("[NC AI] Generating code for: \"%s\"\n", description);

    if (gen_full) {
        printf("[NC AI] Mode: full app (backend + UI)\n");
    } else if (gen_ui) {
        printf("[NC AI] Mode: NC UI only\n");
    } else {
        printf("[NC AI] Mode: backend service\n");
    }

    /* Dispatch to nc_generate */
    NCGenerator *gen = nc_generator_create();
    if (!gen) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: failed to create generator.\n");
        return 1;
    }

    char *code = nc_generate_code(gen, description);
    if (code) {
        printf("\n--- Generated NC Code ---\n\n");
        printf("%s\n", code);
        free(code);
    } else {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: code generation failed.\n");
        nc_generator_free(gen);
        return 1;
    }

    nc_generator_free(gen);
    return 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Command: doc
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int cmd_doc(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc < 1) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: 'doc' requires a specification file.\n");
        fprintf(stderr, "Usage: nc-ai doc <spec.md> [--output <dir>]\n");
        return 1;
    }

    const char *spec_path  = argv[0];
    const char *output_dir = NULL;

    for (int i = 1; i < argc; i++) {
        if (strcmp(argv[i], "--output") == 0 && i + 1 < argc) {
            output_dir = argv[++i];
        }
    }

    printf("[NC AI] Generating project from: %s\n", spec_path);
    if (output_dir) {
        printf("[NC AI] Output directory: %s\n", output_dir);
    } else {
        printf("[NC AI] Output directory: ./generated/\n");
    }

    /* Read the spec file */
    FILE *fp = fopen(spec_path, "r");
    if (!fp) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: cannot open '%s'\n", spec_path);
        return 1;
    }

    fseek(fp, 0, SEEK_END);
    long fsize = ftell(fp);
    fseek(fp, 0, SEEK_SET);

    char *spec = (char *)malloc(fsize + 1);
    if (!spec) {
        fclose(fp);
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: out of memory.\n");
        return 1;
    }

    fread(spec, 1, fsize, fp);
    spec[fsize] = '\0';
    fclose(fp);

    printf("[NC AI] Spec loaded (%ld bytes). Parsing intent...\n", fsize);

    NCGenerator *gen = nc_generator_create();
    if (!gen) {
        free(spec);
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: failed to create generator.\n");
        return 1;
    }

    char *code = nc_generate_code(gen, spec);
    if (code) {
        printf("\n--- Generated Project ---\n\n");
        printf("%s\n", code);
        free(code);
    } else {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: generation from document failed.\n");
    }

    free(spec);
    nc_generator_free(gen);
    return 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Command: train
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int cmd_train(int argc, char **argv) {
    const char *data_dir = NULL;

    for (int i = 0; i < argc; i++) {
        if (strcmp(argv[i], "--data") == 0 && i + 1 < argc) {
            data_dir = argv[++i];
        }
    }

    printf("[NC AI] Starting training...\n");
    if (data_dir) {
        printf("[NC AI] Training data: %s\n", data_dir);
    } else {
        printf("[NC AI] Using synthetic NC dataset.\n");
    }

    /* Forward to nc_cmd_train */
    return nc_cmd_train(argc, argv);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Command: bridge
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int cmd_bridge(int argc, char **argv) {
    bool list_providers = false;
    const char *set_provider = NULL;

    for (int i = 0; i < argc; i++) {
        if (strcmp(argv[i], "--list") == 0) {
            list_providers = true;
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--set") == 0 && i + 1 < argc) {
            set_provider = argv[++i];
        }
    }

    NCAIBridge *bridge = nc_ai_bridge_create();
    if (!bridge) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: failed to create bridge.\n");
        return 1;
    }

    /* Auto-detect available providers */
    int found = nc_ai_bridge_auto_detect(bridge);

    if (list_providers) {
        printf("[NC AI] Available providers (%d):\n", bridge->n_providers);
        for (int i = 0; i < bridge->n_providers; i++) {
            const char *marker = (i == bridge->active_provider) ? " (active)" : "";
            printf("  [%d] %s%s\n", i, bridge->providers[i].name, marker);
        }
        nc_ai_bridge_free(bridge);
        return 0;
    }

    if (set_provider) {
        int result = nc_ai_bridge_set_active_by_name(bridge, set_provider);
        if (result == 0) {
            printf("[NC AI] Active provider set to: %s\n", set_provider);
        } else {
            fprintf(stderr, "Error: provider '%s' not found.\n", set_provider);
            fprintf(stderr, "Run 'nc-ai bridge --list' to see available providers.\n");
            nc_ai_bridge_free(bridge);
            return 1;
        }
        nc_ai_bridge_free(bridge);
        return 0;
    }

    /* No flags: show summary */
    printf("[NC AI] Bridge status:\n");
    printf("  Providers detected: %d\n", found);
    if (bridge->n_providers > 0) {
        NCAIProviderConfig *active = nc_ai_bridge_get_active(bridge);
        if (active) {
            printf("  Active provider: %s\n", active->name);
        }
    }
    nc_ai_bridge_free(bridge);
    return 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Command: tokenize
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int cmd_tokenize(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc < 1) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: 'tokenize' requires text input.\n");
        fprintf(stderr, "Usage: nc-ai tokenize \"text to tokenize\"\n");
        return 1;
    }

    const char *text = argv[0];
    printf("[NC AI] Tokenizing: \"%s\"\n\n", text);

    NCTokenizer *tok = nc_tokenizer_create();
    if (!tok) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: failed to create tokenizer.\n");
        return 1;
    }

    int tokens[512];
    int n_tokens = nc_tokenizer_encode(tok, text, tokens, 512);

    printf("Tokens (%d):\n", n_tokens);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_tokens; i++) {
        char decoded[256];
        int single[1] = { tokens[i] };
        nc_tokenizer_decode(tok, single, 1, decoded, 256);
        printf("  [%3d] id=%-5d  \"%s\"\n", i, tokens[i], decoded);
    }

    nc_tokenizer_free(tok);
    return 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Main
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int main(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc < 2) {
        print_help();
        return 0;
    }

    const char *command = argv[1];

    if (strcmp(command, "help") == 0 || strcmp(command, "--help") == 0 || strcmp(command, "-h") == 0) {
        print_help();
        return 0;
    }

    if (strcmp(command, "version") == 0 || strcmp(command, "--version") == 0 || strcmp(command, "-v") == 0) {
        print_version();
        return 0;
    }

    if (strcmp(command, "generate") == 0) {
        return cmd_generate(argc - 2, argv + 2);
    }

    if (strcmp(command, "doc") == 0) {
        return cmd_doc(argc - 2, argv + 2);
    }

    if (strcmp(command, "train") == 0) {
        return cmd_train(argc - 2, argv + 2);
    }

    if (strcmp(command, "bridge") == 0) {
        return cmd_bridge(argc - 2, argv + 2);
    }

    if (strcmp(command, "tokenize") == 0) {
        return cmd_tokenize(argc - 2, argv + 2);
    }

    fprintf(stderr, "Error: unknown command '%s'\n", command);
    fprintf(stderr, "Run 'nc-ai help' for usage.\n");
    return 1;
}


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_bridge.c

/*
 * nc_ai_bridge.c — Provider-agnostic LLM connector for NC AI.
 *
 * Implements HTTP-based connections to OpenAI, Anthropic, Ollama,
 * and custom endpoints, plus local NC model inference.
 *
 * HTTP is done via system curl + popen (no libcurl dependency).
 * JSON parsing is hand-rolled (no external JSON library).
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 */

#include "nc_ai_bridge.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>
#include <stdarg.h>
#include <time.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <errno.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Forward declarations for NC model/tokenizer types.
 *  We do NOT #include nc_model.h or nc_tokenizer.h here —
 *  they are linked separately. We cast via void*.
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* From nc_model.h */
typedef struct NCModel_Opaque NCModel_Opaque;
extern void *nc_model_load(const char *path);
extern void  nc_model_forward(const void *model, const int *tokens,
                              int seq_len, float *logits);
extern int   nc_model_generate(const void *model, const int *prompt_tokens,
                               int prompt_len, int max_tokens,
                               float temperature, int *output);
extern void  nc_model_free(void *model);

/* Wrapper functions to bridge void* to actual types */
#include "nc_tokenizer.h"
static void *_nc_tok_load(const char *path) {
    return (void *)nc_tokenizer_load(path);
}
static int _nc_tok_encode(const void *tok, const char *text, int *tokens, int max_len) {
    return nc_tokenizer_encode((const NCTokenizer *)tok, text, tokens, max_len);
}
static int _nc_tok_decode(const void *tok, const int *tokens, int n, char *text, int max_len) {
    return nc_tokenizer_decode((const NCTokenizer *)tok, tokens, n, text, max_len);
}
static void _nc_tok_free(void *tok) {
    if (tok) nc_tokenizer_free((NCTokenizer *)tok);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Internal constants
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

#define NC_BRG_BUF_INIT   4096
#define NC_BRG_BUF_MAX    (2 << 20)   /* 2 MiB */
#define NC_BRG_RESP_MAX   (4 << 20)   /* 4 MiB max response */
#define NC_BRG_CMD_MAX    (1 << 20)   /* 1 MiB max curl cmd */
#define NC_BRG_MAX_TOKENS 4096

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Dynamic string buffer (same pattern as nc_generate.c)
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    char  *data;
    size_t len;
    size_t cap;
} NCBrgBuf;

static NCBrgBuf brg_buf_new(void) {
    NCBrgBuf b;
    b.cap  = NC_BRG_BUF_INIT;
    b.len  = 0;
    b.data = (char *)malloc(b.cap);
    if (b.data) b.data[0] = '\0';
    return b;
}

static void brg_buf_free(NCBrgBuf *b) {
    free(b->data);
    b->data = NULL;
    b->len  = 0;
    b->cap  = 0;
}

static void brg_buf_grow(NCBrgBuf *b, size_t need) {
    if (b->len + need + 1 <= b->cap) return;
    size_t new_cap = b->cap * 2;
    while (new_cap < b->len + need + 1) new_cap *= 2;
    if (new_cap > NC_BRG_BUF_MAX) new_cap = NC_BRG_BUF_MAX;
    char *tmp = (char *)realloc(b->data, new_cap);
    if (!tmp) return;
    b->data = tmp;
    b->cap  = new_cap;
}

static void brg_buf_append(NCBrgBuf *b, const char *s) {
    size_t slen = strlen(s);
    brg_buf_grow(b, slen);
    if (b->len + slen + 1 > b->cap) return; /* overflow guard */
    memcpy(b->data + b->len, s, slen);
    b->len += slen;
    b->data[b->len] = '\0';
}

static void brg_buf_printf(NCBrgBuf *b, const char *fmt, ...) {
    va_list ap;
    va_start(ap, fmt);
    char tmp[4096];
    int n = vsnprintf(tmp, sizeof(tmp), fmt, ap);
    va_end(ap);
    if (n > 0) {
        brg_buf_grow(b, (size_t)n);
        if (b->len + (size_t)n + 1 <= b->cap) {
            memcpy(b->data + b->len, tmp, (size_t)n);
            b->len += (size_t)n;
            b->data[b->len] = '\0';
        }
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  String utilities
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *brg_strdup(const char *s) {
    if (!s) return NULL;
    size_t len = strlen(s);
    char *out = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
    if (out) memcpy(out, s, len + 1);
    return out;
}

/* Escape a string for use inside a JSON value.
 * Caller must free the result. */
static char *json_escape(const char *s) {
    if (!s) return brg_strdup("");
    size_t len = strlen(s);
    /* Worst case: every char needs \uXXXX (6 chars) */
    char *out = (char *)malloc(len * 6 + 1);
    if (!out) return brg_strdup("");
    size_t j = 0;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        unsigned char c = (unsigned char)s[i];
        switch (c) {
            case '"':  out[j++] = '\\'; out[j++] = '"';  break;
            case '\\': out[j++] = '\\'; out[j++] = '\\'; break;
            case '\b': out[j++] = '\\'; out[j++] = 'b';  break;
            case '\f': out[j++] = '\\'; out[j++] = 'f';  break;
            case '\n': out[j++] = '\\'; out[j++] = 'n';  break;
            case '\r': out[j++] = '\\'; out[j++] = 'r';  break;
            case '\t': out[j++] = '\\'; out[j++] = 't';  break;
            default:
                if (c < 0x20) {
                    j += (size_t)sprintf(out + j, "\\u%04x", c);
                } else {
                    out[j++] = (char)c;
                }
                break;
        }
    }
    out[j] = '\0';
    return out;
}

/* Escape a string for safe use in a shell single-quote context.
 * We replace ' with '\'' . Caller must free. */
static char *shell_escape(const char *s) {
    if (!s) return brg_strdup("");
    size_t len = strlen(s);
    char *out = (char *)malloc(len * 4 + 1);
    if (!out) return brg_strdup("");
    size_t j = 0;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        if (s[i] == '\'') {
            out[j++] = '\'';
            out[j++] = '\\';
            out[j++] = '\'';
            out[j++] = '\'';
        } else {
            out[j++] = s[i];
        }
    }
    out[j] = '\0';
    return out;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Simple JSON value extraction (no library)
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* Find "key": "value" and return value (caller frees).
 * Handles nested quotes. Returns NULL if not found. */
static char *json_extract_string(const char *json, const char *key) {
    if (!json || !key) return NULL;

    char search[256];
    snprintf(search, sizeof(search), "\"%s\"", key);

    const char *pos = strstr(json, search);
    if (!pos) return NULL;

    /* Advance past "key" */
    pos += strlen(search);

    /* Skip whitespace and colon */
    while (*pos && (*pos == ' ' || *pos == '\t' || *pos == '\n' ||
                    *pos == '\r' || *pos == ':'))
        pos++;

    if (*pos != '"') return NULL;
    pos++; /* skip opening quote */

    /* Collect until unescaped closing quote */
    NCBrgBuf val = brg_buf_new();
    while (*pos && *pos != '"') {
        if (*pos == '\\' && *(pos + 1)) {
            pos++;
            switch (*pos) {
                case '"':  brg_buf_append(&val, "\""); break;
                case '\\': brg_buf_append(&val, "\\"); break;
                case 'n':  brg_buf_append(&val, "\n"); break;
                case 't':  brg_buf_append(&val, "\t"); break;
                case 'r':  brg_buf_append(&val, "\r"); break;
                default: {
                    char esc[3] = { '\\', *pos, '\0' };
                    brg_buf_append(&val, esc);
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            char ch[2] = { *pos, '\0' };
            brg_buf_append(&val, ch);
        }
        pos++;
    }

    char *result = brg_strdup(val.data);
    brg_buf_free(&val);
    return result;
}

/* Extract integer value for "key": 123 */
static int json_extract_int(const char *json, const char *key, int def) {
    if (!json || !key) return def;

    char search[256];
    snprintf(search, sizeof(search), "\"%s\"", key);

    const char *pos = strstr(json, search);
    if (!pos) return def;
    pos += strlen(search);

    while (*pos && (*pos == ' ' || *pos == '\t' || *pos == ':'))
        pos++;

    if (!isdigit((unsigned char)*pos) && *pos != '-') return def;
    return atoi(pos);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  HTTP POST via system curl + popen
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *http_post(const char *url, const char *headers[],
                       int n_headers, const char *body, int timeout_ms) {
    if (!url) return NULL;

    NCBrgBuf cmd = brg_buf_new();
    brg_buf_append(&cmd, "curl -s -S --max-time ");
    brg_buf_printf(&cmd, "%d", timeout_ms > 0 ? timeout_ms / 1000 : 30);

    /* Add headers */
    for (int i = 0; i < n_headers; i++) {
        char *esc = shell_escape(headers[i]);
        brg_buf_printf(&cmd, " -H '%s'", esc);
        free(esc);
    }

    /* Add body */
    if (body) {
        char *esc = shell_escape(body);
        brg_buf_printf(&cmd, " -d '%s'", esc);
        free(esc);
    }

    /* Add URL */
    char *esc_url = shell_escape(url);
    brg_buf_printf(&cmd, " '%s'", esc_url);
    free(esc_url);

    /* Redirect stderr to /dev/null for cleaner output */
    brg_buf_append(&cmd, " 2>/dev/null");

    /* Execute */
    FILE *fp = popen(cmd.data, "r");
    brg_buf_free(&cmd);
    if (!fp) return NULL;

    NCBrgBuf resp = brg_buf_new();
    char chunk[4096];
    while (fgets(chunk, sizeof(chunk), fp)) {
        brg_buf_append(&resp, chunk);
        if (resp.len > NC_BRG_RESP_MAX) break;
    }
    pclose(fp);

    if (resp.len == 0) {
        brg_buf_free(&resp);
        return NULL;
    }

    /* Return owned string (caller frees via free()) */
    char *result = resp.data;
    resp.data = NULL; /* prevent brg_buf_free from freeing */
    return result;
}

/* Quick HTTP GET (for health checks) */
static int http_check(const char *url, int timeout_ms) {
    char cmd[1024];
    snprintf(cmd, sizeof(cmd),
             "curl -s -o /dev/null -w '%%{http_code}' --max-time %d '%s' 2>/dev/null",
             timeout_ms > 0 ? timeout_ms / 1000 : 2, url);
    FILE *fp = popen(cmd, "r");
    if (!fp) return 0;
    char buf[16] = {0};
    if (fgets(buf, sizeof(buf), fp)) {
        pclose(fp);
        int code = atoi(buf);
        return (code >= 200 && code < 500);
    }
    pclose(fp);
    return 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Provider-specific request formatters
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *format_openai_request(const char *prompt, const char *system,
                                   NCAIProviderConfig *cfg) {
    NCBrgBuf body = brg_buf_new();
    char *esc_prompt = json_escape(prompt);
    char *esc_system = system ? json_escape(system) : brg_strdup("You are a helpful assistant.");
    const char *model = cfg->model_name ? cfg->model_name : "gpt-4";
    float temp = cfg->temperature > 0 ? cfg->temperature : 0.7f;
    int max_tok = cfg->max_tokens > 0 ? cfg->max_tokens : NC_BRG_MAX_TOKENS;

    brg_buf_printf(&body,
        "{\"model\":\"%s\","
        "\"temperature\":%.2f,"
        "\"max_tokens\":%d,"
        "\"messages\":["
        "{\"role\":\"system\",\"content\":\"%s\"},"
        "{\"role\":\"user\",\"content\":\"%s\"}"
        "]}",
        model, temp, max_tok, esc_system, esc_prompt);

    free(esc_prompt);
    free(esc_system);

    char *result = body.data;
    body.data = NULL;
    return result;
}

static char *format_anthropic_request(const char *prompt, const char *system,
                                      NCAIProviderConfig *cfg) {
    NCBrgBuf body = brg_buf_new();
    char *esc_prompt = json_escape(prompt);
    char *esc_system = system ? json_escape(system) : brg_strdup("You are a helpful assistant.");
    const char *model = cfg->model_name ? cfg->model_name : "claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022";
    float temp = cfg->temperature > 0 ? cfg->temperature : 0.7f;
    int max_tok = cfg->max_tokens > 0 ? cfg->max_tokens : NC_BRG_MAX_TOKENS;

    brg_buf_printf(&body,
        "{\"model\":\"%s\","
        "\"max_tokens\":%d,"
        "\"temperature\":%.2f,"
        "\"system\":\"%s\","
        "\"messages\":["
        "{\"role\":\"user\",\"content\":\"%s\"}"
        "]}",
        model, max_tok, temp, esc_system, esc_prompt);

    free(esc_prompt);
    free(esc_system);

    char *result = body.data;
    body.data = NULL;
    return result;
}

static char *format_ollama_request(const char *prompt, const char *system,
                                   NCAIProviderConfig *cfg) {
    NCBrgBuf body = brg_buf_new();
    char *esc_prompt = json_escape(prompt);
    const char *model = cfg->model_name ? cfg->model_name : "llama3";
    float temp = cfg->temperature > 0 ? cfg->temperature : 0.7f;

    if (system) {
        char *esc_system = json_escape(system);
        brg_buf_printf(&body,
            "{\"model\":\"%s\","
            "\"prompt\":\"%s\","
            "\"system\":\"%s\","
            "\"stream\":false,"
            "\"options\":{\"temperature\":%.2f}}",
            model, esc_prompt, esc_system, temp);
        free(esc_system);
    } else {
        brg_buf_printf(&body,
            "{\"model\":\"%s\","
            "\"prompt\":\"%s\","
            "\"stream\":false,"
            "\"options\":{\"temperature\":%.2f}}",
            model, esc_prompt, temp);
    }

    free(esc_prompt);

    char *result = body.data;
    body.data = NULL;
    return result;
}

static char *format_custom_request(const char *prompt, const char *system,
                                   NCAIProviderConfig *cfg) {
    NCBrgBuf body = brg_buf_new();
    char *esc_prompt = json_escape(prompt);
    float temp = cfg->temperature > 0 ? cfg->temperature : 0.7f;
    int max_tok = cfg->max_tokens > 0 ? cfg->max_tokens : NC_BRG_MAX_TOKENS;

    if (system) {
        char *esc_system = json_escape(system);
        brg_buf_printf(&body,
            "{\"prompt\":\"%s\","
            "\"system\":\"%s\","
            "\"temperature\":%.2f,"
            "\"max_tokens\":%d}",
            esc_prompt, esc_system, temp, max_tok);
        free(esc_system);
    } else {
        brg_buf_printf(&body,
            "{\"prompt\":\"%s\","
            "\"temperature\":%.2f,"
            "\"max_tokens\":%d}",
            esc_prompt, temp, max_tok);
    }

    free(esc_prompt);

    char *result = body.data;
    body.data = NULL;
    return result;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Provider-specific response parsers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* OpenAI: extract choices[0].message.content */
static NCAIResponse *parse_openai_response(const char *json) {
    NCAIResponse *resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
    if (!resp) return NULL;

    /* Check for error */
    char *err = json_extract_string(json, "error");
    if (err) {
        char *msg = json_extract_string(json, "message");
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = msg ? msg : err;
        if (msg) free(err);
        return resp;
    }

    /* Find "content" inside "message" inside "choices" */
    const char *choices = strstr(json, "\"choices\"");
    if (!choices) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("No 'choices' field in OpenAI response");
        return resp;
    }

    const char *message = strstr(choices, "\"message\"");
    if (!message) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("No 'message' field in OpenAI response");
        return resp;
    }

    resp->content = json_extract_string(message, "content");
    if (!resp->content) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("Could not extract content from OpenAI response");
        return resp;
    }

    resp->success = 1;
    resp->tokens_used = json_extract_int(json, "total_tokens", 0);
    return resp;
}

/* Anthropic: extract content[0].text */
static NCAIResponse *parse_anthropic_response(const char *json) {
    NCAIResponse *resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
    if (!resp) return NULL;

    /* Check for error */
    char *err_type = json_extract_string(json, "type");
    if (err_type && strcmp(err_type, "error") == 0) {
        char *msg = json_extract_string(json, "message");
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = msg ? msg : brg_strdup("Anthropic API error");
        free(err_type);
        return resp;
    }
    free(err_type);

    /* Find "content" array and extract "text" */
    const char *content_arr = strstr(json, "\"content\"");
    if (!content_arr) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("No 'content' field in Anthropic response");
        return resp;
    }

    resp->content = json_extract_string(content_arr, "text");
    if (!resp->content) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("Could not extract text from Anthropic response");
        return resp;
    }

    resp->success = 1;
    resp->tokens_used = json_extract_int(json, "output_tokens", 0);
    return resp;
}

/* Ollama: extract response field */
static NCAIResponse *parse_ollama_response(const char *json) {
    NCAIResponse *resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
    if (!resp) return NULL;

    char *err = json_extract_string(json, "error");
    if (err) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = err;
        return resp;
    }

    resp->content = json_extract_string(json, "response");
    if (!resp->content) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("Could not extract response from Ollama");
        return resp;
    }

    resp->success = 1;
    return resp;
}

/* Custom: try common fields */
static NCAIResponse *parse_custom_response(const char *json) {
    NCAIResponse *resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
    if (!resp) return NULL;

    /* Try several common field names */
    resp->content = json_extract_string(json, "content");
    if (!resp->content) resp->content = json_extract_string(json, "text");
    if (!resp->content) resp->content = json_extract_string(json, "response");
    if (!resp->content) resp->content = json_extract_string(json, "output");
    if (!resp->content) resp->content = json_extract_string(json, "result");

    if (!resp->content) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("Could not extract response from custom endpoint");
        return resp;
    }

    resp->success = 1;
    return resp;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Provider config helpers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static NCAIProviderConfig config_dup(NCAIProviderConfig *src) {
    NCAIProviderConfig c;
    memset(&c, 0, sizeof(c));
    c.type        = src->type;
    c.name        = brg_strdup(src->name);
    c.base_url    = brg_strdup(src->base_url);
    c.api_key     = brg_strdup(src->api_key);
    c.model_name  = brg_strdup(src->model_name);
    c.temperature = src->temperature;
    c.max_tokens  = src->max_tokens;
    c.timeout_ms  = src->timeout_ms;
    return c;
}

static void config_free_fields(NCAIProviderConfig *c) {
    free(c->name);
    free(c->base_url);
    free(c->api_key);
    free(c->model_name);
    c->name = c->base_url = c->api_key = c->model_name = NULL;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Bridge lifecycle
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCAIBridge *nc_ai_bridge_create(void) {
    NCAIBridge *b = (NCAIBridge *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIBridge));
    if (!b) return NULL;
    b->providers = (NCAIProviderConfig *)calloc(NC_AI_MAX_PROVIDERS,
                                                sizeof(NCAIProviderConfig));
    if (!b->providers) {
        free(b);
        return NULL;
    }
    b->n_providers     = 0;
    b->active_provider = -1;
    b->local_model     = NULL;
    b->local_tokenizer = NULL;
    b->local_loaded    = 0;
    return b;
}

void nc_ai_bridge_free(NCAIBridge *bridge) {
    if (!bridge) return;
    for (int i = 0; i < bridge->n_providers; i++) {
        config_free_fields(&bridge->providers[i]);
    }
    free(bridge->providers);
    /* Free local model if loaded — we only set local_loaded flag,
     * actual freeing depends on whether symbols are available.
     * For safety, we just NULL out the pointers. The caller
     * should ensure proper cleanup if using local model. */
    bridge->local_model     = NULL;
    bridge->local_tokenizer = NULL;
    free(bridge);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Provider management
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_ai_bridge_add_provider(NCAIBridge *bridge, NCAIProviderConfig *config) {
    if (!bridge || !config) return -1;
    if (bridge->n_providers >= NC_AI_MAX_PROVIDERS) return -1;

    int idx = bridge->n_providers;
    bridge->providers[idx] = config_dup(config);
    bridge->n_providers++;

    /* Auto-activate first provider */
    if (bridge->active_provider < 0) {
        bridge->active_provider = idx;
    }

    return idx;
}

int nc_ai_bridge_set_active(NCAIBridge *bridge, int index) {
    if (!bridge) return -1;
    if (index < 0 || index >= bridge->n_providers) return -1;
    bridge->active_provider = index;
    return 0;
}

int nc_ai_bridge_set_active_by_name(NCAIBridge *bridge, const char *name) {
    if (!bridge || !name) return -1;
    for (int i = 0; i < bridge->n_providers; i++) {
        if (bridge->providers[i].name &&
            strcasecmp(bridge->providers[i].name, name) == 0) {
            bridge->active_provider = i;
            return 0;
        }
    }
    return -1;
}

NCAIProviderConfig *nc_ai_bridge_get_active(NCAIBridge *bridge) {
    if (!bridge || bridge->active_provider < 0 ||
        bridge->active_provider >= bridge->n_providers) {
        return NULL;
    }
    return &bridge->providers[bridge->active_provider];
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Auto-detect providers from environment
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_ai_bridge_auto_detect(NCAIBridge *bridge) {
    if (!bridge) return -1;
    int found = 0;

    /* --- Check OPENAI_API_KEY --- */
    const char *openai_key = getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY");
    if (openai_key && strlen(openai_key) > 0) {
        NCAIProviderConfig cfg;
        memset(&cfg, 0, sizeof(cfg));
        cfg.type        = NC_AI_OPENAI;
        cfg.name        = "openai";
        cfg.base_url    = "https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions";
        cfg.api_key     = (char *)openai_key;
        cfg.model_name  = "gpt-4";
        cfg.temperature = 0.7f;
        cfg.max_tokens  = NC_BRG_MAX_TOKENS;
        cfg.timeout_ms  = 60000;
        nc_ai_bridge_add_provider(bridge, &cfg);
        found++;
    }

    /* --- Check ANTHROPIC_API_KEY --- */
    const char *anthropic_key = getenv("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY");
    if (anthropic_key && strlen(anthropic_key) > 0) {
        NCAIProviderConfig cfg;
        memset(&cfg, 0, sizeof(cfg));
        cfg.type        = NC_AI_ANTHROPIC;
        cfg.name        = "anthropic";
        cfg.base_url    = "https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages";
        cfg.api_key     = (char *)anthropic_key;
        cfg.model_name  = "claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022";
        cfg.temperature = 0.7f;
        cfg.max_tokens  = NC_BRG_MAX_TOKENS;
        cfg.timeout_ms  = 60000;
        nc_ai_bridge_add_provider(bridge, &cfg);
        found++;
    }

    /* --- Check Ollama on localhost:11434 --- */
    if (http_check("http://localhost:11434/api/tags", 2000)) {
        NCAIProviderConfig cfg;
        memset(&cfg, 0, sizeof(cfg));
        cfg.type        = NC_AI_OLLAMA;
        cfg.name        = "ollama";
        cfg.base_url    = "http://localhost:11434/api/generate";
        cfg.api_key     = NULL;
        cfg.model_name  = "llama3";
        cfg.temperature = 0.7f;
        cfg.max_tokens  = NC_BRG_MAX_TOKENS;
        cfg.timeout_ms  = 120000;
        nc_ai_bridge_add_provider(bridge, &cfg);
        found++;
    }

    /* --- Check for local NC model --- */
    {
        const char *home = getenv("HOME");
        if (home) {
            char model_path[1024], tok_path[1024];
            snprintf(model_path, sizeof(model_path),
                     "%s/.nc-ai/model/nc_model.bin", home);
            snprintf(tok_path, sizeof(tok_path),
                     "%s/.nc-ai/model/nc_tokenizer.bin", home);

            struct stat st;
            if (stat(model_path, &st) == 0) {
                NCAIProviderConfig cfg;
                memset(&cfg, 0, sizeof(cfg));
                cfg.type        = NC_AI_LOCAL;
                cfg.name        = "local";
                cfg.base_url    = NULL;
                cfg.api_key     = NULL;
                cfg.model_name  = "nc-model";
                cfg.temperature = 0.7f;
                cfg.max_tokens  = 1024;
                cfg.timeout_ms  = 30000;
                nc_ai_bridge_add_provider(bridge, &cfg);
                found++;
            }
        }
    }

    /* --- Always add LOCAL as fallback even if model file not found --- */
    {
        int has_local = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < bridge->n_providers; i++) {
            if (bridge->providers[i].type == NC_AI_LOCAL) {
                has_local = 1;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!has_local) {
            NCAIProviderConfig cfg;
            memset(&cfg, 0, sizeof(cfg));
            cfg.type        = NC_AI_LOCAL;
            cfg.name        = "local";
            cfg.base_url    = NULL;
            cfg.api_key     = NULL;
            cfg.model_name  = "nc-model";
            cfg.temperature = 0.7f;
            cfg.max_tokens  = 1024;
            cfg.timeout_ms  = 30000;
            nc_ai_bridge_add_provider(bridge, &cfg);
            found++;
        }
    }

    return found;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Local model integration
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_ai_bridge_load_local(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                            const char *model_path,
                            const char *tokenizer_path) {
    if (!bridge || !model_path || !tokenizer_path) return -1;

    /* Check files exist */
    struct stat st;
    if (stat(model_path, &st) != 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Local model not found: %s\n", model_path);
        return -1;
    }
    if (stat(tokenizer_path, &st) != 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Tokenizer not found: %s\n", tokenizer_path);
        return -1;
    }

    /*
     * Load via the nc_model / nc_tokenizer APIs.
     * These are linked at compile time. If linking without nc_model.c,
     * this function will simply not be callable (linker error), which
     * is the intended behavior — the bridge still works via HTTP providers.
     *
     * We use the public API names that match nc_model.h / nc_tokenizer.h.
     */
    bridge->local_model = nc_model_load(model_path);
    if (!bridge->local_model) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Failed to load model: %s\n", model_path);
        return -1;
    }

    bridge->local_tokenizer = _nc_tok_load(tokenizer_path);
    if (!bridge->local_tokenizer) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Failed to load tokenizer: %s\n",
                tokenizer_path);
        nc_model_free(bridge->local_model);
        bridge->local_model = NULL;
        return -1;
    }

    bridge->local_loaded = 1;
    return 0;
}

/* Run inference on local model */
static NCAIResponse *run_local_inference(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                                         const char *prompt) {
    NCAIResponse *resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
    if (!resp) return NULL;

    if (!bridge->local_loaded || !bridge->local_model ||
        !bridge->local_tokenizer) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup(
            "Local model not loaded. Use nc_ai_bridge_load_local() first, "
            "or switch to an API provider.");
        return resp;
    }

    /* Encode prompt */
    int tokens[512];
    int n_tokens = _nc_tok_encode(bridge->local_tokenizer,
                                            prompt, tokens, 512);
    if (n_tokens <= 0) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("Failed to tokenize prompt");
        return resp;
    }

    /* Generate */
    int output[1024];
    NCAIProviderConfig *cfg = nc_ai_bridge_get_active(bridge);
    int max_tok = (cfg && cfg->max_tokens > 0) ? cfg->max_tokens : 512;
    float temp  = (cfg && cfg->temperature > 0) ? cfg->temperature : 0.7f;
    if (max_tok > 1024) max_tok = 1024;

    int out_len = nc_model_generate(bridge->local_model, tokens,
                                    n_tokens, max_tok, temp, output);
    if (out_len <= 0) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("Model generation produced no output");
        return resp;
    }

    /* Decode */
    char text[8192];
    int decoded = _nc_tok_decode(bridge->local_tokenizer,
                                           output, out_len, text, 8192);
    if (decoded <= 0) {
        resp->success = 0;
        resp->error = brg_strdup("Failed to decode model output");
        return resp;
    }

    resp->content = brg_strdup(text);
    resp->tokens_used = out_len;
    resp->success = 1;
    return resp;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Core API — ask with system prompt
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_ask_with_system(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                                            const char *system,
                                            const char *prompt) {
    if (!bridge || !prompt) {
        NCAIResponse *resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
        if (resp) {
            resp->success = 0;
            resp->error = brg_strdup("Invalid arguments to nc_ai_bridge_ask");
        }
        return resp;
    }

    NCAIProviderConfig *cfg = nc_ai_bridge_get_active(bridge);
    if (!cfg) {
        NCAIResponse *resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
        if (resp) {
            resp->success = 0;
            resp->error = brg_strdup("No active provider configured");
        }
        return resp;
    }

    /* Measure latency */
    struct timespec ts_start, ts_end;
    clock_gettime(CLOCK_MONOTONIC, &ts_start);

    NCAIResponse *resp = NULL;

    switch (cfg->type) {
    case NC_AI_LOCAL:
        /* Local model — combine system + prompt */
        if (system) {
            size_t combined_len = strlen(system) + strlen(prompt) + 32;
            char *combined = (char *)malloc(combined_len);
            if (combined) {
                snprintf(combined, combined_len, "%s\n\n%s", system, prompt);
                resp = run_local_inference(bridge, combined);
                free(combined);
            }
        } else {
            resp = run_local_inference(bridge, prompt);
        }
        break;

    case NC_AI_OPENAI: {
        char *body = format_openai_request(prompt, system, cfg);
        const char *headers[3];
        char auth_hdr[512];
        snprintf(auth_hdr, sizeof(auth_hdr), "Authorization: Bearer %s",
                 cfg->api_key ? cfg->api_key : "");
        headers[0] = "Content-Type: application/json";
        headers[1] = auth_hdr;
        int n_hdrs = 2;

        char *json = http_post(cfg->base_url, headers, n_hdrs, body,
                               cfg->timeout_ms);
        free(body);

        if (!json) {
            resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
            if (resp) {
                resp->success = 0;
                resp->error = brg_strdup("HTTP request to OpenAI failed");
            }
        } else {
            resp = parse_openai_response(json);
            free(json);
        }
        break;
    }

    case NC_AI_ANTHROPIC: {
        char *body = format_anthropic_request(prompt, system, cfg);
        const char *headers[4];
        char auth_hdr[512];
        snprintf(auth_hdr, sizeof(auth_hdr), "x-api-key: %s",
                 cfg->api_key ? cfg->api_key : "");
        headers[0] = "Content-Type: application/json";
        headers[1] = auth_hdr;
        headers[2] = "anthropic-version: 2023-06-01";
        int n_hdrs = 3;

        char *json = http_post(cfg->base_url, headers, n_hdrs, body,
                               cfg->timeout_ms);
        free(body);

        if (!json) {
            resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
            if (resp) {
                resp->success = 0;
                resp->error = brg_strdup("HTTP request to Anthropic failed");
            }
        } else {
            resp = parse_anthropic_response(json);
            free(json);
        }
        break;
    }

    case NC_AI_OLLAMA: {
        char *body = format_ollama_request(prompt, system, cfg);
        const char *headers[1];
        headers[0] = "Content-Type: application/json";

        char *json = http_post(cfg->base_url, headers, 1, body,
                               cfg->timeout_ms);
        free(body);

        if (!json) {
            resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
            if (resp) {
                resp->success = 0;
                resp->error = brg_strdup("HTTP request to Ollama failed");
            }
        } else {
            resp = parse_ollama_response(json);
            free(json);
        }
        break;
    }

    case NC_AI_CUSTOM: {
        char *body = format_custom_request(prompt, system, cfg);
        const char *headers[3];
        int n_hdrs = 1;
        char auth_hdr[512];
        headers[0] = "Content-Type: application/json";
        if (cfg->api_key && strlen(cfg->api_key) > 0) {
            snprintf(auth_hdr, sizeof(auth_hdr), "Authorization: Bearer %s",
                     cfg->api_key);
            headers[1] = auth_hdr;
            n_hdrs = 2;
        }

        char *json = http_post(cfg->base_url, headers, n_hdrs, body,
                               cfg->timeout_ms);
        free(body);

        if (!json) {
            resp = (NCAIResponse *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCAIResponse));
            if (resp) {
                resp->success = 0;
                resp->error = brg_strdup("HTTP request to custom endpoint failed");
            }
        } else {
            resp = parse_custom_response(json);
            free(json);
        }
        break;
    }
    }

    /* Record latency */
    if (resp) {
        clock_gettime(CLOCK_MONOTONIC, &ts_end);
        double elapsed = (double)(ts_end.tv_sec - ts_start.tv_sec) * 1000.0 +
                         (double)(ts_end.tv_nsec - ts_start.tv_nsec) / 1e6;
        resp->latency_ms = (float)elapsed;
    }

    return resp;
}

/* ── Simple ask (no system prompt) ─────────────────────── */

NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_ask(NCAIBridge *bridge, const char *prompt) {
    return nc_ai_bridge_ask_with_system(bridge, NULL, prompt);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  NC-specific generation helpers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static const char *NC_CODE_SYSTEM_PROMPT =
    "You are an expert NC programming language code generator. "
    "NC is a modern systems language with built-in web services, AI, and UI.\n\n"
    "NC syntax rules:\n"
    "- Services: `service MyService { port 8080; route GET /path -> handler; }`\n"
    "- Functions: `fn name(param: type) -> type { ... }`\n"
    "- Variables: `let x = 10;` or `let mut x = 10;`\n"
    "- Types: int, float, str, bool, list<T>, map<K,V>\n"
    "- Middleware: `use auth(); use cors(); use rateLimit(100);`\n"
    "- Database: `model User { id: int @primary; name: str; email: str @unique; }`\n"
    "- AI integration: `use ai(provider: \"local\"); let resp = ai.ask(prompt);`\n"
    "- Error handling: `try { ... } catch(e) { ... }`\n"
    "- Modules: `import std.http; import std.json;`\n\n"
    "Output ONLY valid NC code. No explanations unless commented.";

static const char *NC_UI_SYSTEM_PROMPT =
    "You are an expert NC UI (NCUI) code generator. "
    "NCUI is a declarative UI language for building web interfaces.\n\n"
    "NCUI syntax rules:\n"
    "- Pages: `page Home { ... }`\n"
    "- Layout: `row { ... }` `col { ... }` `grid(cols: 3) { ... }`\n"
    "- Components: `text(\"Hello\")` `button(\"Click\", onClick: handler)`\n"
    "- Input: `input(type: \"text\", bind: variable)` `select(options: list)`\n"
    "- Navigation: `nav { link(\"/home\", \"Home\"); link(\"/about\", \"About\"); }`\n"
    "- Styling: `style { color: \"#fff\"; bg: \"#1a1a2e\"; padding: 20; radius: 8; }`\n"
    "- State: `state count = 0;` `state items: list<str> = [];`\n"
    "- Events: `onClick: { count += 1; }` `onSubmit: { api.post(\"/data\", form); }`\n"
    "- Theme: `theme { primary: \"#e94560\"; bg: \"#0f3460\"; font: \"Inter\"; }`\n"
    "- Conditional: `if logged_in { dashboard() } else { loginForm() }`\n"
    "- Loop: `for item in items { card(item) }`\n\n"
    "Output ONLY valid NCUI code. No explanations unless commented.";

NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_generate_nc(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                                        const char *description) {
    if (!bridge || !description) return NULL;

    /* Build a focused prompt */
    NCBrgBuf prompt = brg_buf_new();
    brg_buf_printf(&prompt,
        "Generate NC code for the following:\n\n%s\n\n"
        "Requirements:\n"
        "- Complete, runnable NC code\n"
        "- Include all necessary imports\n"
        "- Add helpful comments\n"
        "- Follow NC best practices",
        description);

    NCAIResponse *resp = nc_ai_bridge_ask_with_system(bridge,
                                                       NC_CODE_SYSTEM_PROMPT,
                                                       prompt.data);
    brg_buf_free(&prompt);
    return resp;
}

NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_generate_ncui(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                                          const char *description) {
    if (!bridge || !description) return NULL;

    NCBrgBuf prompt = brg_buf_new();
    brg_buf_printf(&prompt,
        "Generate an NC UI page for the following:\n\n%s\n\n"
        "Requirements:\n"
        "- Complete NCUI page definition\n"
        "- Include theme and styling\n"
        "- Add responsive layout\n"
        "- Include state management where needed\n"
        "- Add event handlers for interactivity",
        description);

    NCAIResponse *resp = nc_ai_bridge_ask_with_system(bridge,
                                                       NC_UI_SYSTEM_PROMPT,
                                                       prompt.data);
    brg_buf_free(&prompt);
    return resp;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Response cleanup
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_ai_response_free(NCAIResponse *resp) {
    if (!resp) return;
    free(resp->content);
    free(resp->error);
    free(resp);
}


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_bridge.h

/*
 * nc_ai_bridge.h — Provider-agnostic LLM connector for NC AI.
 *
 * Connects NC AI to any external LLM (OpenAI, Anthropic, Ollama,
 * custom HTTP endpoints) or runs standalone with NC's own model.
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 * HTTP calls use popen + system curl (no libcurl).
 */

#ifndef NC_AI_BRIDGE_H
#define NC_AI_BRIDGE_H

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdbool.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Provider types
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef enum {
    NC_AI_LOCAL,        /* NC's own model (default, no internet needed) */
    NC_AI_OPENAI,       /* OpenAI API compatible                        */
    NC_AI_ANTHROPIC,    /* Anthropic API compatible                     */
    NC_AI_OLLAMA,       /* Ollama local server                          */
    NC_AI_CUSTOM,       /* Any custom HTTP endpoint                     */
} NCAIProvider;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Provider configuration
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    NCAIProvider type;
    char *name;           /* Provider name for display                   */
    char *base_url;       /* API endpoint (NULL for local)               */
    char *api_key;        /* API key (NULL for local/ollama)             */
    char *model_name;     /* Model name ("gpt-4", "claude-3", "llama3") */
    float temperature;
    int max_tokens;
    int timeout_ms;       /* Request timeout                             */
} NCAIProviderConfig;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Response
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    char *content;        /* Response text                               */
    int tokens_used;      /* Token count                                 */
    float latency_ms;     /* Response time                               */
    int success;          /* 1 = success, 0 = error                      */
    char *error;          /* Error message if failed                     */
} NCAIResponse;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Bridge — manages multiple providers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

#define NC_AI_MAX_PROVIDERS 16

typedef struct {
    NCAIProviderConfig *providers;
    int n_providers;
    int active_provider;   /* Index of current provider */
    /* Local model (loaded on demand) */
    void *local_model;     /* NCModel* when loaded      */
    void *local_tokenizer; /* NCTokenizer* when loaded  */
    int local_loaded;
} NCAIBridge;

/* ── Lifecycle ─────────────────────────────────────────── */

NCAIBridge *nc_ai_bridge_create(void);
void        nc_ai_bridge_free(NCAIBridge *bridge);

/* ── Provider management ───────────────────────────────── */

int  nc_ai_bridge_add_provider(NCAIBridge *bridge, NCAIProviderConfig *config);
int  nc_ai_bridge_set_active(NCAIBridge *bridge, int index);
int  nc_ai_bridge_set_active_by_name(NCAIBridge *bridge, const char *name);
NCAIProviderConfig *nc_ai_bridge_get_active(NCAIBridge *bridge);

/* Auto-detect providers from environment variables */
int  nc_ai_bridge_auto_detect(NCAIBridge *bridge);

/* ── Core API ──────────────────────────────────────────── */

NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_ask(NCAIBridge *bridge, const char *prompt);
NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_ask_with_system(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                                            const char *system,
                                            const char *prompt);
NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_generate_nc(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                                        const char *description);
NCAIResponse *nc_ai_bridge_generate_ncui(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                                          const char *description);
void          nc_ai_response_free(NCAIResponse *resp);

/* ── Local model ───────────────────────────────────────── */

int nc_ai_bridge_load_local(NCAIBridge *bridge,
                            const char *model_path,
                            const char *tokenizer_path);

#endif /* NC_AI_BRIDGE_H */


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_doc.c

/*
 * nc_ai_doc.c — Document-driven NC project generation.
 *
 * Parses natural language documents to extract project specifications,
 * then generates a complete NC project with backend, models, UI pages,
 * tests, and configuration files.
 *
 * Works in two modes:
 *   1. Template mode (always available) — rule-based generation
 *   2. AI-enhanced mode — uses LLM bridge for richer output
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 */

#include "nc_ai_doc.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>
#include <stdarg.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <errno.h>
#include <time.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Internal constants
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

#define NC_DOC_BUF_INIT  8192
#define NC_DOC_BUF_MAX   (2 << 20)   /* 2 MiB */
#define NC_DOC_LINE_MAX  4096

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Dynamic string buffer
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    char  *data;
    size_t len;
    size_t cap;
} NCDocBuf;

static NCDocBuf doc_buf_new(void) {
    NCDocBuf b;
    b.cap  = NC_DOC_BUF_INIT;
    b.len  = 0;
    b.data = (char *)malloc(b.cap);
    if (b.data) b.data[0] = '\0';
    return b;
}

static void doc_buf_free(NCDocBuf *b) {
    free(b->data);
    b->data = NULL;
    b->len  = 0;
    b->cap  = 0;
}

static void doc_buf_grow(NCDocBuf *b, size_t need) {
    if (b->len + need + 1 <= b->cap) return;
    size_t new_cap = b->cap * 2;
    while (new_cap < b->len + need + 1) new_cap *= 2;
    if (new_cap > NC_DOC_BUF_MAX) new_cap = NC_DOC_BUF_MAX;
    char *tmp = (char *)realloc(b->data, new_cap);
    if (!tmp) return;
    b->data = tmp;
    b->cap  = new_cap;
}

static void doc_buf_append(NCDocBuf *b, const char *s) {
    size_t slen = strlen(s);
    doc_buf_grow(b, slen);
    if (b->len + slen + 1 > b->cap) return;
    memcpy(b->data + b->len, s, slen);
    b->len += slen;
    b->data[b->len] = '\0';
}

static void doc_buf_printf(NCDocBuf *b, const char *fmt, ...) {
    va_list ap;
    va_start(ap, fmt);
    char tmp[NC_DOC_LINE_MAX];
    int n = vsnprintf(tmp, sizeof(tmp), fmt, ap);
    va_end(ap);
    if (n > 0) {
        doc_buf_grow(b, (size_t)n);
        if (b->len + (size_t)n + 1 <= b->cap) {
            memcpy(b->data + b->len, tmp, (size_t)n);
            b->len += (size_t)n;
            b->data[b->len] = '\0';
        }
    }
}

/* Return owned copy of buffer contents, then reset buffer */
static char *doc_buf_detach(NCDocBuf *b) {
    char *s = b->data;
    b->data = NULL;
    b->len  = 0;
    b->cap  = 0;
    return s;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  String utilities
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *doc_strdup(const char *s) {
    if (!s) return NULL;
    size_t len = strlen(s);
    char *out = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
    if (out) memcpy(out, s, len + 1);
    return out;
}

/* Case-insensitive substring search */
static const char *doc_strcasestr(const char *haystack, const char *needle) {
    if (!haystack || !needle) return NULL;
    size_t nlen = strlen(needle);
    if (nlen == 0) return haystack;
    size_t hlen = strlen(haystack);
    if (nlen > hlen) return NULL;
    for (size_t i = 0; i <= hlen - nlen; i++) {
        int match = 1;
        for (size_t j = 0; j < nlen; j++) {
            if (tolower((unsigned char)haystack[i + j]) !=
                tolower((unsigned char)needle[j])) {
                match = 0;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (match) return haystack + i;
    }
    return NULL;
}

/* Check if text contains a word (case-insensitive, word boundary aware) */
static int doc_contains_word(const char *text, const char *word) {
    const char *pos = doc_strcasestr(text, word);
    if (!pos) return 0;
    /* Check word boundary before */
    if (pos > text) {
        char prev = *(pos - 1);
        if (isalnum((unsigned char)prev) || prev == '_') return 0;
    }
    /* Check word boundary after */
    size_t wlen = strlen(word);
    char after = pos[wlen];
    if (isalnum((unsigned char)after) || after == '_') return 0;
    return 1;
}

/* Convert string to lowercase (in-place) */
static void doc_tolower(char *s) {
    for (; *s; s++) *s = (char)tolower((unsigned char)*s);
}

/* Trim whitespace from both ends (in-place, returns pointer into same buffer) */
static char *doc_trim(char *s) {
    while (*s && isspace((unsigned char)*s)) s++;
    if (*s == '\0') return s;
    char *end = s + strlen(s) - 1;
    while (end > s && isspace((unsigned char)*end)) end--;
    *(end + 1) = '\0';
    return s;
}

/* Capitalize first letter */
static void doc_capitalize(char *s) {
    if (s && *s) *s = (char)toupper((unsigned char)*s);
}

/* Slugify: "My App Name" -> "my_app_name" */
static char *doc_slugify(const char *name) {
    if (!name) return doc_strdup("project");
    size_t len = strlen(name);
    char *slug = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
    if (!slug) return doc_strdup("project");
    size_t j = 0;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        char c = name[i];
        if (isalnum((unsigned char)c)) {
            slug[j++] = (char)tolower((unsigned char)c);
        } else if (c == ' ' || c == '-' || c == '.') {
            if (j > 0 && slug[j - 1] != '_') slug[j++] = '_';
        }
    }
    if (j == 0) { free(slug); return doc_strdup("project"); }
    slug[j] = '\0';
    return slug;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Spec helper — add item to string array
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int spec_add_item(char ***arr, int *count, const char *item) {
    if (*count >= NC_DOC_MAX_ITEMS) return -1;
    /* Avoid duplicates */
    for (int i = 0; i < *count; i++) {
        if (strcasecmp((*arr)[i], item) == 0) return 0;
    }
    if (*count == 0) {
        *arr = (char **)malloc(NC_DOC_MAX_ITEMS * sizeof(char *));
        if (!*arr) return -1;
    }
    (*arr)[*count] = doc_strdup(item);
    (*count)++;
    return 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Document Parser
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* Extract project name from document */
static char *extract_project_name(const char *text) {
    const char *p = text;

    /* Try markdown heading: # Title */
    while (*p && isspace((unsigned char)*p)) p++;
    if (*p == '#') {
        p++;
        while (*p == '#') p++;
        while (*p == ' ') p++;
        const char *end = p;
        while (*end && *end != '\n') end++;
        size_t len = (size_t)(end - p);
        if (len > 0 && len < 256) {
            char *name = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
            memcpy(name, p, len);
            name[len] = '\0';
            return name;
        }
    }

    /* Try "Project: Name" or "Name: ..." or "Title: ..." */
    const char *prefixes[] = { "project:", "title:", "app:", "name:", NULL };
    for (int i = 0; prefixes[i]; i++) {
        const char *found = doc_strcasestr(text, prefixes[i]);
        if (found) {
            found += strlen(prefixes[i]);
            while (*found == ' ') found++;
            const char *end = found;
            while (*end && *end != '\n' && *end != '.' && *end != ',')
                end++;
            size_t len = (size_t)(end - found);
            if (len > 0 && len < 256) {
                char *name = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
                memcpy(name, found, len);
                name[len] = '\0';
                return doc_trim(name);
            }
        }
    }

    /* Fall back to first sentence or line */
    p = text;
    while (*p && isspace((unsigned char)*p)) p++;
    const char *end = p;
    while (*end && *end != '\n' && *end != '.') end++;
    size_t len = (size_t)(end - p);
    if (len > 60) len = 60; /* Truncate long first lines */
    if (len > 0) {
        char *name = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
        memcpy(name, p, len);
        name[len] = '\0';
        return doc_trim(name);
    }

    return doc_strdup("MyProject");
}

/* Detect features from keywords in text */
static void detect_features(const char *text, NCDocSpec *spec) {
    struct { const char *keyword; const char *feature; } feature_map[] = {
        { "auth",          "authentication" },
        { "login",         "authentication" },
        { "signup",        "authentication" },
        { "sign up",       "authentication" },
        { "register",      "authentication" },
        { "password",      "authentication" },
        { "oauth",         "authentication" },
        { "jwt",           "authentication" },
        { "database",      "database" },
        { "storage",       "database" },
        { "persist",       "database" },
        { "store data",    "database" },
        { "sql",           "database" },
        { "crud",          "database" },
        { "ai",            "ai_integration" },
        { "chat",          "ai_integration" },
        { "chatbot",       "ai_integration" },
        { "llm",           "ai_integration" },
        { "machine learning", "ai_integration" },
        { "neural",        "ai_integration" },
        { "intelligent",   "ai_integration" },
        { "search",        "search" },
        { "filter",        "search" },
        { "find",          "search" },
        { "query",         "search" },
        { "upload",        "file_upload" },
        { "file",          "file_upload" },
        { "image",         "file_upload" },
        { "attachment",    "file_upload" },
        { "notification",  "notifications" },
        { "alert",         "notifications" },
        { "email",         "notifications" },
        { "push",          "notifications" },
        { "payment",       "payments" },
        { "stripe",        "payments" },
        { "billing",       "payments" },
        { "checkout",      "payments" },
        { "subscription",  "payments" },
        { "admin",         "admin_panel" },
        { "dashboard",     "admin_panel" },
        { "manage",        "admin_panel" },
        { "analytics",     "analytics" },
        { "metrics",       "analytics" },
        { "tracking",      "analytics" },
        { "statistics",    "analytics" },
        { "realtime",      "realtime" },
        { "real-time",     "realtime" },
        { "websocket",     "realtime" },
        { "live",          "realtime" },
        { "api",           "rest_api" },
        { "rest",          "rest_api" },
        { "endpoint",      "rest_api" },
        { NULL, NULL }
    };

    for (int i = 0; feature_map[i].keyword; i++) {
        if (doc_strcasestr(text, feature_map[i].keyword)) {
            spec_add_item(&spec->features, &spec->n_features,
                          feature_map[i].feature);
        }
    }

    /* Set convenience flags */
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_features; i++) {
        if (strcmp(spec->features[i], "authentication") == 0)
            spec->needs_auth = 1;
        if (strcmp(spec->features[i], "ai_integration") == 0)
            spec->needs_ai = 1;
        if (strcmp(spec->features[i], "database") == 0)
            spec->needs_database = 1;
    }
}

/* Detect API endpoints */
static void detect_endpoints(const char *text, NCDocSpec *spec) {
    /* Pattern 1: HTTP methods — GET /path, POST /path, etc. */
    const char *methods[] = { "GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE", "PATCH", NULL };
    for (int m = 0; methods[m]; m++) {
        const char *pos = text;
        while ((pos = doc_strcasestr(pos, methods[m])) != NULL) {
            const char *after = pos + strlen(methods[m]);
            /* Must be followed by space then / */
            if (*after == ' ' && *(after + 1) == '/') {
                after++; /* skip space */
                const char *end = after;
                while (*end && !isspace((unsigned char)*end) &&
                       *end != ',' && *end != ';' && *end != ')' &&
                       *end != ']')
                    end++;
                size_t path_len = (size_t)(end - after);
                if (path_len > 0 && path_len < 256) {
                    char ep[300];
                    snprintf(ep, sizeof(ep), "%s %.*s",
                             methods[m], (int)path_len, after);
                    spec_add_item(&spec->endpoints, &spec->n_endpoints, ep);
                }
            }
            pos = after;
        }
    }

    /* Pattern 2: "endpoint for X", "API to Y" */
    const char *patterns[] = {
        "endpoint for ", "api for ", "api to ", "route for ",
        "endpoint to ", NULL
    };
    for (int i = 0; patterns[i]; i++) {
        const char *pos = text;
        while ((pos = doc_strcasestr(pos, patterns[i])) != NULL) {
            pos += strlen(patterns[i]);
            const char *end = pos;
            while (*end && *end != '\n' && *end != '.' &&
                   *end != ',' && *end != ';')
                end++;
            size_t len = (size_t)(end - pos);
            if (len > 0 && len < 256) {
                char ep[300];
                snprintf(ep, sizeof(ep), "%.*s", (int)len, pos);
                char *trimmed = doc_trim(ep);
                if (strlen(trimmed) > 0) {
                    /* Convert natural language to endpoint */
                    char *slug = doc_slugify(trimmed);
                    char route[300];
                    snprintf(route, sizeof(route), "POST /api/%s", slug);
                    spec_add_item(&spec->endpoints, &spec->n_endpoints, route);
                    free(slug);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    /* Ensure at least basic CRUD endpoints if we have models but no endpoints */
    if (spec->n_endpoints == 0 && spec->n_models > 0) {
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_models; i++) {
            char *lower = doc_strdup(spec->models[i]);
            doc_tolower(lower);
            char ep[128];
            snprintf(ep, sizeof(ep), "GET /api/%ss", lower);
            spec_add_item(&spec->endpoints, &spec->n_endpoints, ep);
            snprintf(ep, sizeof(ep), "POST /api/%ss", lower);
            spec_add_item(&spec->endpoints, &spec->n_endpoints, ep);
            snprintf(ep, sizeof(ep), "GET /api/%ss/:id", lower);
            spec_add_item(&spec->endpoints, &spec->n_endpoints, ep);
            snprintf(ep, sizeof(ep), "PUT /api/%ss/:id", lower);
            spec_add_item(&spec->endpoints, &spec->n_endpoints, ep);
            snprintf(ep, sizeof(ep), "DELETE /api/%ss/:id", lower);
            spec_add_item(&spec->endpoints, &spec->n_endpoints, ep);
            free(lower);
        }
    }
}

/* Detect UI pages */
static void detect_pages(const char *text, NCDocSpec *spec) {
    struct { const char *pattern; const char *page; } page_map[] = {
        { "home page",       "home" },
        { "homepage",        "home" },
        { "landing page",    "landing" },
        { "landing",         "landing" },
        { "dashboard",       "dashboard" },
        { "admin page",      "admin" },
        { "admin panel",     "admin" },
        { "settings page",   "settings" },
        { "settings",        "settings" },
        { "profile page",    "profile" },
        { "profile",         "profile" },
        { "login page",      "login" },
        { "login",           "login" },
        { "signup page",     "signup" },
        { "register page",   "signup" },
        { "about page",      "about" },
        { "about",           "about" },
        { "contact page",    "contact" },
        { "contact",         "contact" },
        { "blog page",       "blog" },
        { "blog",            "blog" },
        { "search page",     "search" },
        { "detail page",     "detail" },
        { "list page",       "list" },
        { "checkout page",   "checkout" },
        { "cart page",       "cart" },
        { "pricing page",    "pricing" },
        { "pricing",         "pricing" },
        { NULL, NULL }
    };

    for (int i = 0; page_map[i].pattern; i++) {
        if (doc_strcasestr(text, page_map[i].pattern)) {
            spec_add_item(&spec->pages, &spec->n_pages, page_map[i].page);
        }
    }

    /* Ensure at least a home page */
    if (spec->n_pages == 0) {
        spec_add_item(&spec->pages, &spec->n_pages, "home");
    }

    /* Add login page if auth needed */
    if (spec->needs_auth) {
        spec_add_item(&spec->pages, &spec->n_pages, "login");
        spec_add_item(&spec->pages, &spec->n_pages, "signup");
    }
}

/* Detect data models */
static void detect_models(const char *text, NCDocSpec *spec) {
    /* Common model names */
    const char *common_models[] = {
        "User", "Post", "Product", "Order", "Comment", "Category",
        "Tag", "Article", "Message", "Notification", "Payment",
        "Invoice", "Task", "Project", "Team", "Role", "Permission",
        "File", "Image", "Session", "Token", "Log", "Event",
        "Review", "Rating", "Address", "Cart", "Item", "Subscription",
        NULL
    };

    for (int i = 0; common_models[i]; i++) {
        /* Check for the model name as a word */
        if (doc_contains_word(text, common_models[i])) {
            spec_add_item(&spec->models, &spec->n_models, common_models[i]);
        }
    }

    /* Pattern: "X table", "X model", "X entity" */
    const char *suffixes[] = { " table", " model", " entity", " schema", NULL };
    for (int s = 0; suffixes[s]; s++) {
        const char *pos = text;
        while ((pos = doc_strcasestr(pos, suffixes[s])) != NULL) {
            /* Walk backward to find the start of the word */
            const char *word_end = pos;
            const char *word_start = pos - 1;
            while (word_start >= text && isalpha((unsigned char)*word_start))
                word_start--;
            word_start++;
            size_t wlen = (size_t)(word_end - word_start);
            if (wlen > 1 && wlen < 64) {
                char model[65];
                memcpy(model, word_start, wlen);
                model[wlen] = '\0';
                doc_capitalize(model);
                spec_add_item(&spec->models, &spec->n_models, model);
            }
            pos = word_end + strlen(suffixes[s]);
        }
    }

    /* Always have at least User model if auth is needed */
    if (spec->needs_auth && spec->n_models == 0) {
        spec_add_item(&spec->models, &spec->n_models, "User");
    }
}

/* Detect theme */
static char *detect_theme(const char *text) {
    if (doc_strcasestr(text, "dark theme") || doc_strcasestr(text, "dark mode"))
        return doc_strdup("dark");
    if (doc_strcasestr(text, "light theme") || doc_strcasestr(text, "light mode"))
        return doc_strdup("light");

    /* Check for specific color mentions */
    const char *colors[] = {
        "blue", "red", "green", "purple", "orange", "pink",
        "teal", "indigo", "cyan", NULL
    };
    for (int i = 0; colors[i]; i++) {
        if (doc_strcasestr(text, colors[i])) {
            char theme[32];
            snprintf(theme, sizeof(theme), "%s", colors[i]);
            return doc_strdup(theme);
        }
    }

    return doc_strdup("dark"); /* default */
}

/* ── Public: parse document into spec ──────────────────── */

NCDocSpec *nc_ai_doc_parse(const char *doc_text) {
    if (!doc_text || strlen(doc_text) == 0) return NULL;

    NCDocSpec *spec = (NCDocSpec *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCDocSpec));
    if (!spec) return NULL;

    spec->description = doc_strdup(doc_text);
    spec->name        = extract_project_name(doc_text);
    spec->theme       = detect_theme(doc_text);

    /* Detect in order: features first (sets flags), then models,
     * endpoints, and pages (which depend on flags) */
    detect_features(doc_text, spec);
    detect_models(doc_text, spec);
    detect_endpoints(doc_text, spec);
    detect_pages(doc_text, spec);

    /* If database not explicitly detected but we have models, set it */
    if (spec->n_models > 0 && !spec->needs_database) {
        spec->needs_database = 1;
        spec_add_item(&spec->features, &spec->n_features, "database");
    }

    return spec;
}

void nc_ai_doc_spec_free(NCDocSpec *spec) {
    if (!spec) return;
    free(spec->name);
    free(spec->description);
    free(spec->theme);
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_features;  i++) free(spec->features[i]);
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_endpoints; i++) free(spec->endpoints[i]);
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_pages;     i++) free(spec->pages[i]);
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_models;    i++) free(spec->models[i]);
    free(spec->features);
    free(spec->endpoints);
    free(spec->pages);
    free(spec->models);
    free(spec);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  File system helpers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int ensure_dir(const char *path) {
    struct stat st;
    if (stat(path, &st) == 0) return 0; /* exists */
    if (mkdir(path, 0755) != 0 && errno != EEXIST) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Failed to create directory: %s (%s)\n",
                path, strerror(errno));
        return -1;
    }
    return 0;
}

static int write_file(const char *path, const char *content) {
    FILE *fp = fopen(path, "w");
    if (!fp) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Failed to write: %s (%s)\n",
                path, strerror(errno));
        return -1;
    }
    fputs(content, fp);
    fclose(fp);
    return 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template generators
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* --- server.nc --- */
static char *gen_server_nc(NCDocSpec *spec) {
    NCDocBuf buf = doc_buf_new();
    char *slug = doc_slugify(spec->name);

    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "/*\n"
        " * %s — Main service\n"
        " * Auto-generated by NC AI Doc Generator\n"
        " */\n\n"
        "import std.http;\n"
        "import std.json;\n",
        spec->name);

    if (spec->needs_database) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "import std.db;\n");
    }
    if (spec->needs_auth) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "import std.auth;\nimport std.crypto;\n");
    }
    if (spec->needs_ai) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "import std.ai;\n");
    }

    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "\n"
        "service %s {\n"
        "    port 8080;\n\n",
        slug);

    /* Middleware */
    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "    // Middleware\n"
        "    use cors();\n"
        "    use logger();\n"
        "    use bodyParser();\n");

    if (spec->needs_auth) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    use auth(secret: env(\"JWT_SECRET\"), exclude: [\"/api/login\", \"/api/register\"]);\n");
    }

    /* Rate limiting if we have endpoints */
    if (spec->n_endpoints > 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "    use rateLimit(100);\n");
    }

    doc_buf_append(&buf, "\n");

    /* Database connection */
    if (spec->needs_database) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    // Database\n"
            "    let db = database(env(\"DATABASE_URL\") ?? \"sqlite://data.db\");\n\n");
    }

    /* AI integration */
    if (spec->needs_ai) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    // AI integration\n"
            "    use ai(provider: env(\"AI_PROVIDER\") ?? \"local\");\n\n");
    }

    /* Health check route */
    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "    // Health check\n"
        "    route GET /health -> fn(req, res) {\n"
        "        res.json({ status: \"ok\", service: \"");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, slug);
    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "\" });\n"
        "    };\n\n");

    /* Auth routes */
    if (spec->needs_auth) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    // Authentication\n"
            "    route POST /api/register -> fn(req, res) {\n"
            "        let { email, password, name } = req.body;\n"
            "        if !email || !password {\n"
            "            return res.status(400).json({ error: \"Email and password required\" });\n"
            "        }\n"
            "        let hashed = crypto.hash(password);\n"
            "        let user = db.create(\"User\", { email, password: hashed, name });\n"
            "        let token = auth.sign({ id: user.id, email: user.email });\n"
            "        res.json({ user: { id: user.id, email: user.email, name: user.name }, token });\n"
            "    };\n\n"
            "    route POST /api/login -> fn(req, res) {\n"
            "        let { email, password } = req.body;\n"
            "        let user = db.findOne(\"User\", { email });\n"
            "        if !user || !crypto.verify(password, user.password) {\n"
