            "            return res.status(401).json({ error: \"Invalid credentials\" });\n"
            "        }\n"
            "        let token = auth.sign({ id: user.id, email: user.email });\n"
            "        res.json({ user: { id: user.id, email: user.email, name: user.name }, token });\n"
            "    };\n\n");
    }

    /* Generate routes for each endpoint */
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_endpoints; i++) {
        char *ep = spec->endpoints[i];
        /* Parse "METHOD /path" */
        char method[16] = "GET";
        char path[256] = "/";
        if (sscanf(ep, "%15s %255s", method, path) >= 1) {
            /* Skip auth endpoints (already generated) */
            if (spec->needs_auth &&
                (strstr(path, "/login") || strstr(path, "/register")))
                continue;

            doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                "    route %s %s -> fn(req, res) {\n", method, path);

            if (strcmp(method, "GET") == 0) {
                /* Check if it's a single-item route (has :id) */
                if (strstr(path, ":id")) {
                    doc_buf_append(&buf,
                        "        let item = db.findById(req.params.id);\n"
                        "        if !item {\n"
                        "            return res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" });\n"
                        "        }\n"
                        "        res.json(item);\n");
                } else {
                    doc_buf_append(&buf,
                        "        let items = db.findAll(req.query);\n"
                        "        res.json(items);\n");
                }
            } else if (strcmp(method, "POST") == 0) {
                doc_buf_append(&buf,
                    "        let item = db.create(req.body);\n"
                    "        res.status(201).json(item);\n");
            } else if (strcmp(method, "PUT") == 0) {
                doc_buf_append(&buf,
                    "        let item = db.update(req.params.id, req.body);\n"
                    "        if !item {\n"
                    "            return res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" });\n"
                    "        }\n"
                    "        res.json(item);\n");
            } else if (strcmp(method, "DELETE") == 0) {
                doc_buf_append(&buf,
                    "        let ok = db.delete(req.params.id);\n"
                    "        if !ok {\n"
                    "            return res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" });\n"
                    "        }\n"
                    "        res.json({ deleted: true });\n");
            } else {
                doc_buf_append(&buf,
                    "        res.json({ message: \"OK\" });\n");
            }
            doc_buf_append(&buf, "    };\n\n");
        }
    }

    /* AI endpoint if needed */
    if (spec->needs_ai) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    // AI endpoint\n"
            "    route POST /api/ai/ask -> fn(req, res) {\n"
            "        let { prompt } = req.body;\n"
            "        if !prompt {\n"
            "            return res.status(400).json({ error: \"Prompt required\" });\n"
            "        }\n"
            "        let response = ai.ask(prompt);\n"
            "        res.json({ response });\n"
            "    };\n\n");
    }

    doc_buf_append(&buf, "}\n");
    free(slug);
    return doc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* --- model file (e.g., user.nc) --- */
static char *gen_model_nc(const char *model_name, NCDocSpec *spec) {
    NCDocBuf buf = doc_buf_new();
    char lower[64];
    snprintf(lower, sizeof(lower), "%s", model_name);
    doc_tolower(lower);

    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "/*\n"
        " * %s model\n"
        " * Auto-generated by NC AI Doc Generator\n"
        " */\n\n"
        "import std.db;\nimport std.json;\n\n",
        model_name);

    doc_buf_printf(&buf, "model %s {\n", model_name);

    /* Generate fields based on model name */
    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "    id:         int    @primary @auto;\n"
        "    created_at: str    @default(now());\n"
        "    updated_at: str    @default(now());\n");

    if (strcasecmp(model_name, "User") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    email:      str    @unique;\n"
            "    password:   str;\n"
            "    name:       str;\n"
            "    role:       str    @default(\"user\");\n"
            "    active:     bool   @default(true);\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Post") == 0 ||
               strcasecmp(model_name, "Article") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    title:      str;\n"
            "    content:    str;\n"
            "    slug:       str    @unique;\n"
            "    published:  bool   @default(false);\n"
            "    author_id:  int    @ref(User.id);\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Product") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    name:       str;\n"
            "    description:str;\n"
            "    price:      float;\n"
            "    stock:      int    @default(0);\n"
            "    category:   str;\n"
            "    image_url:  str;\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Order") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    user_id:    int    @ref(User.id);\n"
            "    total:      float;\n"
            "    status:     str    @default(\"pending\");\n"
            "    items:      str;   // JSON array of items\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Comment") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    content:    str;\n"
            "    author_id:  int    @ref(User.id);\n"
            "    post_id:    int    @ref(Post.id);\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Message") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    sender_id:  int    @ref(User.id);\n"
            "    receiver_id:int    @ref(User.id);\n"
            "    content:    str;\n"
            "    read:       bool   @default(false);\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Task") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    title:      str;\n"
            "    description:str;\n"
            "    status:     str    @default(\"todo\");\n"
            "    priority:   int    @default(0);\n"
            "    assignee_id:int    @ref(User.id);\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Category") == 0 ||
               strcasecmp(model_name, "Tag") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    name:       str    @unique;\n"
            "    slug:       str    @unique;\n"
            "    description:str;\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Payment") == 0 ||
               strcasecmp(model_name, "Invoice") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    user_id:    int    @ref(User.id);\n"
            "    amount:     float;\n"
            "    currency:   str    @default(\"USD\");\n"
            "    status:     str    @default(\"pending\");\n"
            "    method:     str;\n");
    } else if (strcasecmp(model_name, "Notification") == 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    user_id:    int    @ref(User.id);\n"
            "    title:      str;\n"
            "    message:    str;\n"
            "    read:       bool   @default(false);\n"
            "    type:       str    @default(\"info\");\n");
    } else {
        /* Generic model — add name and description */
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "    name:       str;\n"
            "    description:str;\n"
            "    status:     str    @default(\"active\");\n");
    }

    doc_buf_append(&buf, "}\n\n");

    /* CRUD functions */
    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "// CRUD operations for %s\n\n"
        "fn create_%s(data: map) -> %s {\n"
        "    return db.create(\"%s\", data);\n"
        "}\n\n"
        "fn find_%s(id: int) -> %s {\n"
        "    return db.findById(\"%s\", id);\n"
        "}\n\n"
        "fn list_%ss(query: map) -> list<%s> {\n"
        "    return db.findAll(\"%s\", query);\n"
        "}\n\n"
        "fn update_%s(id: int, data: map) -> %s {\n"
        "    return db.update(\"%s\", id, data);\n"
        "}\n\n"
        "fn delete_%s(id: int) -> bool {\n"
        "    return db.delete(\"%s\", id);\n"
        "}\n",
        model_name,
        lower, model_name, model_name,
        lower, model_name, model_name,
        lower, model_name, model_name,
        lower, model_name, model_name,
        lower, model_name);

    return doc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* --- NCUI page --- */
static char *gen_page_ncui(const char *page_name, NCDocSpec *spec) {
    NCDocBuf buf = doc_buf_new();
    char capitalized[64];
    snprintf(capitalized, sizeof(capitalized), "%s", page_name);
    doc_capitalize(capitalized);

    /* Theme colors based on spec */
    const char *primary_color = "#e94560";
    const char *bg_color      = "#1a1a2e";
    const char *text_color    = "#eee";
    const char *card_bg       = "#16213e";

    if (spec->theme) {
        if (strcmp(spec->theme, "light") == 0) {
            bg_color   = "#ffffff";
            text_color = "#333333";
            card_bg    = "#f5f5f5";
        } else if (strcmp(spec->theme, "blue") == 0) {
            primary_color = "#2196F3";
            bg_color      = "#0d1b2a";
            card_bg       = "#1b2838";
        } else if (strcmp(spec->theme, "green") == 0) {
            primary_color = "#4CAF50";
            bg_color      = "#1a2e1a";
            card_bg       = "#213e21";
        } else if (strcmp(spec->theme, "purple") == 0) {
            primary_color = "#9C27B0";
            bg_color      = "#1a1a2e";
            card_bg       = "#2e1a3e";
        }
    }

    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "/*\n"
        " * %s page\n"
        " * Auto-generated by NC AI Doc Generator\n"
        " */\n\n"
        "page %s {\n\n"
        "    theme {\n"
        "        primary: \"%s\";\n"
        "        bg:      \"%s\";\n"
        "        text:    \"%s\";\n"
        "        font:    \"Inter\";\n"
        "    }\n\n",
        capitalized, capitalized,
        primary_color, bg_color, text_color);

    /* Page-specific content */
    if (strcmp(page_name, "home") == 0 ||
        strcmp(page_name, "landing") == 0) {
        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "    // Navigation\n"
            "    nav {\n"
            "        style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 16; }\n"
            "        row {\n"
            "            text(\"%s\") { style { fontSize: 24; fontWeight: \"bold\"; color: \"%s\"; } }\n"
            "            spacer;\n",
            card_bg, spec->name, primary_color);

        /* Nav links based on available pages */
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_pages; i++) {
            char cap[64];
            snprintf(cap, sizeof(cap), "%s", spec->pages[i]);
            doc_capitalize(cap);
            doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                "            link(\"/%s\", \"%s\");\n", spec->pages[i], cap);
        }

        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n"
            "    // Hero section\n"
            "    col {\n"
            "        style { padding: 80; align: \"center\"; }\n"
            "        text(\"%s\") {\n"
            "            style { fontSize: 48; fontWeight: \"bold\"; }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "        text(\"Built with NC\") {\n"
            "            style { fontSize: 20; color: \"#888\"; marginTop: 16; }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "        row {\n"
            "            style { marginTop: 32; gap: 16; }\n"
            "            button(\"Get Started\", onClick: { navigate(\"/dashboard\"); }) {\n"
            "                style { bg: \"%s\"; color: \"#fff\"; padding: 16; radius: 8; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            button(\"Learn More\", onClick: { navigate(\"/about\"); }) {\n"
            "                style { bg: \"transparent\"; border: \"1px solid %s\"; color: \"%s\"; padding: 16; radius: 8; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n",
            spec->name, primary_color, primary_color, primary_color);

        /* Features section */
        if (spec->n_features > 0) {
            doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                "    // Features\n"
                "    col {\n"
                "        style { padding: 40; }\n"
                "        text(\"Features\") { style { fontSize: 32; fontWeight: \"bold\"; align: \"center\"; } }\n"
                "        grid(cols: 3) {\n"
                "            style { gap: 24; marginTop: 32; }\n");
            for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_features && i < 6; i++) {
                char feat[64];
                snprintf(feat, sizeof(feat), "%s", spec->features[i]);
                /* Make feature name presentable */
                for (int j = 0; feat[j]; j++) {
                    if (feat[j] == '_') feat[j] = ' ';
                }
                doc_capitalize(feat);
                doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                    "            col {\n"
                    "                style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 24; radius: 12; }\n"
                    "                text(\"%s\") { style { fontSize: 18; fontWeight: \"bold\"; } }\n"
                    "                text(\"Powered by NC\") { style { color: \"#888\"; marginTop: 8; } }\n"
                    "            }\n",
                    card_bg, feat);
            }
            doc_buf_append(&buf,
                "        }\n"
                "    }\n\n");
        }

    } else if (strcmp(page_name, "login") == 0) {
        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "    state email = \"\";\n"
            "    state password = \"\";\n"
            "    state error = \"\";\n"
            "    state loading = false;\n\n"
            "    col {\n"
            "        style { maxWidth: 400; margin: \"80px auto\"; padding: 40; bg: \"%s\"; radius: 12; }\n\n"
            "        text(\"Login\") { style { fontSize: 32; fontWeight: \"bold\"; align: \"center\"; } }\n\n"
            "        if error {\n"
            "            text(error) { style { color: \"#f44336\"; padding: 12; bg: \"#f4433620\"; radius: 8; } }\n"
            "        }\n\n"
            "        col {\n"
            "            style { gap: 16; marginTop: 24; }\n"
            "            input(type: \"email\", bind: email, placeholder: \"Email\") {\n"
            "                style { padding: 12; radius: 8; border: \"1px solid #333\"; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            input(type: \"password\", bind: password, placeholder: \"Password\") {\n"
            "                style { padding: 12; radius: 8; border: \"1px solid #333\"; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            button(loading ? \"Logging in...\" : \"Login\", onClick: {\n"
            "                loading = true;\n"
            "                error = \"\";\n"
            "                let resp = api.post(\"/api/login\", { email, password });\n"
            "                if resp.ok {\n"
            "                    auth.setToken(resp.data.token);\n"
            "                    navigate(\"/dashboard\");\n"
            "                } else {\n"
            "                    error = resp.data.error ?? \"Login failed\";\n"
            "                }\n"
            "                loading = false;\n"
            "            }) {\n"
            "                style { bg: \"%s\"; color: \"#fff\"; padding: 14; radius: 8; fontWeight: \"bold\"; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "        }\n\n"
            "        row {\n"
            "            style { marginTop: 16; justify: \"center\"; }\n"
            "            text(\"Don't have an account? \");\n"
            "            link(\"/signup\", \"Sign up\") { style { color: \"%s\"; } }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n",
            card_bg, primary_color, primary_color);

    } else if (strcmp(page_name, "signup") == 0) {
        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "    state name = \"\";\n"
            "    state email = \"\";\n"
            "    state password = \"\";\n"
            "    state error = \"\";\n"
            "    state loading = false;\n\n"
            "    col {\n"
            "        style { maxWidth: 400; margin: \"80px auto\"; padding: 40; bg: \"%s\"; radius: 12; }\n\n"
            "        text(\"Create Account\") { style { fontSize: 32; fontWeight: \"bold\"; align: \"center\"; } }\n\n"
            "        if error {\n"
            "            text(error) { style { color: \"#f44336\"; padding: 12; bg: \"#f4433620\"; radius: 8; } }\n"
            "        }\n\n"
            "        col {\n"
            "            style { gap: 16; marginTop: 24; }\n"
            "            input(type: \"text\", bind: name, placeholder: \"Full Name\") {\n"
            "                style { padding: 12; radius: 8; border: \"1px solid #333\"; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            input(type: \"email\", bind: email, placeholder: \"Email\") {\n"
            "                style { padding: 12; radius: 8; border: \"1px solid #333\"; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            input(type: \"password\", bind: password, placeholder: \"Password\") {\n"
            "                style { padding: 12; radius: 8; border: \"1px solid #333\"; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            button(loading ? \"Creating...\" : \"Sign Up\", onClick: {\n"
            "                loading = true;\n"
            "                error = \"\";\n"
            "                let resp = api.post(\"/api/register\", { name, email, password });\n"
            "                if resp.ok {\n"
            "                    auth.setToken(resp.data.token);\n"
            "                    navigate(\"/dashboard\");\n"
            "                } else {\n"
            "                    error = resp.data.error ?? \"Registration failed\";\n"
            "                }\n"
            "                loading = false;\n"
            "            }) {\n"
            "                style { bg: \"%s\"; color: \"#fff\"; padding: 14; radius: 8; fontWeight: \"bold\"; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "        }\n\n"
            "        row {\n"
            "            style { marginTop: 16; justify: \"center\"; }\n"
            "            text(\"Already have an account? \");\n"
            "            link(\"/login\", \"Login\") { style { color: \"%s\"; } }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n",
            card_bg, primary_color, primary_color);

    } else if (strcmp(page_name, "dashboard") == 0) {
        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "    state data = [];\n"
            "    state loading = true;\n\n"
            "    onMount: {\n"
            "        data = api.get(\"/api/stats\").data ?? [];\n"
            "        loading = false;\n"
            "    }\n\n"
            "    // Sidebar + main layout\n"
            "    row {\n"
            "        // Sidebar\n"
            "        col {\n"
            "            style { width: 240; bg: \"%s\"; padding: 24; minHeight: \"100vh\"; }\n"
            "            text(\"%s\") { style { fontSize: 20; fontWeight: \"bold\"; color: \"%s\"; } }\n"
            "            col {\n"
            "                style { marginTop: 32; gap: 8; }\n",
            card_bg, spec->name, primary_color);

        /* Sidebar links */
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_pages && i < 8; i++) {
            char cap[64];
            snprintf(cap, sizeof(cap), "%s", spec->pages[i]);
            doc_capitalize(cap);
            doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                "                link(\"/%s\", \"%s\") { style { padding: 12; radius: 8; } }\n",
                spec->pages[i], cap);
        }

        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "            }\n"
            "        }\n\n"
            "        // Main content\n"
            "        col {\n"
            "            style { flex: 1; padding: 32; }\n"
            "            text(\"Dashboard\") { style { fontSize: 32; fontWeight: \"bold\"; } }\n\n"
            "            if loading {\n"
            "                text(\"Loading...\") { style { color: \"#888\"; } }\n"
            "            } else {\n"
            "                // Stats grid\n"
            "                grid(cols: 3) {\n"
            "                    style { gap: 24; marginTop: 24; }\n"
            "                    col {\n"
            "                        style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 24; radius: 12; }\n"
            "                        text(\"Total Items\") { style { color: \"#888\"; } }\n"
            "                        text(\"0\") { style { fontSize: 36; fontWeight: \"bold\"; marginTop: 8; } }\n"
            "                    }\n"
            "                    col {\n"
            "                        style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 24; radius: 12; }\n"
            "                        text(\"Active\") { style { color: \"#888\"; } }\n"
            "                        text(\"0\") { style { fontSize: 36; fontWeight: \"bold\"; color: \"#4CAF50\"; marginTop: 8; } }\n"
            "                    }\n"
            "                    col {\n"
            "                        style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 24; radius: 12; }\n"
            "                        text(\"Pending\") { style { color: \"#888\"; } }\n"
            "                        text(\"0\") { style { fontSize: 36; fontWeight: \"bold\"; color: \"%s\"; marginTop: 8; } }\n"
            "                    }\n"
            "                }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n",
            card_bg, card_bg, card_bg, primary_color);

    } else if (strcmp(page_name, "settings") == 0) {
        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "    state name = \"\";\n"
            "    state email = \"\";\n"
            "    state saved = false;\n\n"
            "    onMount: {\n"
            "        let user = api.get(\"/api/me\").data;\n"
            "        if user {\n"
            "            name = user.name;\n"
            "            email = user.email;\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n"
            "    col {\n"
            "        style { maxWidth: 600; margin: \"40px auto\"; padding: 32; }\n"
            "        text(\"Settings\") { style { fontSize: 32; fontWeight: \"bold\"; } }\n\n"
            "        col {\n"
            "            style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 32; radius: 12; marginTop: 24; gap: 16; }\n"
            "            text(\"Profile\") { style { fontSize: 20; fontWeight: \"bold\"; } }\n"
            "            input(type: \"text\", bind: name, label: \"Name\") {\n"
            "                style { padding: 12; radius: 8; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            input(type: \"email\", bind: email, label: \"Email\") {\n"
            "                style { padding: 12; radius: 8; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            button(\"Save Changes\", onClick: {\n"
            "                api.put(\"/api/me\", { name, email });\n"
            "                saved = true;\n"
            "            }) {\n"
            "                style { bg: \"%s\"; color: \"#fff\"; padding: 12; radius: 8; }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "            if saved {\n"
            "                text(\"Settings saved!\") { style { color: \"#4CAF50\"; } }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n",
            card_bg, primary_color);

    } else if (strcmp(page_name, "profile") == 0) {
        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "    state user = null;\n\n"
            "    onMount: {\n"
            "        user = api.get(\"/api/me\").data;\n"
            "    }\n\n"
            "    col {\n"
            "        style { maxWidth: 600; margin: \"40px auto\"; padding: 32; }\n"
            "        if user {\n"
            "            col {\n"
            "                style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 32; radius: 12; align: \"center\"; }\n"
            "                text(user.name) { style { fontSize: 28; fontWeight: \"bold\"; } }\n"
            "                text(user.email) { style { color: \"#888\"; marginTop: 8; } }\n"
            "                row {\n"
            "                    style { marginTop: 24; gap: 16; }\n"
            "                    button(\"Edit Profile\", onClick: { navigate(\"/settings\"); }) {\n"
            "                        style { bg: \"%s\"; color: \"#fff\"; padding: 12; radius: 8; }\n"
            "                    }\n"
            "                    button(\"Logout\", onClick: { auth.logout(); navigate(\"/\"); }) {\n"
            "                        style { bg: \"#f44336\"; color: \"#fff\"; padding: 12; radius: 8; }\n"
            "                    }\n"
            "                }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "        } else {\n"
            "            text(\"Loading...\") { style { color: \"#888\"; } }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n",
            card_bg, primary_color);

    } else {
        /* Generic page */
        doc_buf_printf(&buf,
            "    state data = [];\n"
            "    state loading = true;\n\n"
            "    onMount: {\n"
            "        data = api.get(\"/api/%s\").data ?? [];\n"
            "        loading = false;\n"
            "    }\n\n"
            "    col {\n"
            "        style { maxWidth: 1200; margin: \"0 auto\"; padding: 32; }\n"
            "        text(\"%s\") { style { fontSize: 32; fontWeight: \"bold\"; } }\n\n"
            "        if loading {\n"
            "            text(\"Loading...\") { style { color: \"#888\"; } }\n"
            "        } else {\n"
            "            grid(cols: 2) {\n"
            "                style { gap: 24; marginTop: 24; }\n"
            "                for item in data {\n"
            "                    col {\n"
            "                        style { bg: \"%s\"; padding: 24; radius: 12; }\n"
            "                        text(item.name ?? item.title ?? \"Item\") {\n"
            "                            style { fontSize: 18; fontWeight: \"bold\"; }\n"
            "                        }\n"
            "                        text(item.description ?? \"\") {\n"
            "                            style { color: \"#888\"; marginTop: 8; }\n"
            "                        }\n"
            "                    }\n"
            "                }\n"
            "            }\n"
            "        }\n"
            "    }\n\n",
            page_name, capitalized, card_bg);
    }

    doc_buf_append(&buf, "}\n");
    return doc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* --- test file --- */
static char *gen_test_nc(NCDocSpec *spec) {
    NCDocBuf buf = doc_buf_new();
    char *slug = doc_slugify(spec->name);

    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "/*\n"
        " * Tests for %s\n"
        " * Auto-generated by NC AI Doc Generator\n"
        " */\n\n"
        "import std.test;\nimport std.http;\n\n"
        "let BASE_URL = \"http://localhost:8080\";\n\n",
        spec->name);

    /* Health check test */
    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "test \"health check\" {\n"
        "    let resp = http.get(BASE_URL + \"/health\");\n"
        "    assert(resp.status == 200);\n"
        "    assert(resp.body.status == \"ok\");\n"
        "}\n\n");

    /* Auth tests */
    if (spec->needs_auth) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf,
            "test \"register new user\" {\n"
            "    let resp = http.post(BASE_URL + \"/api/register\", {\n"
            "        email: \"test@example.com\",\n"
            "        password: \"testpass123\",\n"
            "        name: \"Test User\"\n"
            "    });\n"
            "    assert(resp.status == 200);\n"
            "    assert(resp.body.token != null);\n"
            "    assert(resp.body.user.email == \"test@example.com\");\n"
            "}\n\n"
            "test \"login\" {\n"
            "    let resp = http.post(BASE_URL + \"/api/login\", {\n"
            "        email: \"test@example.com\",\n"
            "        password: \"testpass123\"\n"
            "    });\n"
            "    assert(resp.status == 200);\n"
            "    assert(resp.body.token != null);\n"
            "}\n\n"
            "test \"login with wrong password\" {\n"
            "    let resp = http.post(BASE_URL + \"/api/login\", {\n"
            "        email: \"test@example.com\",\n"
            "        password: \"wrong\"\n"
            "    });\n"
            "    assert(resp.status == 401);\n"
            "}\n\n");
    }

    /* Endpoint tests */
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_endpoints; i++) {
        char method[16], path[256];
        if (sscanf(spec->endpoints[i], "%15s %255s", method, path) >= 2) {
            /* Skip auth endpoints */
            if (strstr(path, "/login") || strstr(path, "/register"))
                continue;

            /* Replace :id with 1 for test */
            char test_path[256];
            snprintf(test_path, sizeof(test_path), "%s", path);
            char *id_pos = strstr(test_path, ":id");
            if (id_pos) {
                memmove(id_pos + 1, id_pos + 3, strlen(id_pos + 3) + 1);
                *id_pos = '1';
            }

            doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                "test \"%s %s\" {\n", method, path);

            if (strcmp(method, "GET") == 0) {
                doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                    "    let resp = http.get(BASE_URL + \"%s\");\n"
                    "    assert(resp.status == 200 || resp.status == 404);\n",
                    test_path);
            } else if (strcmp(method, "POST") == 0) {
                doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                    "    let resp = http.post(BASE_URL + \"%s\", {\n"
                    "        name: \"Test Item\"\n"
                    "    });\n"
                    "    assert(resp.status == 201 || resp.status == 200);\n",
                    test_path);
            } else if (strcmp(method, "PUT") == 0) {
                doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                    "    let resp = http.put(BASE_URL + \"%s\", {\n"
                    "        name: \"Updated Item\"\n"
                    "    });\n"
                    "    assert(resp.status == 200 || resp.status == 404);\n",
                    test_path);
            } else if (strcmp(method, "DELETE") == 0) {
                doc_buf_printf(&buf,
                    "    let resp = http.delete(BASE_URL + \"%s\");\n"
                    "    assert(resp.status == 200 || resp.status == 404);\n",
                    test_path);
            }

            doc_buf_append(&buf, "}\n\n");
        }
    }

    free(slug);
    return doc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* --- README.md --- */
static char *gen_readme(NCDocSpec *spec) {
    NCDocBuf buf = doc_buf_new();

    doc_buf_printf(&buf, "# %s\n\n", spec->name);

    /* Description */
    if (spec->description) {
        /* Use first paragraph or first 500 chars */
        const char *end = strstr(spec->description, "\n\n");
        if (!end || (size_t)(end - spec->description) > 500)
            end = spec->description + (strlen(spec->description) > 500 ?
                                       500 : strlen(spec->description));
        doc_buf_printf(&buf, "%.*s\n\n", (int)(end - spec->description),
                       spec->description);
    }

    doc_buf_append(&buf, "## Getting Started\n\n```bash\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "# Start the server\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "chmod +x start.sh\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "./start.sh\n\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "# Or run directly\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "nc run server.nc\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "```\n\n");

    /* Features */
    if (spec->n_features > 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "## Features\n\n");
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_features; i++) {
            char feat[64];
            snprintf(feat, sizeof(feat), "%s", spec->features[i]);
            for (int j = 0; feat[j]; j++) {
                if (feat[j] == '_') feat[j] = ' ';
            }
            doc_capitalize(feat);
            doc_buf_printf(&buf, "- %s\n", feat);
        }
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "\n");
    }

    /* API endpoints */
    if (spec->n_endpoints > 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "## API Endpoints\n\n");
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "| Method | Path | Description |\n");
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "|--------|------|-------------|\n");

        if (spec->needs_auth) {
            doc_buf_append(&buf,
                "| POST | /api/register | Register new user |\n"
                "| POST | /api/login | User login |\n");
        }

        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_endpoints; i++) {
            char method[16], path[256];
            if (sscanf(spec->endpoints[i], "%15s %255s", method, path) >= 2) {
                doc_buf_printf(&buf, "| %s | %s | - |\n", method, path);
            }
        }
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "\n");
    }

    /* Pages */
    if (spec->n_pages > 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "## Pages\n\n");
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_pages; i++) {
            char cap[64];
            snprintf(cap, sizeof(cap), "%s", spec->pages[i]);
            doc_capitalize(cap);
            doc_buf_printf(&buf, "- `/%s` — %s page\n", spec->pages[i], cap);
        }
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "\n");
    }

    /* Data models */
    if (spec->n_models > 0) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "## Data Models\n\n");
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_models; i++) {
            doc_buf_printf(&buf, "- `%s`\n", spec->models[i]);
        }
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "\n");
    }

    /* Tech stack */
    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "## Tech Stack\n\n"
        "- **Backend**: NC language\n"
        "- **Frontend**: NC UI (NCUI)\n");
    if (spec->needs_database)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "- **Database**: SQLite (configurable)\n");
    if (spec->needs_auth)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "- **Auth**: JWT\n");
    if (spec->needs_ai)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "- **AI**: NC AI bridge\n");

    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "\n---\n*Generated by NC AI Doc Generator*\n");

    return doc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* --- start.sh --- */
static char *gen_start_script(NCDocSpec *spec) {
    NCDocBuf buf = doc_buf_new();

    doc_buf_append(&buf, "#!/bin/bash\n");
    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "# Start script for %s\n"
        "# Auto-generated by NC AI Doc Generator\n\n"
        "set -e\n\n"
        "echo \"Starting %s...\"\n\n",
        spec->name, spec->name);

    /* Environment variables */
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "# Environment (override with .env file)\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "export PORT=${PORT:-8080}\n");
    if (spec->needs_database)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "export DATABASE_URL=${DATABASE_URL:-\"sqlite://data.db\"}\n");
    if (spec->needs_auth)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "export JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET:-\"change-me-in-production\"}\n");
    if (spec->needs_ai)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "export AI_PROVIDER=${AI_PROVIDER:-\"local\"}\n");

    doc_buf_append(&buf,
        "\n"
        "# Load .env if exists\n"
        "if [ -f .env ]; then\n"
        "    export $(cat .env | grep -v '^#' | xargs)\n"
        "fi\n\n"
        "# Run the server\n"
        "nc run server.nc\n");

    return doc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* --- nc.pkg manifest --- */
static char *gen_package_manifest(NCDocSpec *spec) {
    NCDocBuf buf = doc_buf_new();
    char *slug = doc_slugify(spec->name);

    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "# NC Package Manifest\n"
        "# Auto-generated by NC AI Doc Generator\n\n"
        "name: \"%s\"\n"
        "version: \"0.1.0\"\n"
        "entry: \"server.nc\"\n\n",
        slug);

    doc_buf_append(&buf, "dependencies:\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "  std.http: \"*\"\n");
    doc_buf_append(&buf, "  std.json: \"*\"\n");
    if (spec->needs_database)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "  std.db: \"*\"\n");
    if (spec->needs_auth) {
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "  std.auth: \"*\"\n");
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "  std.crypto: \"*\"\n");
    }
    if (spec->needs_ai)
        doc_buf_append(&buf, "  std.ai: \"*\"\n");

    doc_buf_printf(&buf,
        "\nscripts:\n"
        "  start: \"nc run server.nc\"\n"
        "  test:  \"nc test tests/\"\n"
        "  dev:   \"nc run --watch server.nc\"\n");

    free(slug);
    return doc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  AI-enhanced generation (uses bridge if available)
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* Try to enhance template output with AI. If AI fails, return template as-is. */
static char *ai_enhance(NCAIBridge *bridge, const char *template_code,
                        const char *file_type, const char *context) {
    if (!bridge) return doc_strdup(template_code);

    NCAIProviderConfig *cfg = nc_ai_bridge_get_active(bridge);
    if (!cfg) return doc_strdup(template_code);

    /* Only enhance with non-local providers (local model may not be loaded) */
    if (cfg->type == NC_AI_LOCAL && !bridge->local_loaded)
        return doc_strdup(template_code);

    NCDocBuf prompt = doc_buf_new();
    doc_buf_printf(&prompt,
        "Improve this %s code. Keep the same structure but make it more "
        "complete and production-ready. Context: %s\n\n"
        "Current code:\n```\n%s\n```\n\n"
        "Output ONLY the improved code, no explanations.",
        file_type, context ? context : "NC project",
        template_code);

    NCAIResponse *resp = nc_ai_bridge_ask(bridge, prompt.data);
    doc_buf_free(&prompt);

    if (resp && resp->success && resp->content && strlen(resp->content) > 10) {
        char *enhanced = doc_strdup(resp->content);
        nc_ai_response_free(resp);
        return enhanced;
    }

    if (resp) nc_ai_response_free(resp);
    return doc_strdup(template_code);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Project generator
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_ai_doc_generate(NCAIBridge *bridge, NCDocSpec *spec,
                       const char *output_dir) {
    if (!spec || !output_dir) return -1;

    printf("[nc-ai] Generating project: %s\n", spec->name);
    printf("[nc-ai] Output directory: %s\n", output_dir);

    /* Create directory structure */
    if (ensure_dir(output_dir) != 0) return -1;

    char path[1024];

    snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/models", output_dir);
    ensure_dir(path);

    snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/pages", output_dir);
    ensure_dir(path);

    snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/tests", output_dir);
    ensure_dir(path);

    /* Determine if AI enhancement is available */
    int use_ai = 0;
    if (bridge) {
        NCAIProviderConfig *cfg = nc_ai_bridge_get_active(bridge);
        if (cfg) {
            if (cfg->type != NC_AI_LOCAL || bridge->local_loaded)
                use_ai = 1;
        }
    }

    if (use_ai) {
        printf("[nc-ai] AI enhancement enabled (%s)\n",
               nc_ai_bridge_get_active(bridge)->name);
    } else {
        printf("[nc-ai] Using template-based generation\n");
    }

    int files_written = 0;

    /* 1. server.nc */
    printf("[nc-ai] Generating server.nc...\n");
    {
        char *code = gen_server_nc(spec);
        if (use_ai) {
            char *enhanced = ai_enhance(bridge, code, "NC service", spec->name);
            free(code);
            code = enhanced;
        }
        snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/server.nc", output_dir);
        if (write_file(path, code) == 0) files_written++;
        free(code);
    }

    /* 2. Model files */
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_models; i++) {
        printf("[nc-ai] Generating models/%s.nc...\n", spec->models[i]);
        char *code = gen_model_nc(spec->models[i], spec);
        char lower[64];
        snprintf(lower, sizeof(lower), "%s", spec->models[i]);
        doc_tolower(lower);
        snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/models/%s.nc", output_dir, lower);
        if (write_file(path, code) == 0) files_written++;
        free(code);
    }

    /* 3. UI pages */
    for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_pages; i++) {
        printf("[nc-ai] Generating pages/%s.ncui...\n", spec->pages[i]);
        char *code = gen_page_ncui(spec->pages[i], spec);
        snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/pages/%s.ncui", output_dir,
                 spec->pages[i]);
        if (write_file(path, code) == 0) files_written++;
        free(code);
    }

    /* 4. Test file */
    printf("[nc-ai] Generating tests/test_server.nc...\n");
    {
        char *code = gen_test_nc(spec);
        snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/tests/test_server.nc", output_dir);
        if (write_file(path, code) == 0) files_written++;
        free(code);
    }

    /* 5. start.sh */
    printf("[nc-ai] Generating start.sh...\n");
    {
        char *code = gen_start_script(spec);
        snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/start.sh", output_dir);
        if (write_file(path, code) == 0) {
            /* Make executable */
            chmod(path, 0755);
            files_written++;
        }
        free(code);
    }

    /* 6. README.md */
    printf("[nc-ai] Generating README.md...\n");
    {
        char *code = gen_readme(spec);
        snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/README.md", output_dir);
        if (write_file(path, code) == 0) files_written++;
        free(code);
    }

    /* 7. nc.pkg */
    printf("[nc-ai] Generating nc.pkg...\n");
    {
        char *code = gen_package_manifest(spec);
        snprintf(path, sizeof(path), "%s/nc.pkg", output_dir);
        if (write_file(path, code) == 0) files_written++;
        free(code);
    }

    printf("[nc-ai] Done! Generated %d files in %s\n",
           files_written, output_dir);

    return files_written;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Generate from file
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_ai_doc_from_file(NCAIBridge *bridge, const char *doc_path,
                        const char *output_dir) {
    if (!doc_path || !output_dir) return -1;

    /* Read the document file */
    FILE *fp = fopen(doc_path, "r");
    if (!fp) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Cannot open document: %s (%s)\n",
                doc_path, strerror(errno));
        return -1;
    }

    /* Get file size */
    fseek(fp, 0, SEEK_END);
    long size = ftell(fp);
    fseek(fp, 0, SEEK_SET);

    if (size <= 0 || size > NC_DOC_BUF_MAX) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Document too large or empty: %s\n", doc_path);
        fclose(fp);
        return -1;
    }

    char *text = (char *)malloc((size_t)size + 1);
    if (!text) {
        fclose(fp);
        return -1;
    }

    size_t read_bytes = fread(text, 1, (size_t)size, fp);
    text[read_bytes] = '\0';
    fclose(fp);

    /* Parse */
    NCDocSpec *spec = nc_ai_doc_parse(text);
    free(text);

    if (!spec) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Failed to parse document: %s\n", doc_path);
        return -1;
    }

    /* Print summary */
    printf("[nc-ai] Parsed document: %s\n", doc_path);
    printf("[nc-ai]   Project: %s\n", spec->name);
    printf("[nc-ai]   Features: %d\n", spec->n_features);
    printf("[nc-ai]   Endpoints: %d\n", spec->n_endpoints);
    printf("[nc-ai]   Pages: %d\n", spec->n_pages);
    printf("[nc-ai]   Models: %d\n", spec->n_models);
    printf("[nc-ai]   Auth: %s\n", spec->needs_auth ? "yes" : "no");
    printf("[nc-ai]   AI: %s\n", spec->needs_ai ? "yes" : "no");
    printf("[nc-ai]   Database: %s\n", spec->needs_database ? "yes" : "no");
    printf("[nc-ai]   Theme: %s\n", spec->theme);

    /* Generate */
    int result = nc_ai_doc_generate(bridge, spec, output_dir);
    nc_ai_doc_spec_free(spec);
    return result;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  CLI handler
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_cmd_doc_generate(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc < 2) {
        fprintf(stderr,
            "Usage: nc-ai doc <document> [options]\n\n"
            "Generate an NC project from a document.\n\n"
            "Arguments:\n"
            "  <document>     Path to spec document (.md, .txt)\n\n"
            "Options:\n"
            "  --output DIR   Output directory (default: ./<project-name>)\n"
            "  --provider P   AI provider (openai, anthropic, ollama, local)\n"
            "  --no-ai        Skip AI enhancement, use templates only\n"
            "  --dry-run      Parse document and show spec without generating\n\n"
            "Examples:\n"
            "  nc-ai doc project_spec.md\n"
            "  nc-ai doc project_spec.md --output ./my-app\n"
            "  nc-ai doc project_spec.md --provider openai\n"
            "  nc-ai doc project_spec.md --dry-run\n");
        return 1;
    }

    const char *doc_path   = NULL;
    const char *output_dir = NULL;
    const char *provider   = NULL;
    int no_ai    = 0;
    int dry_run  = 0;

    /* Parse arguments */
    for (int i = 1; i < argc; i++) {
        if (strcmp(argv[i], "--output") == 0 && i + 1 < argc) {
            output_dir = argv[++i];
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--provider") == 0 && i + 1 < argc) {
            provider = argv[++i];
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--no-ai") == 0) {
            no_ai = 1;
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--dry-run") == 0) {
            dry_run = 1;
        } else if (argv[i][0] != '-') {
            doc_path = argv[i];
        } else {
            fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Unknown option: %s\n", argv[i]);
            return 1;
        }
    }

    if (!doc_path) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Error: No document path provided\n");
        return 1;
    }

    /* Read and parse document for dry-run or generation */
    FILE *fp = fopen(doc_path, "r");
    if (!fp) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Cannot open: %s (%s)\n",
                doc_path, strerror(errno));
        return 1;
    }

    fseek(fp, 0, SEEK_END);
    long size = ftell(fp);
    fseek(fp, 0, SEEK_SET);

    if (size <= 0 || size > NC_DOC_BUF_MAX) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Document too large or empty\n");
        fclose(fp);
        return 1;
    }

    char *text = (char *)malloc((size_t)size + 1);
    if (!text) { fclose(fp); return 1; }
    size_t rbytes = fread(text, 1, (size_t)size, fp);
    text[rbytes] = '\0';
    fclose(fp);

    NCDocSpec *spec = nc_ai_doc_parse(text);
    free(text);

    if (!spec) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc-ai] Failed to parse document\n");
        return 1;
    }

    /* Print parsed spec */
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Project:    %s\n", spec->name);
    printf("  Theme:      %s\n", spec->theme);
    printf("  Auth:       %s\n", spec->needs_auth ? "yes" : "no");
    printf("  AI:         %s\n", spec->needs_ai ? "yes" : "no");
    printf("  Database:   %s\n", spec->needs_database ? "yes" : "no");

    if (spec->n_features > 0) {
        printf("  Features:   ");
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_features; i++)
            printf("%s%s", spec->features[i], i < spec->n_features - 1 ? ", " : "");
        printf("\n");
    }
    if (spec->n_models > 0) {
        printf("  Models:     ");
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_models; i++)
            printf("%s%s", spec->models[i], i < spec->n_models - 1 ? ", " : "");
        printf("\n");
    }
    if (spec->n_endpoints > 0) {
        printf("  Endpoints:  %d routes\n", spec->n_endpoints);
    }
    if (spec->n_pages > 0) {
        printf("  Pages:      ");
        for (int i = 0; i < spec->n_pages; i++)
            printf("%s%s", spec->pages[i], i < spec->n_pages - 1 ? ", " : "");
        printf("\n");
    }
    printf("\n");

    if (dry_run) {
        printf("[nc-ai] Dry run complete. No files generated.\n");
        nc_ai_doc_spec_free(spec);
        return 0;
    }

    /* Determine output directory */
    char out_buf[1024];
    if (!output_dir) {
        char *slug = doc_slugify(spec->name);
        snprintf(out_buf, sizeof(out_buf), "./%s", slug);
        output_dir = out_buf;
        free(slug);
    }

    /* Set up bridge */
    NCAIBridge *bridge = NULL;
    if (!no_ai) {
        bridge = nc_ai_bridge_create();
        nc_ai_bridge_auto_detect(bridge);

        if (provider) {
            if (nc_ai_bridge_set_active_by_name(bridge, provider) != 0) {
                fprintf(stderr,
                    "[nc-ai] Warning: Provider '%s' not found, using default\n",
                    provider);
            }
        }
    }

    /* Generate */
    int result = nc_ai_doc_generate(bridge, spec, output_dir);

    /* Cleanup */
    nc_ai_doc_spec_free(spec);
    if (bridge) nc_ai_bridge_free(bridge);

    return (result > 0) ? 0 : 1;
}


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_doc.h

/*
 * nc_ai_doc.h — Document-driven NC project generation.
 *
 * Takes a natural language document (text, markdown, spec) and
 * generates an entire NC project with backend, models, UI pages,
 * tests, and configuration.
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 */

#ifndef NC_AI_DOC_H
#define NC_AI_DOC_H

#include "nc_ai_bridge.h"

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Document specification — parsed from natural language
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

#define NC_DOC_MAX_ITEMS 64

typedef struct {
    char *name;            /* Project name                  */
    char *description;     /* Full description text         */
    char **features;       /* Extracted features            */
    int n_features;
    char **endpoints;      /* Extracted API endpoints       */
    int n_endpoints;
    char **pages;          /* Extracted UI pages            */
    int n_pages;
    char **models;         /* Data models (User, Post, etc) */
    int n_models;
    int needs_auth;        /* Requires authentication       */
    int needs_ai;          /* Requires AI integration       */
    int needs_database;    /* Requires database             */
    char *theme;           /* UI theme (dark/light/color)   */
} NCDocSpec;

/* ── Parsing ───────────────────────────────────────────── */

NCDocSpec *nc_ai_doc_parse(const char *doc_text);
void       nc_ai_doc_spec_free(NCDocSpec *spec);

/* ── Generation ────────────────────────────────────────── */

int nc_ai_doc_generate(NCAIBridge *bridge, NCDocSpec *spec,
                       const char *output_dir);

int nc_ai_doc_from_file(NCAIBridge *bridge, const char *doc_path,
                        const char *output_dir);

/* ── CLI handler ───────────────────────────────────────── */

int nc_cmd_doc_generate(int argc, char **argv);

#endif /* NC_AI_DOC_H */


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_memory.c

/*
 * nc_ai_memory.c — Multi-Layer Cognitive Memory for NC AI.
 *
 * Full implementation of the 5-layer memory architecture:
 *   1. Working       — current task context (local to each ant)
 *   2. Episodic      — past problem-solution pairs with rewards
 *   3. Semantic      — learned concepts (code patterns, rules)
 *   4. Procedural    — how-to knowledge (generation strategies)
 *   5. Reinforcement — Q-table state-action-reward values
 *
 * Features:
 *   - Auto-decay recency scores over time
 *   - Prioritize frequently accessed entries
 *   - Consolidate patterns (3+ occurrences -> procedural)
 *   - Fuzzy matching for recall (keyword intersection scoring)
 *   - Graceful forgetting of low-relevance entries
 *   - Binary persistence (save/load)
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 *
 * By DevHeal Labs AI
 */

#include "nc_ai_memory.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>
#include <math.h>
#include <time.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Internal constants
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

#define NCM_DEFAULT_CAP        512
#define NCM_KEY_CAP            1024
#define NCM_DECAY_RATE         0.02f    /* 2% recency decay per cycle        */
#define NCM_FORGET_THRESHOLD   0.05f    /* forget entries below this score   */
#define NCM_CONSOLIDATE_THRESH 3        /* promote after 3+ accesses         */
#define NCM_CONSOLIDATE_REL    0.6f     /* min relevance to consolidate      */
#define NCM_MAX_RESULTS        64
#define NCM_BUF_SIZE           4096

/* Binary file magic */
#define NCM_MAGIC              0x4E434D45  /* "NCME" */
#define NCM_VERSION            1

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Internal helpers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *ncm_strdup(const char *s) {
    if (!s) return NULL;
    size_t len = strlen(s);
    char *dup = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
    if (dup) memcpy(dup, s, len + 1);
    return dup;
}

static void ncm_str_lower(char *dst, const char *src, size_t max) {
    size_t i = 0;
    while (src[i] && i < max - 1) {
        dst[i] = (char)tolower((unsigned char)src[i]);
        i++;
    }
    dst[i] = '\0';
}

/* Extract keywords from content for indexing */
static char *ncm_extract_key(const char *content) {
    if (!content) return NULL;

    /* Take first 128 chars, lowercase, strip punctuation */
    char buf[256];
    ncm_str_lower(buf, content, sizeof(buf));

    /* Keep only alphanumeric and spaces */
    for (int i = 0; buf[i]; i++) {
        if (!isalnum((unsigned char)buf[i]) && buf[i] != ' ')
            buf[i] = ' ';
    }
    return ncm_strdup(buf);
}

/* Keyword intersection scoring for fuzzy match (0.0 - 1.0) */
static float ncm_fuzzy_score(const char *query, const char *content) {
    if (!query || !content) return 0.0f;

    char lq[512], lc[1024];
    ncm_str_lower(lq, query, sizeof(lq));
    ncm_str_lower(lc, content, sizeof(lc));

    /* Tokenize query, count matches in content */
    int matches = 0;
    int total   = 0;
    char *tmp = ncm_strdup(lq);
    if (!tmp) return 0.0f;

    char *tok = strtok(tmp, " _-.,;:/\n\t");
    while (tok) {
        if (strlen(tok) > 2) {
            total++;
            if (strstr(lc, tok)) matches++;
        }
        tok = strtok(NULL, " _-.,;:/\n\t");
    }
    free(tmp);

    if (total == 0) {
        /* Fallback: direct substring */
        return strstr(lc, lq) ? 0.8f : 0.0f;
    }
    return (float)matches / (float)total;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Lifecycle
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCMemoryStore *nc_memory_create(int capacity) {
    if (capacity <= 0) capacity = NCM_DEFAULT_CAP;

    NCMemoryStore *mem = (NCMemoryStore *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCMemoryStore));
    if (!mem) return NULL;

    mem->entries = (NCMemoryEntry *)calloc((size_t)capacity, sizeof(NCMemoryEntry));
    if (!mem->entries) {
        free(mem);
        return NULL;
    }
    mem->n_entries = 0;
    mem->capacity  = capacity;

    /* Key index */
    mem->keys    = (char **)calloc(NCM_KEY_CAP, sizeof(char *));
    mem->key_map = (int *)calloc(NCM_KEY_CAP, sizeof(int));
    mem->n_keys  = 0;

    return mem;
}

void nc_memory_free(NCMemoryStore *mem) {
    if (!mem) return;
    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
        free(mem->entries[i].content);
    }
    free(mem->entries);
    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_keys; i++) {
        free(mem->keys[i]);
    }
    free(mem->keys);
    free(mem->key_map);
    free(mem);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Store
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_memory_store(NCMemoryStore *mem, const char *content,
                     NCMemoryType type, float relevance) {
    if (!mem || !content) return;
    if (relevance < 0.0f) relevance = 0.0f;
    if (relevance > 1.0f) relevance = 1.0f;

    /* Check for duplicates — if same content exists, boost it */
    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
        if (mem->entries[i].content &&
            strcmp(mem->entries[i].content, content) == 0) {
            /* Boost existing entry */
            mem->entries[i].access_count++;
            mem->entries[i].recency = 1.0f;  /* refresh recency */
            if (relevance > mem->entries[i].relevance)
                mem->entries[i].relevance = relevance;
            return;
        }
    }

    /* If at capacity, evict lowest-scoring entry */
    if (mem->n_entries >= mem->capacity) {
        int worst = 0;
        float worst_score = 1e9f;
        for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
            float score = mem->entries[i].relevance * 0.4f +
                          mem->entries[i].recency * 0.3f +
                          (float)mem->entries[i].access_count * 0.01f;
            if (score < worst_score) {
                worst_score = score;
                worst = i;
            }
        }
        free(mem->entries[worst].content);
        mem->entries[worst].content = NULL;
        /* Shift down */
        if (worst < mem->n_entries - 1) {
            memmove(&mem->entries[worst], &mem->entries[worst + 1],
                    (size_t)(mem->n_entries - worst - 1) * sizeof(NCMemoryEntry));
        }
        mem->n_entries--;
    }

    /* Add new entry */
    int idx = mem->n_entries;
    mem->entries[idx].content      = ncm_strdup(content);
    mem->entries[idx].relevance    = relevance;
    mem->entries[idx].recency      = 1.0f;
    mem->entries[idx].access_count = 1;
    mem->entries[idx].type         = type;
    mem->n_entries++;

    /* Add key index */
    if (mem->n_keys < NCM_KEY_CAP) {
        char *key = ncm_extract_key(content);
        if (key) {
            mem->keys[mem->n_keys]    = key;
            mem->key_map[mem->n_keys] = idx;
            mem->n_keys++;
        }
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Recall — search by similarity with type filter
 *
 *  Returns array of pointers to matching entries (caller must
 *  free the array, but NOT the entries themselves).
 *  Sets n_results to the number of results found.
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* Internal: scored result for sorting */
typedef struct {
    NCMemoryEntry *entry;
    float          score;
} NCMemoryMatch;

static int ncm_match_cmp(const void *a, const void *b) {
    float sa = ((const NCMemoryMatch *)a)->score;
    float sb = ((const NCMemoryMatch *)b)->score;
    if (sb > sa) return 1;
    if (sb < sa) return -1;
    return 0;
}

NCMemoryEntry **nc_memory_recall(NCMemoryStore *mem, const char *query,
                                 NCMemoryType type, int max_results) {
    if (!mem || !query) return NULL;
    if (max_results <= 0) max_results = NCM_MAX_RESULTS;
    if (max_results > NCM_MAX_RESULTS) max_results = NCM_MAX_RESULTS;

    /* Score all entries of matching type */
    NCMemoryMatch *matches = (NCMemoryMatch *)calloc(
        (size_t)mem->n_entries, sizeof(NCMemoryMatch));
    if (!matches) return NULL;

    int n_matches = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
        if (!mem->entries[i].content) continue;

        /* Type filter: -1 means any type */
        if ((int)type >= 0 && mem->entries[i].type != type) continue;

        float text_score = ncm_fuzzy_score(query, mem->entries[i].content);

        /* Also check key index for faster matching */
        float key_score = 0.0f;
        for (int k = 0; k < mem->n_keys; k++) {
            if (mem->key_map[k] == i && mem->keys[k]) {
                float ks = ncm_fuzzy_score(query, mem->keys[k]);
                if (ks > key_score) key_score = ks;
            }
        }

        float combined = text_score > key_score ? text_score : key_score;

        /* Weight by relevance, recency, and access count */
        combined = combined * 0.5f +
                   mem->entries[i].relevance * 0.2f +
                   mem->entries[i].recency * 0.2f +
                   fminf((float)mem->entries[i].access_count * 0.02f, 0.1f);

        if (combined > 0.1f) {
            matches[n_matches].entry = &mem->entries[i];
            matches[n_matches].score = combined;
            n_matches++;
        }
    }

    if (n_matches == 0) {
        free(matches);
        return NULL;
    }

    /* Sort by score descending */
    qsort(matches, (size_t)n_matches, sizeof(NCMemoryMatch), ncm_match_cmp);

    /* Cap results */
    if (n_matches > max_results) n_matches = max_results;

    /* Build result array */
    NCMemoryEntry **results = (NCMemoryEntry **)calloc(
        (size_t)(n_matches + 1), sizeof(NCMemoryEntry *));
    if (!results) {
        free(matches);
        return NULL;
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < n_matches; i++) {
        results[i] = matches[i].entry;
        /* Boost access count for recalled entries */
        matches[i].entry->access_count++;
        matches[i].entry->recency = 1.0f;  /* refresh recency */
    }
    results[n_matches] = NULL;  /* sentinel */

    free(matches);
    return results;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Consolidation — memory consolidation (like human sleep)
 *
 *  Promotes high-access working memory entries to semantic or
 *  procedural memory. If the same pattern appears 3+ times
 *  across working/episodic memory, it gets promoted to
 *  procedural memory as a "learned strategy".
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_memory_consolidate(NCMemoryStore *mem) {
    if (!mem) return;

    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
        if (!mem->entries[i].content) continue;

        /* Promote working memory with high access to episodic */
        if (mem->entries[i].type == NC_MEM_WORKING &&
            mem->entries[i].access_count >= NCM_CONSOLIDATE_THRESH &&
            mem->entries[i].relevance >= NCM_CONSOLIDATE_REL) {
            mem->entries[i].type = NC_MEM_EPISODIC;
        }

        /* Promote episodic with high access to semantic */
        if (mem->entries[i].type == NC_MEM_EPISODIC &&
            mem->entries[i].access_count >= NCM_CONSOLIDATE_THRESH * 2 &&
            mem->entries[i].relevance >= NCM_CONSOLIDATE_REL) {
            mem->entries[i].type = NC_MEM_SEMANTIC;
        }

        /* Check if similar patterns exist 3+ times -> promote to procedural */
        if (mem->entries[i].type == NC_MEM_EPISODIC ||
            mem->entries[i].type == NC_MEM_SEMANTIC) {
            int similar_count = 0;
            for (int j = 0; j < mem->n_entries; j++) {
                if (i == j || !mem->entries[j].content) continue;
                float sim = ncm_fuzzy_score(mem->entries[i].content,
                                            mem->entries[j].content);
                if (sim > 0.7f) similar_count++;
            }
            if (similar_count >= NCM_CONSOLIDATE_THRESH) {
                mem->entries[i].type = NC_MEM_PROCEDURAL;
                mem->entries[i].relevance = 0.9f;  /* high relevance */
            }
        }
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Forgetting — graceful removal of low-value entries
 *
 *  Removes entries where both relevance and recency are below
 *  threshold, unless they have high access counts (indicating
 *  they are important despite being old).
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_memory_forget(NCMemoryStore *mem) {
    if (!mem) return;

    /* First: decay recency for all entries */
    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
        mem->entries[i].recency *= (1.0f - NCM_DECAY_RATE);
    }

    /* Then: remove entries below threshold */
    int write_idx = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
        float combined = mem->entries[i].relevance * 0.4f +
                         mem->entries[i].recency * 0.3f +
                         fminf((float)mem->entries[i].access_count * 0.02f, 0.3f);

        /* Never forget procedural or reinforcement memory easily */
        if (mem->entries[i].type == NC_MEM_PROCEDURAL ||
            mem->entries[i].type == NC_MEM_REINFORCEMENT) {
            combined += 0.3f;
        }

        /* Never forget high-access entries */
        if (mem->entries[i].access_count >= 10) {
            combined += 0.2f;
        }

        if (combined < NCM_FORGET_THRESHOLD) {
            /* Forget this entry */
            free(mem->entries[i].content);
            mem->entries[i].content = NULL;
        } else {
            if (write_idx != i) {
                mem->entries[write_idx] = mem->entries[i];
                mem->entries[i].content = NULL;
            }
            write_idx++;
        }
    }
    mem->n_entries = write_idx;

    /* Rebuild key index */
    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_keys; i++) {
        free(mem->keys[i]);
        mem->keys[i] = NULL;
    }
    mem->n_keys = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries && mem->n_keys < NCM_KEY_CAP; i++) {
        if (mem->entries[i].content) {
            char *key = ncm_extract_key(mem->entries[i].content);
            if (key) {
                mem->keys[mem->n_keys]    = key;
                mem->key_map[mem->n_keys] = i;
                mem->n_keys++;
            }
        }
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Persistence — binary save/load
 *
 *  Format:
 *    [magic:4][version:4]
 *    [n_entries:4][capacity:4]
 *    for each entry:
 *      [content_len:4][content]
 *      [relevance:4][recency:4][access_count:4][type:4]
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int ncm_write_str(FILE *f, const char *s) {
    if (!s) {
        int z = 0;
        return (int)fwrite(&z, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    }
    int len = (int)strlen(s);
    if (fwrite(&len, sizeof(int), 1, f) != 1) return 0;
    if (len > 0 && fwrite(s, 1, (size_t)len, f) != (size_t)len) return 0;
    return 1;
}

static char *ncm_read_str(FILE *f) {
    int len = 0;
    if (fread(&len, sizeof(int), 1, f) != 1) return NULL;
    if (len <= 0) return NULL;
    if (len > 10000000) return NULL;  /* 10MB sanity check */
    char *s = (char *)malloc((size_t)len + 1);
    if (!s) return NULL;
    if (fread(s, 1, (size_t)len, f) != (size_t)len) {
        free(s);
        return NULL;
    }
    s[len] = '\0';
    return s;
}

int nc_memory_save(NCMemoryStore *mem, const char *path) {
    if (!mem || !path) return 0;

    FILE *f = fopen(path, "wb");
    if (!f) return 0;

    unsigned int magic = NCM_MAGIC;
    int version = NCM_VERSION;
    fwrite(&magic,   sizeof(unsigned int), 1, f);
    fwrite(&version, sizeof(int), 1, f);

    fwrite(&mem->n_entries, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    fwrite(&mem->capacity,  sizeof(int), 1, f);

    for (int i = 0; i < mem->n_entries; i++) {
        ncm_write_str(f, mem->entries[i].content);
        fwrite(&mem->entries[i].relevance,    sizeof(float), 1, f);
        fwrite(&mem->entries[i].recency,      sizeof(float), 1, f);
        fwrite(&mem->entries[i].access_count, sizeof(int),   1, f);
        int type_int = (int)mem->entries[i].type;
        fwrite(&type_int, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    }

    fclose(f);
    return 1;
}

NCMemoryStore *nc_memory_load(const char *path) {
    if (!path) return NULL;

    FILE *f = fopen(path, "rb");
    if (!f) return NULL;

    unsigned int magic = 0;
    int version = 0;
    if (fread(&magic, sizeof(unsigned int), 1, f) != 1 ||
        magic != NCM_MAGIC) {
        fclose(f);
        return NULL;
    }
    if (fread(&version, sizeof(int), 1, f) != 1 ||
        version != NCM_VERSION) {
        fclose(f);
        return NULL;
    }

    int n_entries = 0, capacity = 0;
    fread(&n_entries, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    fread(&capacity,  sizeof(int), 1, f);

    if (capacity <= 0) capacity = NCM_DEFAULT_CAP;
    NCMemoryStore *mem = nc_memory_create(capacity);
    if (!mem) {
        fclose(f);
        return NULL;
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < n_entries; i++) {
        char *content = ncm_read_str(f);
        float relevance = 0.0f, recency = 0.0f;
        int access_count = 0, type_int = 0;

        fread(&relevance,    sizeof(float), 1, f);
        fread(&recency,      sizeof(float), 1, f);
        fread(&access_count, sizeof(int),   1, f);
        fread(&type_int,     sizeof(int),   1, f);

        if (content) {
            /* Use nc_memory_store for proper indexing */
            nc_memory_store(mem, content, (NCMemoryType)type_int, relevance);

            /* Restore recency and access_count (store sets them to 1.0/1) */
            int idx = mem->n_entries - 1;
            if (idx >= 0) {
                mem->entries[idx].recency      = recency;
                mem->entries[idx].access_count = access_count;
            }
            free(content);
        }
    }

    fclose(f);
    return mem;
}


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_memory.h

/*
 * nc_ai_memory.h — Multi-Layer Cognitive Memory for NC AI.
 *
 * A 5-layer memory architecture inspired by cognitive science:
 *   1. Working      — current task context (local to each ant)
 *   2. Episodic     — past problem-solution pairs with rewards
 *   3. Semantic     — learned concepts (code patterns, rules)
 *   4. Procedural   — how-to knowledge (generation strategies)
 *   5. Reinforcement — Q-table state-action-reward values
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 */

#ifndef NC_AI_MEMORY_H
#define NC_AI_MEMORY_H

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <time.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  NC AI Memory System — Multi-Layer Cognitive Architecture
 *
 *  5 memory layers (inspired by HiveANT):
 *  1. Working       — Active processing — current task
 *  2. Episodic      — Experiences — past solutions
 *  3. Semantic      — Concepts — learned patterns
 *  4. Procedural    — Strategies — how to generate
 *  5. Reinforcement — Q-table — reward-based decisions
 *
 *  By DevHeal Labs AI
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

#define NC_MEM_MAX_TAGS       8
#define NC_MEM_MAX_RESULTS    64
#define NC_MEM_DEFAULT_CAP    512

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Core types
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef enum {
    NC_MEM_WORKING,         /* Active processing — current task  */
    NC_MEM_EPISODIC,        /* Experiences — past solutions      */
    NC_MEM_SEMANTIC,        /* Concepts — learned patterns       */
    NC_MEM_PROCEDURAL,      /* Strategies — how to generate      */
    NC_MEM_REINFORCEMENT,   /* Q-table — reward-based decisions  */
} NCMemoryType;

typedef struct {
    char *content;
    float relevance;    /* 0.0 to 1.0                            */
    float recency;      /* Decays over time                      */
    int access_count;
    NCMemoryType type;
} NCMemoryEntry;

typedef struct {
    NCMemoryEntry *entries;
    int n_entries;
    int capacity;
    /* Indexes for fast lookup */
    char **keys;
    int *key_map;       /* key index -> entry index               */
    int n_keys;
} NCMemoryStore;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Lifecycle
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCMemoryStore *nc_memory_create(int capacity);
void nc_memory_free(NCMemoryStore *mem);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Store
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_memory_store(NCMemoryStore *mem, const char *content,
                     NCMemoryType type, float relevance);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Recall — search by similarity
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCMemoryEntry **nc_memory_recall(NCMemoryStore *mem, const char *query,
                                 NCMemoryType type, int max_results);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Consolidation and decay
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* Move high-access working memory to semantic/procedural */
void nc_memory_consolidate(NCMemoryStore *mem);

/* Remove low-relevance, low-recency entries (graceful forgetting) */
void nc_memory_forget(NCMemoryStore *mem);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Persistence
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_memory_save(NCMemoryStore *mem, const char *path);
NCMemoryStore *nc_memory_load(const char *path);

#endif /* NC_AI_MEMORY_H */


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_security.c

/*
 * nc_ai_security.c — Enterprise-grade security for NC AI code generation.
 *
 * Full implementation of OWASP Top 10 vulnerability scanning,
 * secure code template generation, and compliance checking.
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 * By DevHeal Labs AI
 */

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>

#include "nc_ai_security.h"

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Internal helpers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *nc_strdup(const char *s) {
    if (!s) return NULL;
    size_t len = strlen(s);
    char *dup = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
    if (dup) memcpy(dup, s, len + 1);
    return dup;
}

static NCSecurityReport *nc_security_report_create(void) {
    NCSecurityReport *report = (NCSecurityReport *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCSecurityReport));
    if (!report) return NULL;
    report->capacity = 64;
    report->issues = (NCSecurityIssue *)calloc((size_t)report->capacity, sizeof(NCSecurityIssue));
    if (!report->issues) {
        free(report);
        return NULL;
    }
    report->security_score = 100.0f;
    return report;
}

static void nc_security_add_issue(NCSecurityReport *report,
                                  const char *vulnerability,
                                  const char *severity,
                                  int line,
                                  const char *description,
                                  const char *recommendation) {
    if (!report) return;
    if (report->n_issues >= report->capacity) {
        int new_cap = report->capacity * 2;
        NCSecurityIssue *tmp = (NCSecurityIssue *)realloc(
            report->issues, (size_t)new_cap * sizeof(NCSecurityIssue));
        if (!tmp) return;
        report->issues = tmp;
        report->capacity = new_cap;
    }

    NCSecurityIssue *issue = &report->issues[report->n_issues];
    issue->vulnerability = nc_strdup(vulnerability);
    issue->severity      = nc_strdup(severity);
    issue->line          = line;
    issue->description   = nc_strdup(description);
    issue->recommendation = nc_strdup(recommendation);
    report->n_issues++;

    /* Update severity counters and score */
    if (strcmp(severity, "CRITICAL") == 0) {
        report->critical_count++;
        report->security_score -= 25.0f;
    } else if (strcmp(severity, "HIGH") == 0) {
        report->high_count++;
        report->security_score -= 15.0f;
    } else if (strcmp(severity, "MEDIUM") == 0) {
        report->medium_count++;
        report->security_score -= 8.0f;
    } else if (strcmp(severity, "LOW") == 0) {
        report->low_count++;
        report->security_score -= 3.0f;
    }
    if (report->security_score < 0.0f) report->security_score = 0.0f;
}

/* Count how many lines come before a given position in code */
static int nc_line_at(const char *code, const char *pos) {
    int line = 1;
    for (const char *p = code; p < pos; p++) {
        if (*p == '\n') line++;
    }
    return line;
}

/* Case-insensitive substring search */
static const char *nc_strcasestr(const char *haystack, const char *needle) {
    if (!haystack || !needle) return NULL;
    size_t nlen = strlen(needle);
    if (nlen == 0) return haystack;
    for (const char *p = haystack; *p; p++) {
        int match = 1;
        for (size_t i = 0; i < nlen; i++) {
            if (tolower((unsigned char)p[i]) != tolower((unsigned char)needle[i])) {
                match = 0;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (match) return p;
    }
    return NULL;
}

/* Check if a line contains a specific keyword (case-insensitive) */
static int nc_line_contains(const char *line_start, const char *line_end, const char *keyword) {
    size_t klen = strlen(keyword);
    for (const char *p = line_start; p + klen <= line_end; p++) {
        int match = 1;
        for (size_t i = 0; i < klen; i++) {
            if (tolower((unsigned char)p[i]) != tolower((unsigned char)keyword[i])) {
                match = 0;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (match) return 1;
    }
    return 0;
}

/* Get start and end of line containing pos */
static void nc_get_line_bounds(const char *code, const char *pos,
                               const char **start, const char **end) {
    *start = pos;
    while (*start > code && (*start)[-1] != '\n') (*start)--;
    *end = pos;
    while (**end && **end != '\n') (*end)++;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  OWASP Check 1: Injection (SQL, Command, Code)
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_security_check_injection(const char *code, NCSecurityReport *report) {
    if (!code || !report) return 0;
    int found = 0;

    /* Pattern: ask AI user_input — unsanitized AI prompt injection */
    const char *p = code;
    while ((p = nc_strcasestr(p, "ask AI")) != NULL) {
        const char *line_start, *line_end;
        nc_get_line_bounds(code, p, &line_start, &line_end);
        if (nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "user_input") ||
            nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "user_data") ||
            nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "request.body")) {
            if (!nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "sanitize") &&
                !nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "validate") &&
                !nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "escape")) {
                nc_security_add_issue(report,
                    "Prompt Injection", "CRITICAL", nc_line_at(code, p),
                    "User input passed directly to AI without sanitization",
                    "Use nc_sanitize_input() before passing to AI queries");
                found++;
            }
        }
        p++;
    }

    /* Pattern: load(user_input) — path traversal / injection */
    p = code;
    while ((p = nc_strcasestr(p, "load")) != NULL) {
        const char *line_start, *line_end;
        nc_get_line_bounds(code, p, &line_start, &line_end);
        if (nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "user_input") ||
            nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "request.path") ||
            nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "request.param")) {
            if (!nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "validate") &&
                !nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "whitelist")) {
                nc_security_add_issue(report,
                    "Path Injection", "HIGH", nc_line_at(code, p),
                    "User-controlled path in load operation — path traversal risk",
                    "Validate and whitelist file paths before loading");
                found++;
            }
        }
        p++;
    }

    /* Pattern: save to user_input — arbitrary file write */
    p = code;
    while ((p = nc_strcasestr(p, "save to")) != NULL) {
        const char *line_start, *line_end;
        nc_get_line_bounds(code, p, &line_start, &line_end);
        if (nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "user_input") ||
            nc_line_contains(line_start, line_end, "request.param")) {
            nc_security_add_issue(report,
                "File Write Injection", "CRITICAL", nc_line_at(code, p),
                "User-controlled path in save operation — arbitrary file write",
