/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Pheromone Trail Implementation
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCPheromoneTrail *nc_pheromone_create(int capacity) {
    NCPheromoneTrail *trail = (NCPheromoneTrail *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCPheromoneTrail));
    if (!trail) return NULL;

    if (capacity <= 0) capacity = NC_COL_PHEROMONE_CAP;
    trail->trails = (NCPheromone *)calloc((size_t)capacity, sizeof(NCPheromone));
    if (!trail->trails) {
        free(trail);
        return NULL;
    }
    trail->capacity        = capacity;
    trail->n_trails        = 0;
    trail->evaporation_rate = NC_COL_EVAPORATION_RATE;
    trail->min_strength     = NC_COL_MIN_STRENGTH;
    return trail;
}

void nc_pheromone_deposit(NCPheromoneTrail *trail, const char *key,
                          const char *value, float strength) {
    if (!trail || !key || !value) return;
    if (strength < 0.0f) strength = 0.0f;
    if (strength > 1.0f) strength = 1.0f;

    /* Check if key already exists — strengthen and update */
    for (int i = 0; i < trail->n_trails; i++) {
        if (trail->trails[i].key && strcmp(trail->trails[i].key, key) == 0) {
            trail->trails[i].strength += strength * 0.3f;
            if (trail->trails[i].strength > 1.0f)
                trail->trails[i].strength = 1.0f;
            trail->trails[i].uses++;
            trail->trails[i].timestamp = (float)time(NULL);
            free(trail->trails[i].value);
            trail->trails[i].value = nc_strdup(value);
            return;
        }
    }

    /* New entry — evict weakest if at capacity */
    if (trail->n_trails >= trail->capacity) {
        int weakest = 0;
        float weakest_str = trail->trails[0].strength;
        for (int i = 1; i < trail->n_trails; i++) {
            if (trail->trails[i].strength < weakest_str) {
                weakest_str = trail->trails[i].strength;
                weakest = i;
            }
        }
        free(trail->trails[weakest].key);
        free(trail->trails[weakest].value);
        trail->trails[weakest].key       = nc_strdup(key);
        trail->trails[weakest].value     = nc_strdup(value);
        trail->trails[weakest].strength  = strength;
        trail->trails[weakest].uses      = 1;
        trail->trails[weakest].successes = 0;
        trail->trails[weakest].timestamp = (float)time(NULL);
        return;
    }

    int idx = trail->n_trails++;
    trail->trails[idx].key       = nc_strdup(key);
    trail->trails[idx].value     = nc_strdup(value);
    trail->trails[idx].strength  = strength;
    trail->trails[idx].uses      = 1;
    trail->trails[idx].successes = 0;
    trail->trails[idx].timestamp = (float)time(NULL);
}

const char *nc_pheromone_lookup(NCPheromoneTrail *trail, const char *key) {
    if (!trail || !key) return NULL;

    /* Exact match first */
    for (int i = 0; i < trail->n_trails; i++) {
        if (trail->trails[i].key && strcmp(trail->trails[i].key, key) == 0) {
            trail->trails[i].uses++;
            return trail->trails[i].value;
        }
    }

    /* Fuzzy match — find best */
    float best_score = 0.0f;
    int   best_idx   = -1;
    for (int i = 0; i < trail->n_trails; i++) {
        if (!trail->trails[i].key) continue;
        float score = nc_fuzzy_match(key, trail->trails[i].key);
        score *= trail->trails[i].strength;   /* weight by pheromone strength */
        if (score > best_score) {
            best_score = score;
            best_idx   = i;
        }
    }

    if (best_idx >= 0 && best_score > 0.3f) {
        trail->trails[best_idx].uses++;
        return trail->trails[best_idx].value;
    }
    return NULL;
}

void nc_pheromone_evaporate(NCPheromoneTrail *trail) {
    if (!trail) return;

    int write_idx = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < trail->n_trails; i++) {
        trail->trails[i].strength *= (1.0f - trail->evaporation_rate);

        if (trail->trails[i].strength < trail->min_strength) {
            /* Remove this entry */
            free(trail->trails[i].key);
            free(trail->trails[i].value);
            trail->trails[i].key   = NULL;
            trail->trails[i].value = NULL;
        } else {
            if (write_idx != i) {
                trail->trails[write_idx] = trail->trails[i];
                trail->trails[i].key     = NULL;
                trail->trails[i].value   = NULL;
            }
            write_idx++;
        }
    }
    trail->n_trails = write_idx;
}

void nc_pheromone_free(NCPheromoneTrail *trail) {
    if (!trail) return;
    for (int i = 0; i < trail->n_trails; i++) {
        free(trail->trails[i].key);
        free(trail->trails[i].value);
    }
    free(trail->trails);
    free(trail);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Ant Operations — init / free / local memory
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static void nc_ant_init(NCAnt *ant, int id, NCAntType type) {
    memset(ant, 0, sizeof(NCAnt));
    ant->id              = id;
    ant->type            = type;
    ant->fitness         = 0.0f;
    ant->generation      = 0;
    ant->memory_capacity = NC_COL_ANT_MEMORY_CAP;
    ant->local_memory    = (char **)calloc((size_t)ant->memory_capacity, sizeof(char *));
    ant->memory_size     = 0;
    ant->current_task    = NULL;
}

static void nc_ant_free(NCAnt *ant) {
    if (!ant) return;
    free(ant->current_task);
    ant->current_task = NULL;
    for (int i = 0; i < ant->memory_size; i++)
        free(ant->local_memory[i]);
    free(ant->local_memory);
    ant->local_memory = NULL;
    ant->memory_size  = 0;
}

static void nc_ant_remember(NCAnt *ant, const char *info) {
    if (!ant || !info || !ant->local_memory) return;
    if (ant->memory_size >= ant->memory_capacity) {
        free(ant->local_memory[0]);
        memmove(ant->local_memory, ant->local_memory + 1,
                (size_t)(ant->memory_size - 1) * sizeof(char *));
        ant->memory_size--;
    }
    ant->local_memory[ant->memory_size++] = nc_strdup(info);
}

static void nc_ant_clear_memory(NCAnt *ant) {
    if (!ant) return;
    for (int i = 0; i < ant->memory_size; i++) {
        free(ant->local_memory[i]);
        ant->local_memory[i] = NULL;
    }
    ant->memory_size = 0;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Scout Ant — analyzes problem, extracts features
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    char *type_str;         /* "service", "ui", "crud", etc.       */
    int   q_state;          /* Q-table state index                 */
    char *name;             /* extracted name                      */
    char *features[16];     /* extracted feature keywords           */
    int   n_features;
} NCScoutResult;

static void nc_scout_result_free(NCScoutResult *r) {
    if (!r) return;
    free(r->type_str);
    free(r->name);
    for (int i = 0; i < r->n_features; i++) free(r->features[i]);
    memset(r, 0, sizeof(NCScoutResult));
}

static NCScoutResult nc_ant_scout_analyze(NCAnt *ant, const char *problem) {
    NCScoutResult result;
    memset(&result, 0, sizeof(result));

    char lower[2048];
    nc_str_lower(lower, problem, sizeof(lower));

    /* ── Detect problem type ──────────────────────────── */
    if (strstr(lower, "crud") ||
        (strstr(lower, "create") && strstr(lower, "delete"))) {
        result.type_str = nc_strdup("crud");
        result.q_state  = NC_Q_STATE_CRUD;
    } else if (strstr(lower, "full app") || strstr(lower, "full application") ||
               (strstr(lower, "service") && strstr(lower, "ui"))) {
        result.type_str = nc_strdup("full_app");
        result.q_state  = NC_Q_STATE_FULL_APP;
    } else if (strstr(lower, "ui") || strstr(lower, "page") ||
               strstr(lower, "frontend") || strstr(lower, "dashboard") ||
               strstr(lower, "ncui")) {
        result.type_str = nc_strdup("ui");
        result.q_state  = NC_Q_STATE_UI;
    } else if (strstr(lower, "ai") || strstr(lower, "model") ||
               strstr(lower, "predict") || strstr(lower, "ml") ||
               strstr(lower, "intelligence")) {
        result.type_str = nc_strdup("ai");
        result.q_state  = NC_Q_STATE_AI;
    } else if (strstr(lower, "test") || strstr(lower, "spec") ||
               strstr(lower, "assert")) {
        result.type_str = nc_strdup("test");
        result.q_state  = NC_Q_STATE_TEST;
    } else if (strstr(lower, "middleware") || strstr(lower, "auth") ||
               strstr(lower, "filter")) {
        result.type_str = nc_strdup("middleware");
        result.q_state  = NC_Q_STATE_MIDDLEWARE;
    } else {
        result.type_str = nc_strdup("service");
        result.q_state  = NC_Q_STATE_SERVICE;
    }

    /* ── Extract name (quoted, or after "called"/"named"/"for") ── */
    const char *q1 = strchr(problem, '"');
    if (q1) {
        const char *q2 = strchr(q1 + 1, '"');
        if (q2 && q2 > q1 + 1) {
            size_t nlen = (size_t)(q2 - q1 - 1);
            result.name = (char *)malloc(nlen + 1);
            if (result.name) {
                memcpy(result.name, q1 + 1, nlen);
                result.name[nlen] = '\0';
            }
        }
    }
    if (!result.name) {
        const char *markers[] = {"called ", "named ", "for ", NULL};
        for (int m = 0; markers[m]; m++) {
            const char *found = strstr(lower, markers[m]);
            if (found) {
                found += strlen(markers[m]);
                char word[128];
                int wi = 0;
                while (*found && !isspace((unsigned char)*found) && wi < 126)
                    word[wi++] = *found++;
                word[wi] = '\0';
                if (wi > 0) {
                    word[0] = (char)toupper((unsigned char)word[0]);
                    result.name = nc_strdup(word);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if (!result.name) result.name = nc_strdup("Generated");

    /* ── Extract feature keywords ─────────────────────── */
    static const char *feature_words[] = {
        "auth", "login", "jwt", "token", "user", "password",
        "crud", "list", "create", "update", "delete", "read",
        "dark", "light", "theme", "style", "color",
        "api", "rest", "http", "websocket", "realtime",
        "database", "store", "cache", "redis", "sql",
        "upload", "file", "image", "video", "media",
        "search", "filter", "sort", "paginate", "pagination",
        "notify", "email", "sms", "push", "notification",
        "chat", "message", "conversation",
        "dashboard", "chart", "graph", "analytics",
        "payment", "stripe", "billing",
        NULL
    };
    for (int i = 0; feature_words[i] && result.n_features < 16; i++) {
        if (strstr(lower, feature_words[i]))
            result.features[result.n_features++] = nc_strdup(feature_words[i]);
    }

    nc_ant_remember(ant, result.type_str);
    nc_ant_remember(ant, result.name);
    ant->fitness = 0.5f + 0.1f * (float)result.n_features;
    if (ant->fitness > 1.0f) ant->fitness = 1.0f;

    return result;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Worker Ant — generates NC code sections
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int nc_has_feature(const NCScoutResult *s, const char *feat) {
    for (int i = 0; i < s->n_features; i++)
        if (strcmp(s->features[i], feat) == 0) return 1;
    return 0;
}

/* Generate a service / CRUD service */
static void nc_gen_service(NCBuf *buf, const NCScoutResult *s, int is_crud) {
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "service %s on port 3000:\n\n", s->name);

    if (nc_has_feature(s, "auth") || nc_has_feature(s, "jwt") ||
        nc_has_feature(s, "login")) {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "    load JWTAuth\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "    apply JWTAuth\n\n");
    }

    if (is_crud) {
        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    set items to []\n\n");

        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior list_%s:\n", s->name);
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with items\n\n");

        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior create_%s:\n", s->name);
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set new_item to request.body\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        remember new_item in items\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with new_item\n\n");

        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior get_%s:\n", s->name);
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set id to request.params.id\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set item to recall from items where id matches\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with item\n\n");

        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior update_%s:\n", s->name);
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set id to request.params.id\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set updates to request.body\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set item to recall from items where id matches\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        update item with updates\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with item\n\n");

        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior delete_%s:\n", s->name);
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set id to request.params.id\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        forget from items where id matches\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with \"deleted\"\n\n");
    } else {
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "    behavior handle_request:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set data to request.body\n");
        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        show \"Processing %s request\"\n", s->name);
        nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with data\n\n");

        if (nc_has_feature(s, "search")) {
            nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior search_%s:\n", s->name);
            nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set query to request.params.q\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set results to recall from items where name contains query\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with results\n\n");
        }
        if (nc_has_feature(s, "notify") || nc_has_feature(s, "notification")) {
            nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior send_notification:\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        set message to request.body.message\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        set target to request.body.target\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        connect to notification_service\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with \"notification sent\"\n\n");
        }
        if (nc_has_feature(s, "upload") || nc_has_feature(s, "file")) {
            nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior upload_%s:\n", s->name);
            nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set file to request.body.file\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf,  "        remember file in uploads\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with file.id\n\n");
        }
        if (nc_has_feature(s, "chat") || nc_has_feature(s, "message")) {
            nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior send_message:\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        set msg to request.body\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        remember msg in messages\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with msg\n\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior get_messages:\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with messages\n\n");
        }
        if (nc_has_feature(s, "payment") || nc_has_feature(s, "stripe") ||
            nc_has_feature(s, "billing")) {
            nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior process_payment:\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        set amount to request.body.amount\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        set token to request.body.token\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        connect to payment_provider\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        set result to charge payment_provider with amount token\n");
            nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with result\n\n");
        }
    }
}

/* Generate a UI page */
static void nc_gen_ui(NCBuf *buf, const NCScoutResult *s) {
    int dark = nc_has_feature(s, "dark");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "page %s:\n\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf, "    box layout=\"column\" align=\"center\":\n\n");
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        text \"%s\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf, "            style: fontSize 24, fontWeight \"bold\"\n\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        box layout=\"column\" padding=20:\n");

    if (nc_has_feature(s, "dashboard") || nc_has_feature(s, "chart") ||
        nc_has_feature(s, "analytics")) {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "\n            box layout=\"row\" gap=16:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                box class=\"card\":\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text \"Total Users\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text \"1,234\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                        style: fontSize 32, fontWeight \"bold\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                box class=\"card\":\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text \"Active Today\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text \"567\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                        style: fontSize 32, fontWeight \"bold\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                box class=\"card\":\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text \"Revenue\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text \"$12,345\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                        style: fontSize 32, fontWeight \"bold\"\n\n");
    }

    if (nc_has_feature(s, "search") || nc_has_feature(s, "filter")) {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "\n            box layout=\"row\" gap=8:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                input placeholder=\"Search...\" bind=searchQuery\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                button \"Search\" on_click=handleSearch\n\n");
    }

    if (nc_has_feature(s, "list") || nc_has_feature(s, "crud")) {
        nc_buf_appendf(buf, "\n            repeat item in %s_list:\n", s->name);
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                box class=\"list-item\" layout=\"row\":\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text item.name\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    button \"Edit\" on_click=handleEdit\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    button \"Delete\" on_click=handleDelete\n\n");
    }

    if (nc_has_feature(s, "chat") || nc_has_feature(s, "message")) {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "\n            box class=\"chat-container\" layout=\"column\":\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                box class=\"messages\" scroll=true:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    repeat msg in messages:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                        box class=\"message\":\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                            text msg.sender\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                                style: fontWeight \"bold\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                            text msg.content\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                box layout=\"row\" gap=8:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    input placeholder=\"Type a message...\" bind=newMessage\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                    button \"Send\" on_click=handleSend\n\n");
    }

    nc_buf_append(buf, "\n            input placeholder=\"Enter data...\" bind=inputValue\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "            button \"Submit\" on_click=handleSubmit\n\n");

    /* Style block */
    nc_buf_append(buf, "    style:\n");
    if (dark) {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        background #0a0a0f\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        color #e0e0e0\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        accent #6c63ff\n");
    } else {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        background #ffffff\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        color #333333\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        accent #4a90d9\n");
    }
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        fontFamily \"Inter, sans-serif\"\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        padding 20\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        borderRadius 8\n\n");
}

/* Generate full app (backend + frontend) */
static void nc_gen_full_app(NCBuf *buf, const NCScoutResult *s) {
    nc_buf_append(buf, "// === Backend Service ===\n\n");
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "service %sAPI on port 3000:\n\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf, "    set items to []\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior list_%s:\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with items\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior create_%s:\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set new_item to request.body\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        remember new_item in items\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with new_item\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior get_%s:\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set id to request.params.id\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set item to recall from items where id matches\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with item\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior update_%s:\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set id to request.params.id\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set updates to request.body\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set item to recall from items where id matches\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        update item with updates\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with item\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    behavior delete_%s:\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        set id to request.params.id\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        forget from items where id matches\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        respond with \"deleted\"\n\n");

    nc_buf_append(buf, "\n// === Frontend Page ===\n\n");
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "page %sPage:\n\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf, "    box layout=\"column\" align=\"center\":\n\n");
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        text \"%s\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf, "            style: fontSize 24, fontWeight \"bold\"\n\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        box layout=\"column\" padding=20:\n");
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "            repeat item in %s_list:\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf, "                box class=\"card\" layout=\"row\":\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "                    text item.name\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "                    box layout=\"row\" gap=4:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "                        button \"Edit\" on_click=handleEdit\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "                        button \"Delete\" on_click=handleDelete\n\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        box layout=\"row\" gap=8:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "            input placeholder=\"Add new...\" bind=newItem\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "            button \"Add\" on_click=handleAdd\n\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "    style:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        background #0a0a0f\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        color #e0e0e0\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        accent #6c63ff\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        fontFamily \"Inter, sans-serif\"\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        padding 20\n\n");
}

/* Generate test file */
static void nc_gen_test(NCBuf *buf, const NCScoutResult *s) {
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "test \"%s tests\":\n\n", s->name);

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    test \"should create %s\":\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set result to create_%s with name \"test_item\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        expect result to_be defined\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        expect result.name to_be \"test_item\"\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    test \"should list %s\":\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        create_%s with name \"item_1\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        create_%s with name \"item_2\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set items to list_%s\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        expect items.length to_be 2\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    test \"should get %s by id\":\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set created to create_%s with name \"findme\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set found to get_%s with id created.id\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        expect found.name to_be \"findme\"\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    test \"should update %s\":\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set created to create_%s with name \"old_name\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set updated to update_%s with id created.id name \"new_name\"\n",
                   s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        expect updated.name to_be \"new_name\"\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    test \"should delete %s\":\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set created to create_%s with name \"remove_me\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        delete_%s with id created.id\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set result to get_%s with id created.id\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        expect result to_be null\n\n");

    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "    test \"should handle invalid input\":\n");
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "        set result to create_%s with name \"\"\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf,  "        expect result.error to_be defined\n\n");
}

/* Generate middleware */
static void nc_gen_middleware(NCBuf *buf, const NCScoutResult *s) {
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "middleware %s:\n\n", s->name);

    nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior before_request:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set start_time to now\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        show \"[\" + request.method + \"] \" + request.path\n\n");

    if (nc_has_feature(s, "auth") || nc_has_feature(s, "jwt") ||
        nc_has_feature(s, "token")) {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior authenticate:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        set token to request.headers.authorization\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        check token exists:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "            set decoded to verify_jwt with token\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "            check decoded.valid:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                set request.user to decoded.user\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "            otherwise:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "                respond with status 401 \"Invalid token\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        otherwise:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "            respond with status 401 \"No token provided\"\n\n");
    }

    if (nc_has_feature(s, "filter")) {
        nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior rate_limit:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        set client_ip to request.headers.x_forwarded_for\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        set count to recall from rate_limits where ip matches client_ip\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        check count > 100:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "            respond with status 429 \"Too many requests\"\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "        otherwise:\n");
        nc_buf_append(buf, "            remember count + 1 in rate_limits for client_ip\n\n");
    }

    nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior after_request:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set duration to now - start_time\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        show \"Completed in \" + duration + \"ms\"\n\n");

    nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior on_error:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        show \"Error: \" + error.message\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with status 500 \"Internal server error\"\n\n");
}

/* Generate AI service */
static void nc_gen_ai_service(NCBuf *buf, const NCScoutResult *s) {
    nc_buf_appendf(buf, "service %s on port 3000:\n\n", s->name);
    nc_buf_append(buf, "    connect to ai_provider\n\n");

    nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior predict:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set input to request.body.data\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set prompt to \"Analyze the following: \" + input\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set result to ask ai_provider with prompt\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        remember result in predictions\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with result\n\n");

    nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior train:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set training_data to request.body.data\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set model to train ai_provider with training_data\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with model.status\n\n");

    nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior evaluate:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set test_data to request.body.test_data\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        set metrics to evaluate ai_provider with test_data\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with metrics\n\n");

    nc_buf_append(buf, "    behavior get_predictions:\n");
    nc_buf_append(buf, "        respond with predictions\n\n");
}

/* Main worker dispatch */
static char *nc_ant_worker_generate(NCAnt *ant, NCColony *colony,
                                    const NCScoutResult *scout,
                                    int section_idx) {
    (void)section_idx;

    /* Check pheromone trails for cached pattern */
    char pattern_key[256];
    snprintf(pattern_key, sizeof(pattern_key), "%s_%s",
             scout->type_str, scout->name);
    const char *cached = nc_pheromone_lookup(colony->trail, pattern_key);
    if (cached) {
        nc_ant_remember(ant, "used_pheromone_pattern");
        ant->fitness = 0.8f;
        return nc_strdup(cached);
    }

    NCBuf buf = nc_buf_new(NC_COL_BUF_SIZE);

    if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "crud") == 0) {
        nc_gen_service(&buf, scout, 1);
    } else if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "service") == 0) {
        nc_gen_service(&buf, scout, 0);
    } else if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "ui") == 0) {
        nc_gen_ui(&buf, scout);
    } else if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "full_app") == 0) {
        nc_gen_full_app(&buf, scout);
    } else if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "test") == 0) {
        nc_gen_test(&buf, scout);
    } else if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "middleware") == 0) {
        nc_gen_middleware(&buf, scout);
    } else if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "ai") == 0) {
        nc_gen_ai_service(&buf, scout);
    } else {
        nc_gen_service(&buf, scout, 0);
    }

    nc_ant_remember(ant, "generated_code_section");
    ant->fitness = 0.6f;
    return nc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Validator Ant — checks NC syntax correctness
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static float nc_ant_validator_check(NCAnt *ant, const char *code) {
    if (!code || strlen(code) == 0) {
        ant->fitness = 0.0f;
        return 0.0f;
    }

    float score = 1.0f;
    int errors  = 0;
    int lines   = 0;

    const char *p = code;
    while (*p) { if (*p == '\n') lines++; p++; }
    if (lines == 0) lines = 1;

    /* Must have structural elements */
    int has_structure = 0;
    if (strstr(code, "service ") || strstr(code, "page ") ||
        strstr(code, "middleware ") || strstr(code, "test ") ||
        strstr(code, "to ")) {
        has_structure = 1;
    }
    if (!has_structure) { score -= 0.3f; errors++; }

    /* Must have colon-blocks */
    int colon_count = 0;
    p = code;
    while (*p) {
        if (*p == ':' && (*(p + 1) == '\n' || *(p + 1) == ' '))
            colon_count++;
        p++;
    }
    if (colon_count == 0 && lines > 3) { score -= 0.2f; errors++; }

    /* Check for tab indentation (NC uses spaces) */
    int indent_bad = 0;
    p = code;
    while (*p) {
        if (*p == '\n' && *(p + 1) == '\t') indent_bad++;
        p++;
    }
    if (indent_bad > 0) {
        score -= 0.1f * (float)indent_bad / (float)lines;
        errors++;
    }

    /* Must contain NC keywords */
    static const char *nc_keywords[] = {
        "set ", "to ", "show ", "respond ", "behavior ",
        "check ", "repeat ", "remember ", "connect ",
        "style:", "box ", "text ", "button ", "input ",
        "expect ", "test ", NULL
    };
    int keyword_hits = 0;
    for (int i = 0; nc_keywords[i]; i++) {
        if (strstr(code, nc_keywords[i])) keyword_hits++;
    }
    if (keyword_hits == 0) { score -= 0.3f; errors++; }

    /* Unmatched quotes */
    int quotes = 0;
    p = code;
    while (*p) { if (*p == '"') quotes++; p++; }
    if (quotes % 2 != 0) { score -= 0.2f; errors++; }

    if (score < 0.0f) score = 0.0f;

    nc_ant_remember(ant, errors == 0 ? "validation_passed" : "validation_issues");
    ant->fitness = score;
    return score;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Optimizer Ant — improves code using pheromone knowledge
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *nc_ant_optimizer_improve(NCAnt *ant, NCColony *colony,
                                       const char *code,
                                       const NCScoutResult *scout) {
    if (!code) return NULL;

    NCBuf buf = nc_buf_new(strlen(code) + 4096);
    nc_buf_append(&buf, code);

    /* Check pheromone trails for optimization patterns */
    char opt_key[256];
    snprintf(opt_key, sizeof(opt_key), "optimize_%s", scout->type_str);
    const char *opt_pattern = nc_pheromone_lookup(colony->trail, opt_key);

    if (opt_pattern) {
        nc_buf_append(&buf, "\n");
        nc_buf_append(&buf, opt_pattern);
        nc_ant_remember(ant, "applied_pheromone_optimization");
    } else {
        /* Add standard optimizations per type */
        if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "service") == 0 ||
            strcmp(scout->type_str, "crud") == 0) {
            if (!strstr(code, "handle_error") && !strstr(code, "on_error")) {
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "\n    behavior handle_error:\n");
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "        show \"Error: \" + error.message\n");
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "        respond with status 500 error.message\n\n");
            }
            if (!strstr(code, "health") && !strstr(code, "status")) {
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "    behavior health_check:\n");
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "        respond with status 200 \"OK\"\n\n");
            }
        }

        if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "ui") == 0) {
            if (!strstr(code, "loading")) {
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "\n    // Loading state\n");
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "    // check isLoading:\n");
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "    //     text \"Loading...\"\n");
            }
        }

        if (strcmp(scout->type_str, "full_app") == 0) {
            if (!strstr(code, "handle_error")) {
                nc_buf_append(&buf, "\n// === Error Handling ===\n\n");
                nc_buf_appendf(&buf, "    behavior handle_error:\n");
                nc_buf_append(&buf,  "        show \"Error: \" + error.message\n");
                nc_buf_append(&buf,  "        respond with status 500 error.message\n\n");
            }
        }

        nc_ant_remember(ant, "applied_standard_optimization");
    }

    ant->fitness = 0.7f;
    return nc_buf_detach(&buf);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Memory Ant — updates colony memory with results
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static void nc_ant_memory_update(NCAnt *ant, NCColony *colony,
                                  const char *problem, const char *solution,
                                  float fitness, const NCScoutResult *scout) {
    if (!colony || !problem || !solution) return;

    /* Deposit pheromone: problem pattern -> solution */
    char pkey[256];
    snprintf(pkey, sizeof(pkey), "%s_%s", scout->type_str, scout->name);
    nc_pheromone_deposit(colony->trail, pkey, solution, fitness);

    /* Mark success if fitness is high */
    if (fitness > 0.7f) {
        for (int i = 0; i < colony->trail->n_trails; i++) {
            if (colony->trail->trails[i].key &&
                strcmp(colony->trail->trails[i].key, pkey) == 0) {
                colony->trail->trails[i].successes++;
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    /* Store in episodic memory */
    char episode[512];
    snprintf(episode, sizeof(episode),
             "Solved '%s' (%s) with fitness %.2f", scout->name,
             scout->type_str, fitness);
    nc_colony_remember(colony, episode, "episodic");

    /* If fitness > 0.8, promote to procedural memory */
    if (fitness > 0.8f) {
        char proc[512];
        snprintf(proc, sizeof(proc),
                 "Best practice for %s: use %s approach (fitness %.2f)",
                 scout->type_str, scout->name, fitness);
        nc_colony_remember(colony, proc, "procedural");
    }

    /* Extract patterns for semantic memory */
    if (fitness > 0.5f) {
        char semantic[512];
        snprintf(semantic, sizeof(semantic),
                 "Pattern: %s type maps to %s template approach",
                 scout->type_str, scout->name);
        nc_colony_remember(colony, semantic, "semantic");
    }

    nc_ant_remember(ant, "updated_colony_memory");
    ant->fitness = 0.9f;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Colony Creation / Destruction
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCColony *nc_colony_create(int n_ants) {
    srand((unsigned int)time(NULL));

    if (n_ants <= 0) n_ants = NC_COL_DEFAULT_ANTS;

    NCColony *colony = (NCColony *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCColony));
    if (!colony) return NULL;

    /* Allocate ants with role distribution:
     * ~20% scouts, ~40% workers, ~15% validators,
     * ~15% optimizers, ~10% memory */
    colony->n_ants = n_ants;
    colony->ants   = (NCAnt *)calloc((size_t)n_ants, sizeof(NCAnt));
    if (!colony->ants) { free(colony); return NULL; }

    for (int i = 0; i < n_ants; i++) {
        NCAntType type;
        float ratio = (float)i / (float)n_ants;
        if      (ratio < 0.20f) type = NC_ANT_SCOUT;
        else if (ratio < 0.60f) type = NC_ANT_WORKER;
        else if (ratio < 0.75f) type = NC_ANT_VALIDATOR;
        else if (ratio < 0.90f) type = NC_ANT_OPTIMIZER;
        else                    type = NC_ANT_MEMORY;
        nc_ant_init(&colony->ants[i], i, type);
    }

    /* Create pheromone trail */
    colony->trail = nc_pheromone_create(NC_COL_PHEROMONE_CAP);
    if (!colony->trail) {
        for (int i = 0; i < n_ants; i++) nc_ant_free(&colony->ants[i]);
        free(colony->ants);
        free(colony);
        return NULL;
    }

    /* Initialize memory layers */
    colony->episodic_memory   = (char **)calloc(NC_COL_MEMORY_CAP, sizeof(char *));
    colony->semantic_memory   = (char **)calloc(NC_COL_MEMORY_CAP, sizeof(char *));
    colony->procedural_memory = (char **)calloc(NC_COL_MEMORY_CAP, sizeof(char *));
    colony->n_episodic   = 0;
    colony->n_semantic   = 0;
    colony->n_procedural = 0;

    /* Initialize Q-learning table */
    colony->q_states        = NC_Q_NUM_STATES;
    colony->q_actions       = NC_Q_NUM_ACTIONS;
    colony->q_learning_rate = 0.1f;
    colony->q_discount      = 0.9f;
    colony->q_table = (float *)calloc(
        (size_t)(colony->q_states * colony->q_actions), sizeof(float));

    /* Bootstrap semantic memory with NC language rules */
    for (int i = 0; NC_SEMANTIC_FACTS[i]; i++) {
        if (colony->n_semantic < NC_COL_MEMORY_CAP)
            colony->semantic_memory[colony->n_semantic++] =
                nc_strdup(NC_SEMANTIC_FACTS[i]);
    }

    /* Bootstrap procedural memory with NC how-to patterns */
    for (int i = 0; NC_PROCEDURAL_FACTS[i]; i++) {
        if (colony->n_procedural < NC_COL_MEMORY_CAP)
            colony->procedural_memory[colony->n_procedural++] =
                nc_strdup(NC_PROCEDURAL_FACTS[i]);
    }

    colony->total_generations = 0;
    colony->total_solutions   = 0;
    colony->avg_fitness       = 0.0f;

    return colony;
}

void nc_colony_free(NCColony *colony) {
    if (!colony) return;

    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_ants; i++)
        nc_ant_free(&colony->ants[i]);
    free(colony->ants);

    nc_pheromone_free(colony->trail);

    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_episodic; i++)
        free(colony->episodic_memory[i]);
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_semantic; i++)
        free(colony->semantic_memory[i]);
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_procedural; i++)
        free(colony->procedural_memory[i]);
    free(colony->episodic_memory);
    free(colony->semantic_memory);
    free(colony->procedural_memory);

    free(colony->q_table);
    free(colony);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Colony Memory Operations
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_colony_remember(NCColony *colony, const char *fact,
                        const char *category) {
    if (!colony || !fact || !category) return;

    char **target = NULL;
    int   *count  = NULL;

    if      (strcmp(category, "episodic")   == 0) { target = colony->episodic_memory;   count = &colony->n_episodic;   }
    else if (strcmp(category, "semantic")   == 0) { target = colony->semantic_memory;   count = &colony->n_semantic;   }
    else if (strcmp(category, "procedural") == 0) { target = colony->procedural_memory; count = &colony->n_procedural; }
    else return;

    if (!target) return;

    /* Dedup */
    for (int i = 0; i < *count; i++) {
        if (target[i] && strcmp(target[i], fact) == 0) return;
    }

    /* Evict oldest if full */
    if (*count >= NC_COL_MEMORY_CAP) {
        free(target[0]);
        memmove(target, target + 1, (size_t)(*count - 1) * sizeof(char *));
        (*count)--;
    }

    target[(*count)++] = nc_strdup(fact);
}

const char *nc_colony_recall(NCColony *colony, const char *query) {
    if (!colony || !query) return NULL;

    float best_score      = 0.0f;
    const char *best_match = NULL;

    /* Search semantic memory (highest priority) */
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_semantic; i++) {
        if (!colony->semantic_memory[i]) continue;
        float s = nc_fuzzy_match(query, colony->semantic_memory[i]);
        if (s > best_score) { best_score = s; best_match = colony->semantic_memory[i]; }
    }

    /* Search procedural memory */
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_procedural; i++) {
        if (!colony->procedural_memory[i]) continue;
        float s = nc_fuzzy_match(query, colony->procedural_memory[i]);
        if (s > best_score) { best_score = s; best_match = colony->procedural_memory[i]; }
    }

    /* Search episodic memory */
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_episodic; i++) {
        if (!colony->episodic_memory[i]) continue;
        float s = nc_fuzzy_match(query, colony->episodic_memory[i]);
        if (s > best_score) { best_score = s; best_match = colony->episodic_memory[i]; }
    }

    /* Also check pheromone trails */
    const char *pher = nc_pheromone_lookup(colony->trail, query);
    if (pher && 0.85f > best_score) {
        best_match = pher;
    }

    return best_match;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Q-Learning
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_colony_q_update(NCColony *colony, int state, int action,
                        float reward, int next_state) {
    if (!colony || !colony->q_table) return;
    if (state < 0 || state >= colony->q_states) return;
    if (action < 0 || action >= colony->q_actions) return;
    if (next_state < 0 || next_state >= colony->q_states) return;

    /* max Q(s', a') */
    float max_next = -1e9f;
    for (int a = 0; a < colony->q_actions; a++) {
        float val = colony->q_table[next_state * colony->q_actions + a];
        if (val > max_next) max_next = val;
    }

    /* Q(s,a) = Q(s,a) + alpha * [r + gamma * max(Q(s',a')) - Q(s,a)] */
    int idx    = state * colony->q_actions + action;
    float old  = colony->q_table[idx];
    colony->q_table[idx] = old + colony->q_learning_rate *
        (reward + colony->q_discount * max_next - old);
}

int nc_colony_q_best_action(NCColony *colony, int state) {
    if (!colony || !colony->q_table) return 0;
    if (state < 0 || state >= colony->q_states) return 0;

    /* Epsilon-greedy: 10% exploration */
    float r = (float)rand() / (float)RAND_MAX;
    if (r < NC_COL_EPSILON) {
        return rand() % colony->q_actions;
    }

    /* Exploit: best action */
    int   best_a = 0;
    float best_v = colony->q_table[state * colony->q_actions];
    for (int a = 1; a < colony->q_actions; a++) {
        float v = colony->q_table[state * colony->q_actions + a];
        if (v > best_v) { best_v = v; best_a = a; }
    }
    return best_a;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Colony Solve — the main multi-phase algorithm
 *
 *  Phase 1: Scout ants analyze the problem
 *  Phase 2: Check pheromone trails for cached solutions
 *  Phase 3: Q-learning selects approach
 *  Phase 4: Worker ants generate code sections
 *  Phase 5: Validator ants check each section
 *  Phase 6: Optimizer ants improve the best result
 *  Phase 7: Memory ants update colony state
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_colony_solve(NCColony *colony, const char *problem) {
    if (!colony || !problem) return NULL;

    /* ── Phase 1: Scout analysis ───────────────────────── */
    NCScoutResult scout;
    memset(&scout, 0, sizeof(scout));
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_ants; i++) {
        if (colony->ants[i].type == NC_ANT_SCOUT) {
            scout = nc_ant_scout_analyze(&colony->ants[i], problem);
            break;
        }
    }

    /* ── Phase 2: Pheromone cache check ────────────────── */
    char cache_key[256];
    snprintf(cache_key, sizeof(cache_key), "%s_%s",
             scout.type_str, scout.name);
    const char *cached = nc_pheromone_lookup(colony->trail, cache_key);
    if (cached) {
        for (int i = 0; i < colony->trail->n_trails; i++) {
            if (colony->trail->trails[i].key &&
                strcmp(colony->trail->trails[i].key, cache_key) == 0 &&
                colony->trail->trails[i].strength > NC_COL_REUSE_THRESHOLD) {
                colony->trail->trails[i].uses++;
                colony->total_solutions++;
                char *result = nc_strdup(cached);
                nc_scout_result_free(&scout);
                return result;
            }
        }
    }

    /* ── Phase 3: Q-learning selects approach ──────────── */
    int approach = nc_colony_q_best_action(colony, scout.q_state);

    /* ── Phase 4: Worker ants generate code ────────────── */
    char *best_code    = NULL;
    float best_fitness = -1.0f;
    int   worker_idx   = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_ants; i++) {
        if (colony->ants[i].type != NC_ANT_WORKER) continue;

        colony->ants[i].generation = colony->total_generations;
        free(colony->ants[i].current_task);
        colony->ants[i].current_task = nc_strdup(problem);

        char *code = nc_ant_worker_generate(&colony->ants[i], colony,
                                             &scout, worker_idx);
        worker_idx++;
        if (!code) continue;

        /* ── Phase 5: Validator check ──────────────────── */
        float validity = 0.0f;
        for (int v = 0; v < colony->n_ants; v++) {
            if (colony->ants[v].type == NC_ANT_VALIDATOR) {
                validity = nc_ant_validator_check(&colony->ants[v], code);
                break;
            }
        }

        float combined = colony->ants[i].fitness * 0.4f + validity * 0.6f;
        if (combined > best_fitness) {
            best_fitness = combined;
            free(best_code);
            best_code = code;
        } else {
            free(code);
        }
    }

    if (!best_code) {
        nc_scout_result_free(&scout);
        return NULL;
    }

    /* ── Phase 6: Optimizer improvement ────────────────── */
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_ants; i++) {
        if (colony->ants[i].type == NC_ANT_OPTIMIZER) {
            char *improved = nc_ant_optimizer_improve(
                &colony->ants[i], colony, best_code, &scout);
            if (improved) {
                free(best_code);
                best_code = improved;
                /* Re-validate */
                for (int v = 0; v < colony->n_ants; v++) {
                    if (colony->ants[v].type == NC_ANT_VALIDATOR) {
                        float nf = nc_ant_validator_check(
                            &colony->ants[v], best_code);
                        if (nf > best_fitness) best_fitness = nf;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            break;
        }
    }

    /* ── Phase 7: Memory update ────────────────────────── */
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_ants; i++) {
        if (colony->ants[i].type == NC_ANT_MEMORY) {
            nc_ant_memory_update(&colony->ants[i], colony, problem,
                                  best_code, best_fitness, &scout);
            break;
        }
    }

    /* Update Q-table */
    nc_colony_q_update(colony, scout.q_state, approach,
                       best_fitness, scout.q_state);

    /* Statistics */
    colony->total_generations++;
    colony->total_solutions++;
    colony->avg_fitness =
        (colony->avg_fitness * (float)(colony->total_solutions - 1)
         + best_fitness) / (float)colony->total_solutions;

    /* Evaporate pheromones */
    nc_pheromone_evaporate(colony->trail);

    /* Clear ant working memories for next round */
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_ants; i++)
        nc_ant_clear_memory(&colony->ants[i]);

    nc_scout_result_free(&scout);
    return best_code;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Colony Learning
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_colony_learn(NCColony *colony, const char *problem,
                     const char *solution, float reward) {
    if (!colony || !problem || !solution) return;
    if (reward < 0.0f) reward = 0.0f;
    if (reward > 1.0f) reward = 1.0f;

    /* 1. Deposit pheromone: problem -> solution, strength = reward */
    nc_pheromone_deposit(colony->trail, problem, solution, reward);

    /* 2. Update Q-table */
    unsigned int phash = nc_hash_str(problem);
    int state = (int)(phash % (unsigned int)colony->q_states);

    int action;
    if (strstr(solution, "template") || strstr(solution, "service "))
        action = NC_Q_ACTION_TEMPLATE;
    else if (strstr(solution, "pheromone") || strstr(solution, "cached"))
        action = NC_Q_ACTION_PHEROMONE;
    else
        action = NC_Q_ACTION_HYBRID;

    nc_colony_q_update(colony, state, action, reward, state);

    /* 3. Store in episodic memory */
    char episode[1024];
    snprintf(episode, sizeof(episode),
             "Solved '%.*s' with approach %d, reward %.2f",
             100, problem, action, reward);
    nc_colony_remember(colony, episode, "episodic");

    /* 4. Extract patterns -> semantic memory */
    if (reward > 0.5f) {
        char semantic[512];
        snprintf(semantic, sizeof(semantic),
                 "Pattern: '%.*s' -> successful with reward %.2f",
                 80, problem, reward);
        nc_colony_remember(colony, semantic, "semantic");
    }

    /* 5. Best practice -> procedural memory */
    if (reward > 0.8f) {
        char proc[512];
        snprintf(proc, sizeof(proc),
                 "Best practice: '%.*s' produces high-quality output (%.2f)",
                 80, problem, reward);
        nc_colony_remember(colony, proc, "procedural");
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Save / Load Colony State (Binary Format)
 *
 *  Format:
 *    [magic:4][version:4]
 *    [total_generations:4][total_solutions:4][avg_fitness:4]
 *    [n_trails:4][evaporation_rate:4][min_strength:4]
 *      for each trail: [key_len:4][key][val_len:4][val]
 *                      [strength:4][uses:4][successes:4][ts:4]
 *    [n_episodic:4] [strings...]
 *    [n_semantic:4] [strings...]
 *    [n_procedural:4] [strings...]
 *    [q_states:4][q_actions:4][lr:4][discount:4][q_table...]
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int write_str(FILE *f, const char *s) {
    if (!s) { int z = 0; return (int)fwrite(&z, sizeof(int), 1, f); }
    int len = (int)strlen(s);
    if (fwrite(&len, sizeof(int), 1, f) != 1) return 0;
    if (len > 0 && fwrite(s, 1, (size_t)len, f) != (size_t)len) return 0;
    return 1;
}

static char *read_str(FILE *f) {
    int len = 0;
    if (fread(&len, sizeof(int), 1, f) != 1) return NULL;
    if (len <= 0) return NULL;
    if (len > 10000000) return NULL;
    char *s = (char *)malloc((size_t)len + 1);
    if (!s) return NULL;
    if (fread(s, 1, (size_t)len, f) != (size_t)len) { free(s); return NULL; }
    s[len] = '\0';
    return s;
}

int nc_colony_save(NCColony *colony, const char *path) {
    if (!colony || !path) return 0;

    FILE *f = fopen(path, "wb");
    if (!f) return 0;

    unsigned int magic = NC_COLONY_MAGIC;
    int version = NC_COLONY_VERSION;
    fwrite(&magic,   sizeof(unsigned int), 1, f);
    fwrite(&version, sizeof(int), 1, f);

    fwrite(&colony->total_generations, sizeof(int),   1, f);
    fwrite(&colony->total_solutions,   sizeof(int),   1, f);
    fwrite(&colony->avg_fitness,       sizeof(float), 1, f);

    /* Pheromone trails */
    fwrite(&colony->trail->n_trails,        sizeof(int),   1, f);
    fwrite(&colony->trail->evaporation_rate, sizeof(float), 1, f);
    fwrite(&colony->trail->min_strength,     sizeof(float), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->trail->n_trails; i++) {
        write_str(f, colony->trail->trails[i].key);
        write_str(f, colony->trail->trails[i].value);
        fwrite(&colony->trail->trails[i].strength,  sizeof(float), 1, f);
        fwrite(&colony->trail->trails[i].uses,      sizeof(int),   1, f);
        fwrite(&colony->trail->trails[i].successes,  sizeof(int),   1, f);
        fwrite(&colony->trail->trails[i].timestamp,  sizeof(float), 1, f);
    }

    /* Memory layers */
    fwrite(&colony->n_episodic, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_episodic; i++)
        write_str(f, colony->episodic_memory[i]);

    fwrite(&colony->n_semantic, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_semantic; i++)
        write_str(f, colony->semantic_memory[i]);

    fwrite(&colony->n_procedural, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_procedural; i++)
        write_str(f, colony->procedural_memory[i]);

    /* Q-table */
    fwrite(&colony->q_states,        sizeof(int),   1, f);
    fwrite(&colony->q_actions,       sizeof(int),   1, f);
    fwrite(&colony->q_learning_rate, sizeof(float), 1, f);
    fwrite(&colony->q_discount,      sizeof(float), 1, f);
    int q_sz = colony->q_states * colony->q_actions;
    fwrite(colony->q_table, sizeof(float), (size_t)q_sz, f);

    fclose(f);
    return 1;
}

NCColony *nc_colony_load(const char *path) {
    if (!path) return NULL;

    FILE *f = fopen(path, "rb");
    if (!f) return NULL;

    unsigned int magic = 0;
    int version = 0;
    if (fread(&magic,   sizeof(unsigned int), 1, f) != 1 ||
        magic != NC_COLONY_MAGIC) { fclose(f); return NULL; }
    if (fread(&version, sizeof(int), 1, f) != 1 ||
        version != NC_COLONY_VERSION) { fclose(f); return NULL; }

    NCColony *colony = nc_colony_create(NC_COL_DEFAULT_ANTS);
    if (!colony) { fclose(f); return NULL; }

    /* Clear bootstrapped data (will be replaced) */
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_semantic; i++)
        free(colony->semantic_memory[i]);
    colony->n_semantic = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < colony->n_procedural; i++)
        free(colony->procedural_memory[i]);
    colony->n_procedural = 0;

    fread(&colony->total_generations, sizeof(int),   1, f);
    fread(&colony->total_solutions,   sizeof(int),   1, f);
    fread(&colony->avg_fitness,       sizeof(float), 1, f);

    /* Pheromone trails */
    int n_trails = 0;
    fread(&n_trails, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    fread(&colony->trail->evaporation_rate, sizeof(float), 1, f);
    fread(&colony->trail->min_strength,     sizeof(float), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_trails; i++) {
        char *key = read_str(f);
        char *val = read_str(f);
        float strength = 0; int uses = 0, successes = 0; float ts = 0;
        fread(&strength,  sizeof(float), 1, f);
        fread(&uses,      sizeof(int),   1, f);
        fread(&successes, sizeof(int),   1, f);
        fread(&ts,        sizeof(float), 1, f);
        if (key && val) {
            nc_pheromone_deposit(colony->trail, key, val, strength);
            int idx = colony->trail->n_trails - 1;
            if (idx >= 0) {
                colony->trail->trails[idx].uses      = uses;
                colony->trail->trails[idx].successes  = successes;
                colony->trail->trails[idx].timestamp  = ts;
            }
        }
        free(key);
        free(val);
    }

    /* Memory layers */
    int n = 0;
    fread(&n, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        char *s = read_str(f);
        if (s) { nc_colony_remember(colony, s, "episodic"); free(s); }
    }
    fread(&n, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        char *s = read_str(f);
        if (s) { nc_colony_remember(colony, s, "semantic"); free(s); }
    }
    fread(&n, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        char *s = read_str(f);
        if (s) { nc_colony_remember(colony, s, "procedural"); free(s); }
    }

    /* Q-table */
    int qs = 0, qa = 0;
    fread(&qs, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    fread(&qa, sizeof(int), 1, f);
    fread(&colony->q_learning_rate, sizeof(float), 1, f);
    fread(&colony->q_discount,      sizeof(float), 1, f);
    if (qs == colony->q_states && qa == colony->q_actions) {
        int q_sz = qs * qa;
        fread(colony->q_table, sizeof(float), (size_t)q_sz, f);
    }

    fclose(f);
    return colony;
}


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_ai_swarm.h

/*
 * nc_ai_swarm.h — Ant-Based Swarm Intelligence for NC AI.
 *
 * Instead of a single model generating code, multiple "ant agents"
 * explore different code paths, share knowledge through pheromone
 * trails, and collectively produce better NC code.
 *
 * Inspired by Ant Colony Optimization (ACO) applied to code generation.
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11 standard library.
 */

#ifndef NC_AI_SWARM_H
#define NC_AI_SWARM_H

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <time.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  NC AI Swarm Intelligence — Ant-Based Learning System
 *
 *  Unlike traditional LLMs, NC AI uses ant colony optimization:
 *  - Multiple ant agents explore code solution space
 *  - Pheromone trails reinforce good patterns
 *  - Colony memory retains successful solutions
 *  - Evaporation removes outdated patterns
 *  - Q-learning drives reinforcement decisions
 *
 *  By DevHeal Labs AI
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Ant types — different roles in the colony
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef enum {
    NC_ANT_SCOUT,       /* Explores problem space, finds patterns      */
    NC_ANT_WORKER,      /* Generates code sections                     */
    NC_ANT_VALIDATOR,   /* Validates generated code                    */
    NC_ANT_OPTIMIZER,   /* Optimizes and improves code                 */
    NC_ANT_MEMORY,      /* Manages colony memory                       */
} NCAntType;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Pheromone — shared knowledge between ants
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    char *key;          /* Pattern identifier                          */
    float strength;     /* 0.0 to 1.0 (evaporates over time)          */
    char *value;        /* Associated code pattern / solution          */
    int uses;           /* How many times this was used                */
    int successes;      /* How many times it led to success            */
    float timestamp;    /* When it was last updated                    */
} NCPheromone;

/* Pheromone trail — the colony's shared memory */
typedef struct {
    NCPheromone *trails;
    int n_trails;
    int capacity;
    float evaporation_rate;  /* 0.05 default (5% decay per cycle)     */
    float min_strength;      /* 0.01 threshold for removal            */
} NCPheromoneTrail;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Single ant agent
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    int id;
    NCAntType type;
    char *current_task;
    float fitness;          /* How well this ant performed             */
    int generation;         /* Which generation this ant belongs to    */
    /* Ant's local memory (what it has learned) */
    char **local_memory;
    int memory_size;
    int memory_capacity;
} NCAnt;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Colony — the swarm
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    NCAnt *ants;
    int n_ants;
    NCPheromoneTrail *trail;

    /* Colony memory (long-term) */
    char **episodic_memory;     /* Past experiences                    */
    int n_episodic;
    char **semantic_memory;     /* Learned facts about NC              */
    int n_semantic;
    char **procedural_memory;   /* How to do things                    */
    int n_procedural;

    /* Q-learning table for reinforcement */
    float *q_table;             /* state-action values                 */
    int q_states;
    int q_actions;
    float q_learning_rate;
    float q_discount;

    /* Statistics */
    int total_generations;
    int total_solutions;
    float avg_fitness;
} NCColony;

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Colony lifecycle
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCColony *nc_colony_create(int n_ants);
void nc_colony_free(NCColony *colony);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Pheromone operations
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCPheromoneTrail *nc_pheromone_create(int capacity);
void nc_pheromone_deposit(NCPheromoneTrail *trail, const char *key,
                          const char *value, float strength);
const char *nc_pheromone_lookup(NCPheromoneTrail *trail, const char *key);
void nc_pheromone_evaporate(NCPheromoneTrail *trail);
void nc_pheromone_free(NCPheromoneTrail *trail);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Colony operations
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_colony_solve(NCColony *colony, const char *problem);
void nc_colony_learn(NCColony *colony, const char *problem,
                     const char *solution, float reward);
void nc_colony_remember(NCColony *colony, const char *fact,
                        const char *category);
const char *nc_colony_recall(NCColony *colony, const char *query);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Q-learning
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

void nc_colony_q_update(NCColony *colony, int state, int action,
                        float reward, int next_state);
int nc_colony_q_best_action(NCColony *colony, int state);

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Persistence — save/load colony state
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_colony_save(NCColony *colony, const char *path);
NCColony *nc_colony_load(const char *path);

#endif /* NC_AI_SWARM_H */


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_dataset.c

/*
 * nc_dataset.c — Synthetic data generator for NC language training.
 *
 * Generates valid NC code examples by combining grammar rules
 * with randomized identifiers, types, and structures. This is
 * the key insight: NC's grammar is small and well-defined, so we
 * can generate unlimited training data from the rules themselves.
 *
 * The model learns the language by seeing every valid pattern.
 */

#include "nc_dataset.h"
#include <stdarg.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Random helpers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static int ds_rand_initialized = 0;

static void ds_rand_init(void) {
    if (!ds_rand_initialized) {
        srand((unsigned int)time(NULL) ^ 0xBEEF);
        ds_rand_initialized = 1;
    }
}

static int rand_range(int lo, int hi) {
    return lo + rand() % (hi - lo + 1);
}

static const char *rand_pick(const char **arr, int n) {
    return arr[rand() % n];
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Word pools for random generation
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

    "ReportService", "InventoryService", "BookingService",
    "CommentService", "ProfileService", "DashboardService"

#define N_STRING_VALUES 18

    "/notifications", "/files/upload", "/reports", "/settings"

    "Register", "Profile", "Settings", "Blog", "Products",

    "minimal", "modern", "classic", "neon", "pastel"
};
#define N_THEME_NAMES 10

static const char *SECTION_TITLES[] = {

    "Pricing", "Contact", "Testimonials", "FAQ",
    "Gallery", "Services", "Blog", "Portfolio"
};
#define N_SECTION_TITLES 12

    "Get Started", "Contact Us", "Download", "Try Free",
    "Buy Now", "Subscribe", "Cancel", "Save"
};
#define N_BUTTON_TEXTS 12

static const char *COLORS[] = {
    "blue", "red", "green", "purple", "orange",
    "teal", "pink", "indigo", "amber", "gray"
};
#define N_COLORS 10

static const char *SIZES[] = { "sm", "md", "lg", "xl" };
#define N_SIZES 4

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  String buffer helper
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

typedef struct {
    char *buf;
    int   len;
    int   cap;
} StrBuf;

static StrBuf strbuf_new(int cap) {
    StrBuf sb;
    sb.cap = cap;
    sb.len = 0;
    sb.buf = (char *)malloc(cap);
    sb.buf[0] = '\0';
    return sb;
}

static void strbuf_append(StrBuf *sb, const char *str) {
    int slen = (int)strlen(str);
    while (sb->len + slen + 1 > sb->cap) {
        sb->cap *= 2;
        sb->buf = realloc(sb->buf, sb->cap);
    }
    memcpy(sb->buf + sb->len, str, slen);
    sb->len += slen;
    sb->buf[sb->len] = '\0';
}

static void strbuf_appendf(StrBuf *sb, const char *fmt, ...) {
    char tmp[512];
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, fmt);
    vsnprintf(tmp, sizeof(tmp), fmt, args);
    va_end(args);
    strbuf_append(sb, tmp);
}

static char *strbuf_finish(StrBuf *sb) {
    return sb->buf; /* caller owns the memory */
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Dataset lifecycle
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCDataset *nc_dataset_create(void) {
    ds_rand_init();

    NCDataset *ds = (NCDataset *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCDataset));
    if (!ds) return NULL;

    ds->capacity = 256;
    ds->examples = (char **)calloc(ds->capacity, sizeof(char *));
    ds->n_examples = 0;

    return ds;
}

void nc_dataset_free(NCDataset *ds) {
    if (!ds) return;
    for (int i = 0; i < ds->n_examples; i++) {
        free(ds->examples[i]);
    }
    free(ds->examples);
    free(ds);
}

static void ds_add(NCDataset *ds, char *example) {
    if (ds->n_examples >= ds->capacity) {
        ds->capacity *= 2;
        ds->examples = realloc(ds->examples, ds->capacity * sizeof(char *));
    }
    ds->examples[ds->n_examples++] = example;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Generate NC backend code examples
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* Generate a random service definition */
static char *gen_service(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(512);
    const char *svc = rand_pick(SERVICE_NAMES, N_SERVICE_NAMES);
    int version = rand_range(1, 3);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "service %s version %d\n\n", svc, version);

    /* Add some behaviors */
    int n_behaviors = rand_range(1, 4);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_behaviors; i++) {
        const char *beh = rand_pick(BEHAVIOR_NAMES, N_BEHAVIOR_NAMES);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "to %s:\n", beh);

        /* Random body statements */
        int n_stmts = rand_range(1, 4);
        for (int j = 0; j < n_stmts; j++) {
            int kind = rand_range(0, 5);
            switch (kind) {
                case 0: {
                    const char *var = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
                    const char *val = rand_pick(STRING_VALUES, N_STRING_VALUES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set %s to \"%s\"\n", var, val);
                    break;
                }
                case 1: {
                    const char *msg = rand_pick(STRING_VALUES, N_STRING_VALUES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    respond with \"%s\"\n", msg);
                    break;
                }
                case 2: {
                    const char *var = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    show %s\n", var);
                    break;
                }
                case 3: {
                    const char *var = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set %s to %d\n", var, rand_range(1, 1000));
                    break;
                }
                case 4: {
                    const char *db = rand_pick(DB_NAMES, N_DB_NAMES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    store data in \"%s\"\n", db);
                    break;
                }
                case 5: {
                    const char *db = rand_pick(DB_NAMES, N_DB_NAMES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    load data from \"%s\"\n", db);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        strbuf_append(&sb, "\n");
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

/* Generate random API routes */
static char *gen_api_routes(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(512);

    int n_routes = rand_range(2, 5);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_routes; i++) {
        const char *methods[] = {"GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE"};
        const char *method = rand_pick(methods, 4);
        const char *route = rand_pick(ROUTES, N_ROUTES);
        const char *beh = rand_pick(BEHAVIOR_NAMES, N_BEHAVIOR_NAMES);

        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "api %s \"%s\" to %s\n", method, route, beh);
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

/* Generate random control flow */
static char *gen_control_flow(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(512);
    int kind = rand_range(0, 3);

    switch (kind) {
        case 0: {
            /* if/else */
            const char *var = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
            int val = rand_range(1, 100);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "if %s is %d:\n", var, val);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    show \"%s matched\"\n", var);
            if (rand_range(0, 1)) {
                strbuf_append(&sb, "else:\n");
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    show \"%s did not match\"\n", var);
            }
            break;
        }
        case 1: {
            /* repeat */
            int times = rand_range(2, 10);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "repeat %d:\n", times);
            const char *var = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    show %s\n", var);
            break;
        }
        case 2: {
            /* while */
            const char *var = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "set %s to 0\n", var);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "while %s < 10:\n", var);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set %s to %s + 1\n", var, var);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    show %s\n", var);
            break;
        }
        case 3: {
            /* nested if */
            const char *v1 = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
            const char *v2 = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "if %s is true:\n", v1);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    if %s > 0:\n", v2);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        show \"both conditions met\"\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    else:\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        show \"only first met\"\n");
            break;
        }
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

/* Generate middleware config */
static char *gen_middleware(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(256);

    const char *mw_types[] = {"auth", "logging", "cors", "rateLimit", "cache"};
    const char *mw = rand_pick(mw_types, 5);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "middleware %s:\n", mw);

    if (strcmp(mw, "auth") == 0) {
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set type to \"jwt\"\n");
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set secret to \"my-secret-key\"\n");
    } else if (strcmp(mw, "logging") == 0) {
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set level to \"info\"\n");
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set format to \"json\"\n");
    } else if (strcmp(mw, "cors") == 0) {
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set origin to \"*\"\n");
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set methods to \"GET, POST, PUT, DELETE\"\n");
    } else if (strcmp(mw, "rateLimit") == 0) {
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set max to %d\n", rand_range(50, 200));
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set window to \"1m\"\n");
    } else {
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set ttl to %d\n", rand_range(60, 3600));
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set strategy to \"lru\"\n");
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

/* Generate database operations */
static char *gen_db_ops(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(512);
    const char *db = rand_pick(DB_NAMES, N_DB_NAMES);
    int kind = rand_range(0, 3);

    switch (kind) {
        case 0:
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "connect to \"%s\"\n", db);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "create in \"%s\" with name: \"example\", status: \"active\"\n", db);
            break;
        case 1:
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "connect to \"%s\"\n", db);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "read from \"%s\" where id is %d\n", db, rand_range(1, 100));
            break;
        case 2:
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "connect to \"%s\"\n", db);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "update \"%s\" where id is %d with status: \"updated\"\n",
                           db, rand_range(1, 100));
            break;
        case 3:
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "connect to \"%s\"\n", db);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "delete from \"%s\" where id is %d\n", db, rand_range(1, 100));
            break;
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

/* Generate HTTP client calls */
static char *gen_http_call(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(256);
    const char *methods[] = {"GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE"};
    const char *method = rand_pick(methods, 4);
    const char *url = rand_pick(ROUTES, N_ROUTES);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "call %s \"https://api.example.com%s\"\n", method, url);
    if (strcmp(method, "POST") == 0 || strcmp(method, "PUT") == 0) {
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    with body: name: \"test\", value: 42\n");
    }
    strbuf_append(&sb, "    set result to response\n");

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

/* Generate a complete NC service file */
static char *gen_full_service(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(2048);
    const char *svc = rand_pick(SERVICE_NAMES, N_SERVICE_NAMES);
    int version = rand_range(1, 3);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "service %s version %d\n\n", svc, version);

    /* Middleware */
    if (rand_range(0, 1)) {
        const char *mw_types[] = {"auth", "logging", "cors"};
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "middleware %s:\n", rand_pick(mw_types, 3));
        strbuf_append(&sb, "    set enabled to true\n\n");
    }

    /* Database connection */
    if (rand_range(0, 1)) {
        const char *db = rand_pick(DB_NAMES, N_DB_NAMES);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "connect to \"%s\"\n\n", db);
    }

    /* Behaviors */
    int n_beh = rand_range(2, 5);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_beh; i++) {
        const char *beh = rand_pick(BEHAVIOR_NAMES, N_BEHAVIOR_NAMES);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "to %s:\n", beh);

        int n_stmts = rand_range(2, 5);
        for (int j = 0; j < n_stmts; j++) {
            int kind = rand_range(0, 7);
            const char *var = rand_pick(VAR_NAMES, N_VAR_NAMES);
            switch (kind) {
                case 0:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set %s to \"%s\"\n",
                                   var, rand_pick(STRING_VALUES, N_STRING_VALUES));
                    break;
                case 1:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set %s to %d\n",
                                   var, rand_range(1, 1000));
                    break;
                case 2:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    show %s\n", var);
                    break;
                case 3:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    respond with %s\n", var);
                    break;
                case 4:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    if %s is true:\n", var);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        respond with \"ok\"\n");
                    break;
                case 5: {
                    const char *db = rand_pick(DB_NAMES, N_DB_NAMES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    store %s in \"%s\"\n", var, db);
                    break;
                }
                case 6: {
                    const char *db = rand_pick(DB_NAMES, N_DB_NAMES);
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    load %s from \"%s\"\n", var, db);
                    break;
                }
                case 7:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    ask \"%s?\"\n", var);
                    break;
            }
        }
        strbuf_append(&sb, "\n");
    }

    /* API routes */
    int n_routes = rand_range(1, 4);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_routes; i++) {
        const char *methods[] = {"GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE"};
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "api %s \"%s\" to %s\n",
                       rand_pick(methods, 4),
                       rand_pick(ROUTES, N_ROUTES),
                       rand_pick(BEHAVIOR_NAMES, N_BEHAVIOR_NAMES));
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

void nc_dataset_generate_nc(NCDataset *ds, int n_examples) {
    ds_rand_init();

    for (int i = 0; i < n_examples; i++) {
        int kind = rand_range(0, 7);
        char *example = NULL;

        switch (kind) {
            case 0: example = gen_service(); break;
            case 1: example = gen_api_routes(); break;
            case 2: example = gen_control_flow(); break;
            case 3: example = gen_middleware(); break;
            case 4: example = gen_db_ops(); break;
            case 5: example = gen_http_call(); break;
            case 6:
            case 7: example = gen_full_service(); break;
        }

        if (example) ds_add(ds, example);
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Generate NC UI code examples
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *gen_page(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(1024);
    const char *page = rand_pick(PAGE_NAMES, N_PAGE_NAMES);
    const char *theme = rand_pick(THEME_NAMES, N_THEME_NAMES);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "page %s:\n", page);
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    theme %s\n\n", theme);

    /* Sections */
    int n_sections = rand_range(1, 4);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_sections; i++) {
        const char *title = rand_pick(SECTION_TITLES, N_SECTION_TITLES);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    section \"%s\":\n", title);

        int n_items = rand_range(1, 3);
        for (int j = 0; j < n_items; j++) {
            int kind = rand_range(0, 4);
            switch (kind) {
                case 0:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"%s\"\n", title);
                    break;
                case 1:
