                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        text \"Welcome to our %s page.\"\n",
                                   page);
                    break;
                case 2:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        button \"%s\":\n",
                                   rand_pick(BUTTON_TEXTS, N_BUTTON_TEXTS));
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            style %s %s\n",
                                   rand_pick(COLORS, N_COLORS),
                                   rand_pick(SIZES, N_SIZES));
                    break;
                case 3:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        image \"hero.jpg\":\n");
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            style width: 100%%\n");
                    break;
                case 4:
                    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        link \"/about\" text \"Learn More\"\n");
                    break;
            }
        }
        strbuf_append(&sb, "\n");
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

static char *gen_nav(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(512);

    strbuf_append(&sb, "nav:\n");
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    heading \"%s\"\n",
                   rand_pick(SERVICE_NAMES, N_SERVICE_NAMES));

    int n_links = rand_range(3, 6);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_links; i++) {
        const char *page = rand_pick(PAGE_NAMES, N_PAGE_NAMES);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    link \"/%s\" text \"%s\"\n",
                       page, page);
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

static char *gen_grid(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(1024);
    int cols = rand_range(2, 4);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "grid columns %d:\n", cols);

    int n_cards = rand_range(cols, cols * 2);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_cards; i++) {
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    card:\n");
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"Card %d\"\n", i + 1);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        text \"Description for card %d.\"\n", i + 1);
        if (rand_range(0, 1)) {
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        button \"%s\":\n",
                           rand_pick(BUTTON_TEXTS, N_BUTTON_TEXTS));
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            style %s\n",
                           rand_pick(COLORS, N_COLORS));
        }
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

static char *gen_form(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(512);
    const char *form_names[] = {"Login", "Register", "Contact", "Search",
                                "Subscribe", "Feedback", "Settings"};
    const char *form = rand_pick(form_names, 7);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "form \"%s\":\n", form);

    int n_fields = rand_range(2, 5);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_fields; i++) {
        const char *types[] = {"text", "email", "password", "number", "textarea"};
        const char *labels[] = {"Name", "Email", "Password", "Phone",
                                "Message", "Age", "Username", "Address"};
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    input type \"%s\" label \"%s\"\n",
                       rand_pick(types, 5), rand_pick(labels, 8));
    }

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    button \"%s\":\n",
                   rand_pick(BUTTON_TEXTS, N_BUTTON_TEXTS));
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        style %s %s\n",
                   rand_pick(COLORS, N_COLORS), rand_pick(SIZES, N_SIZES));

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

static char *gen_component(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(512);
    const char *comp_names[] = {
        "Counter", "Toggle", "Timer", "Dropdown",
        "Modal", "Accordion", "Carousel", "Alert"
    };
    const char *comp = rand_pick(comp_names, 8);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "component %s:\n", comp);
    strbuf_append(&sb, "    state:\n");

    int n_state = rand_range(1, 3);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_state; i++) {
        const char *vars[] = {"count", "isOpen", "value", "selected", "active"};
        const char *vals[] = {"0", "false", "\"\"", "null", "true"};
        int idx = rand_range(0, 4);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        set %s to %s\n", vars[idx], vals[idx]);
    }

    strbuf_append(&sb, "\n    action toggle:\n");
    strbuf_append(&sb, "        set isOpen to not isOpen\n");

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "\n    section \"%s\":\n", comp);
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"%s\"\n", comp);
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        button \"Toggle\":\n");
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            action toggle\n");

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

static char *gen_full_page(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(2048);
    const char *page = rand_pick(PAGE_NAMES, N_PAGE_NAMES);
    const char *theme = rand_pick(THEME_NAMES, N_THEME_NAMES);

    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "page %s:\n", page);
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    theme %s\n\n", theme);

    /* Nav */
    strbuf_append(&sb, "    nav:\n");
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"%s App\"\n", page);
    int n_links = rand_range(2, 4);
    for (int i = 0; i < n_links; i++) {
        const char *p = rand_pick(PAGE_NAMES, N_PAGE_NAMES);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        link \"/%s\" text \"%s\"\n", p, p);
    }
    strbuf_append(&sb, "\n");

    /* Hero section */
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    section \"Hero\":\n");
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"Welcome to %s\"\n", page);
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        text \"Your one-stop solution for everything.\"\n");
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        button \"%s\":\n",
                   rand_pick(BUTTON_TEXTS, N_BUTTON_TEXTS));
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            style %s lg\n", rand_pick(COLORS, N_COLORS));
    strbuf_append(&sb, "\n");

    /* Content grid */
    if (rand_range(0, 1)) {
        int cols = rand_range(2, 4);
        strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    grid columns %d:\n", cols);
        for (int i = 0; i < cols; i++) {
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        card:\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            heading \"Feature %d\"\n", i + 1);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            text \"Description of feature %d.\"\n", i + 1);
        }
        strbuf_append(&sb, "\n");
    }

    /* Footer */
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    footer:\n");
    strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        text \"(c) 2026 %s App. All rights reserved.\"\n", page);

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

void nc_dataset_generate_ncui(NCDataset *ds, int n_examples) {
    ds_rand_init();

    for (int i = 0; i < n_examples; i++) {
        int kind = rand_range(0, 6);
        char *example = NULL;

        switch (kind) {
            case 0: example = gen_page(); break;
            case 1: example = gen_nav(); break;
            case 2: example = gen_grid(); break;
            case 3: example = gen_form(); break;
            case 4: example = gen_component(); break;
            case 5:
            case 6: example = gen_full_page(); break;
        }

        if (example) ds_add(ds, example);
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Generate (description, code) prompt pairs
 *
 *  Format: "PROMPT: <description>\nCODE:\n<nc code>"
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *gen_prompt_pair_backend(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(2048);

    int kind = rand_range(0, 5);

    switch (kind) {
        case 0: {
            const char *svc = rand_pick(SERVICE_NAMES, N_SERVICE_NAMES);
            const char *beh = rand_pick(BEHAVIOR_NAMES, N_BEHAVIOR_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: a %s with a %s behavior\nCODE:\n", svc, beh);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "service %s version 1\n\n", svc);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "to %s:\n", beh);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set result to \"done\"\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    respond with result\n");
            break;
        }
        case 1: {
            const char *route = rand_pick(ROUTES, N_ROUTES);
            const char *beh = rand_pick(BEHAVIOR_NAMES, N_BEHAVIOR_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: an API endpoint for %s\nCODE:\n", route);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "to %s:\n", beh);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    load data from \"database\"\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    respond with data\n\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "api GET \"%s\" to %s\n", route, beh);
            break;
        }
        case 2: {
            const char *db = rand_pick(DB_NAMES, N_DB_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: connect to %s database and read data\nCODE:\n", db);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "connect to \"%s\"\n", db);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "read from \"%s\" where status is \"active\"\n", db);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "show result\n");
            break;
        }
        case 3: {
            strbuf_append(&sb, "PROMPT: a loop that counts from 1 to 10\nCODE:\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "set count to 0\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "repeat 10:\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    set count to count + 1\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    show count\n");
            break;
        }
        case 4: {
            const char *mw = rand_range(0, 1) ? "auth" : "logging";
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: add %s middleware\nCODE:\n", mw);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "middleware %s:\n", mw);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set enabled to true\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    set type to \"%s\"\n",
                           strcmp(mw, "auth") == 0 ? "jwt" : "json");
            break;
        }
        case 5: {
            const char *svc = rand_pick(SERVICE_NAMES, N_SERVICE_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: a complete %s with CRUD operations\nCODE:\n", svc);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "service %s version 1\n\n", svc);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "connect to \"database\"\n\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "to create:\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    store data in \"items\"\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    respond with \"created\"\n\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "to getAll:\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    load items from \"items\"\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    respond with items\n\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "to update:\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    update \"items\" where id is id with data\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    respond with \"updated\"\n\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "to remove:\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    delete from \"items\" where id is id\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    respond with \"deleted\"\n\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "api POST \"/items\" to create\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "api GET \"/items\" to getAll\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "api PUT \"/items\" to update\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "api DELETE \"/items\" to remove\n");
            break;
        }
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

static char *gen_prompt_pair_ui(void) {
    StrBuf sb = strbuf_new(2048);

    int kind = rand_range(0, 4);

    switch (kind) {
        case 0: {
            const char *page = rand_pick(PAGE_NAMES, N_PAGE_NAMES);
            const char *theme = rand_pick(THEME_NAMES, N_THEME_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: a %s page with %s theme\nCODE:\n", page, theme);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "page %s:\n", page);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    theme %s\n\n", theme);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    section \"Main\":\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"Welcome to %s\"\n", page);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        text \"This is the %s page.\"\n", page);
            break;
        }
        case 1: {
            const char *page = rand_pick(PAGE_NAMES, N_PAGE_NAMES);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: a %s page with navigation bar\nCODE:\n", page);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "page %s:\n", page);
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    theme modern\n\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    nav:\n");
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"%s\"\n", page);
            strbuf_append(&sb, "        link \"/home\" text \"Home\"\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "        link \"/about\" text \"About\"\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "        link \"/contact\" text \"Contact\"\n");
            break;
        }
        case 2: {
            int cols = rand_range(2, 4);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: a %d-column card grid\nCODE:\n", cols);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "grid columns %d:\n", cols);
            for (int i = 0; i < cols; i++) {
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    card:\n");
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        heading \"Item %d\"\n", i + 1);
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        text \"Description %d\"\n", i + 1);
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "        button \"View\":\n");
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "            style %s\n", rand_pick(COLORS, N_COLORS));
            }
            break;
        }
        case 3: {
            strbuf_append(&sb, "PROMPT: a contact form with name, email, and message\nCODE:\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "form \"Contact\":\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    input type \"text\" label \"Name\"\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    input type \"email\" label \"Email\"\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    input type \"textarea\" label \"Message\"\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    button \"Send\":\n");
            strbuf_append(&sb, "        style blue lg\n");
            break;
        }
        case 4: {
            const char *comp = rand_range(0, 1) ? "Counter" : "Toggle";
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "PROMPT: a %s component with state\nCODE:\n", comp);
            strbuf_appendf(&sb, "component %s:\n", comp);
            strbuf_append(&sb, "    state:\n");
            if (strcmp(comp, "Counter") == 0) {
                strbuf_append(&sb, "        set count to 0\n\n");
                strbuf_append(&sb, "    action increment:\n");
                strbuf_append(&sb, "        set count to count + 1\n\n");
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    section \"%s\":\n", comp);
                strbuf_append(&sb, "        text count\n");
                strbuf_append(&sb, "        button \"Add\":\n");
                strbuf_append(&sb, "            action increment\n");
            } else {
                strbuf_append(&sb, "        set active to false\n\n");
                strbuf_append(&sb, "    action toggle:\n");
                strbuf_append(&sb, "        set active to not active\n\n");
                strbuf_appendf(&sb, "    section \"%s\":\n", comp);
                strbuf_append(&sb, "        button \"Toggle\":\n");
                strbuf_append(&sb, "            action toggle\n");
            }
            break;
        }
    }

    return strbuf_finish(&sb);
}

void nc_dataset_generate_prompt_pairs(NCDataset *ds, int n_examples) {
    ds_rand_init();

    for (int i = 0; i < n_examples; i++) {
        char *example;
        if (rand_range(0, 1)) {
            example = gen_prompt_pair_backend();
        } else {
            example = gen_prompt_pair_ui();
        }
        if (example) ds_add(ds, example);
    }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Save / Load dataset
 *
 *  Format: examples separated by "\n---\n"
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_dataset_save(const NCDataset *ds, const char *path) {
    FILE *f = fopen(path, "w");
    if (!f) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc_dataset] Error: cannot open '%s' for writing\n", path);
        return -1;
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < ds->n_examples; i++) {
        fprintf(f, "%s", ds->examples[i]);
        if (i < ds->n_examples - 1) {
            fprintf(f, "\n---\n");
        }
    }

    fclose(f);
    printf("[nc_dataset] Saved %d examples to '%s'\n", ds->n_examples, path);
    return 0;
}

NCDataset *nc_dataset_load(const char *path) {
    FILE *f = fopen(path, "r");
    if (!f) {
        fprintf(stderr, "[nc_dataset] Error: cannot open '%s' for reading\n", path);
        return NULL;
    }

    /* Read entire file */
    fseek(f, 0, SEEK_END);
    long len = ftell(f);
    fseek(f, 0, SEEK_SET);

    if (len <= 0) { fclose(f); return NULL; }

    char *content = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
    size_t rd = fread(content, 1, len, f);
    content[rd] = '\0';
    fclose(f);

    NCDataset *ds = nc_dataset_create();

    /* Split by "\n---\n" */
    char *ptr = content;
    while (ptr && *ptr) {
        char *sep = strstr(ptr, "\n---\n");
        int example_len;

        if (sep) {
            example_len = (int)(sep - ptr);
        } else {
            example_len = (int)strlen(ptr);
        }

        if (example_len > 0) {
            char *example = (char *)malloc(example_len + 1);
            memcpy(example, ptr, example_len);
            example[example_len] = '\0';
            ds_add(ds, example);
        }

        if (sep) {
            ptr = sep + 5; /* skip "\n---\n" */
        } else {
            break;
        }
    }

    free(content);
    printf("[nc_dataset] Loaded %d examples from '%s'\n", ds->n_examples, path);
    return ds;
}


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_dataset.h

/*
 * nc_dataset.h — Synthetic data generator for NC language training.
 *
 * Generates valid NC code examples from grammar rules,
 * providing unlimited training data for the NC model.
 */

#ifndef NC_DATASET_H
#define NC_DATASET_H

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <time.h>
#include <stdbool.h>

typedef struct {
    char **examples;
    int    n_examples;
    int    capacity;
} NCDataset;

/* ── Lifecycle ─────────────────────────────────────────── */

NCDataset *nc_dataset_create(void);
void       nc_dataset_free(NCDataset *ds);

/* ── Generation ────────────────────────────────────────── */

void nc_dataset_generate_nc(NCDataset *ds, int n_examples);
void nc_dataset_generate_ncui(NCDataset *ds, int n_examples);
void nc_dataset_generate_prompt_pairs(NCDataset *ds, int n_examples);

/* ── Save / Load ───────────────────────────────────────── */

int        nc_dataset_save(const NCDataset *ds, const char *path);
NCDataset *nc_dataset_load(const char *path);

#endif /* NC_DATASET_H */


// FILE: nc-ai/engine/src/nc_generate.c

/*
 * nc_generate.c — Code generation from natural language descriptions.
 *
 * Implements two generation pipelines:
 *   1. Template engine  — always available, rule-based NLU + code templates
 *   2. Neural model     — uses the NC transformer when weights exist
 *
 * Usage from CLI:
 *   nc generate "a blog service with auth"
 *   nc generate --ui "a dark portfolio page"
 *   nc generate --full "a todo app with login"
 *   nc generate --type crud "users"
 *   nc train
 *   nc train --data ./examples/
 *
 * No external dependencies — pure C11.
 */

#include "nc_generate.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>
#include <stdarg.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <errno.h>

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Internal helpers
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

#define NC_GEN_BUF_INIT  8192
#define NC_GEN_BUF_MAX   (1 << 20)  /* 1 MiB ceiling */
#define NC_MAX_FEATURES  32

/* Dynamic string buffer */
typedef struct {
    char  *data;
    size_t len;
    size_t cap;
} NCBuf;

static NCBuf nc_buf_new(void) {
    NCBuf b;
    b.cap  = NC_GEN_BUF_INIT;
    b.len  = 0;
    b.data = (char *)malloc(b.cap);
    if (b.data) b.data[0] = '\0';
    return b;
}

static void nc_buf_free(NCBuf *b) {
    free(b->data);
    b->data = NULL;
    b->len  = 0;
    b->cap  = 0;
}

static void nc_buf_grow(NCBuf *b, size_t need) {
    if (b->len + need + 1 <= b->cap) return;
    size_t new_cap = b->cap * 2;
    while (new_cap < b->len + need + 1) new_cap *= 2;
    if (new_cap > NC_GEN_BUF_MAX) new_cap = NC_GEN_BUF_MAX;
    char *tmp = (char *)realloc(b->data, new_cap);
    if (!tmp) return;
    b->data = tmp;
    b->cap  = new_cap;
}

static void nc_buf_append(NCBuf *b, const char *s) {
    size_t slen = strlen(s);
    nc_buf_grow(b, slen);
    memcpy(b->data + b->len, s, slen);
    b->len += slen;
    b->data[b->len] = '\0';
}

static void nc_buf_printf(NCBuf *b, const char *fmt, ...) {
    va_list ap;
    va_start(ap, fmt);
    /* Measure first */
    va_list ap2;
    va_copy(ap2, ap);
    int need = vsnprintf(NULL, 0, fmt, ap2);
    va_end(ap2);
    if (need < 0) { va_end(ap); return; }
    nc_buf_grow(b, (size_t)need);
    vsnprintf(b->data + b->len, b->cap - b->len, fmt, ap);
    b->len += (size_t)need;
    b->data[b->len] = '\0';
    va_end(ap);
}

/* Duplicate the buffer content as a standalone string, caller frees */
static char *nc_buf_detach(NCBuf *b) {
    char *s = b->data;
    b->data = NULL;
    b->len  = 0;
    b->cap  = 0;
    return s;
}

/* ── String utilities ──────────────────────────────────── */

static char *nc_strdup(const char *s) {
    if (!s) return NULL;
    size_t n = strlen(s) + 1;
    char *d = (char *)malloc(n);
    if (d) memcpy(d, s, n);
    return d;
}

static void nc_str_lower(char *s) {
    for (; *s; s++) *s = (char)tolower((unsigned char)*s);
}

static int nc_str_contains(const char *haystack, const char *needle) {
    return strstr(haystack, needle) != NULL;
}

/* Capitalize first letter */
static void nc_str_capitalize(char *out, size_t out_sz, const char *src) {
    if (!src || !out || out_sz == 0) return;
    snprintf(out, out_sz, "%s", src);
    if (out[0]) out[0] = (char)toupper((unsigned char)out[0]);
}

/* Check if a file exists */
static int nc_file_exists(const char *path) {
    struct stat st;
    return stat(path, &st) == 0;
}

/* Build the model path: ~/.nc/model/nc_model.bin */
static void nc_model_path(char *buf, size_t sz) {
    const char *home = getenv("HOME");
    if (!home) home = ".";
    snprintf(buf, sz, "%s/.nc/model/nc_model.bin", home);
}

/* Build the tokenizer path: ~/.nc/model/nc_tokenizer.bin */
static void nc_tokenizer_path(char *buf, size_t sz) {
    const char *home = getenv("HOME");
    if (!home) home = ".";
    snprintf(buf, sz, "%s/.nc/model/nc_tokenizer.bin", home);
}

/* Add a feature to intent (avoids duplicates) */
static void nc_intent_add_feature(NCIntent *intent, const char *feature) {
    if (!intent || !feature) return;
    for (int i = 0; i < intent->n_features; i++) {
        if (strcmp(intent->features[i], feature) == 0) return;
    }
    if (intent->n_features >= NC_MAX_FEATURES) return;
    intent->features[intent->n_features++] = nc_strdup(feature);
}

/* Check if intent has a specific feature */
static int nc_intent_has_feature(const NCIntent *intent, const char *feature) {
    for (int i = 0; i < intent->n_features; i++) {
        if (strcmp(intent->features[i], feature) == 0) return 1;
    }
    return 0;
}

/* Write string to file */
static int nc_write_file(const char *path, const char *content) {
    FILE *f = fopen(path, "w");
    if (!f) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: cannot write to '%s': %s\n", path, strerror(errno));
        return -1;
    }
    fputs(content, f);
    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

/* Tokenizer functions now provided by nc_tokenizer.c */

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Intent parser — rule-based NLU
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/*
 * Strips common preamble phrases ("make me a", "create a", etc.)
 * from a lowered copy of the description.  Returns a malloc'd copy.
 */
static char *nc_strip_preamble(const char *desc) {
    char *low = nc_strdup(desc);
    nc_str_lower(low);

    /* Remove leading preamble phrases */
    static const char *preambles[] = {
        "please generate ", "please create ", "please make ", "please build ",
        "can you generate ", "can you create ", "can you make ", "can you build ",
        "i want a ", "i need a ", "i would like a ", "i'd like a ",
        "generate me a ", "create me a ", "build me a ", "make me a ",
        "generate a ", "create a ", "build a ", "make a ",
        "generate an ", "create an ", "build an ", "make an ",
        "generate ", "create ", "build ", "make ",
        "a ", "an ",
        NULL
    };

    for (const char **p = preambles; *p; p++) {
        size_t plen = strlen(*p);
        if (strncmp(low, *p, plen) == 0) {
            char *shifted = nc_strdup(low + plen);
            free(low);
            low = shifted;
            break;  /* only strip one */
        }
    }
    return low;
}

/* Extract the name: first quoted string, or first noun-like word */
static char *nc_extract_name(const char *stripped) {
    /* Check for quoted name */
    const char *q1 = strchr(stripped, '"');
    if (q1) {
        const char *q2 = strchr(q1 + 1, '"');
        if (q2 && q2 > q1 + 1) {
            size_t len = (size_t)(q2 - q1 - 1);
            char *name = (char *)malloc(len + 1);
            memcpy(name, q1 + 1, len);
            name[len] = '\0';
            return name;
        }
    }

    /* Skip adjectives and type words to find the core noun */
    static const char *skip_words[] = {
        "dark", "light", "simple", "complete", "full", "basic", "modern",
        "minimal", "responsive", "beautiful", "cool", "fancy", "clean",
        "new", "small", "big", "fast",
        NULL
    };

    char *copy = nc_strdup(stripped);
    char *saveptr = NULL;
    char *token = strtok_r(copy, " \t\n", &saveptr);
    char *result = NULL;

    while (token) {
        /* Skip articles, adjectives, type-words */
        int skip = 0;
        for (const char **sw = skip_words; *sw; sw++) {
            if (strcmp(token, *sw) == 0) { skip = 1; break; }
        }
        /* Skip type indicators */
        if (strcmp(token, "service") == 0 || strcmp(token, "page") == 0 ||
            strcmp(token, "website") == 0 || strcmp(token, "frontend") == 0 ||
            strcmp(token, "backend") == 0 || strcmp(token, "app") == 0 ||
            strcmp(token, "application") == 0 || strcmp(token, "api") == 0 ||
            strcmp(token, "crud") == 0 || strcmp(token, "ui") == 0) {
            skip = 1;
        }
        /* Skip conjunctions and prepositions */
        if (strcmp(token, "with") == 0 || strcmp(token, "and") == 0 ||
            strcmp(token, "for") == 0 || strcmp(token, "that") == 0 ||
            strcmp(token, "which") == 0 || strcmp(token, "the") == 0 ||
            strcmp(token, "a") == 0 || strcmp(token, "an") == 0) {
            skip = 1;
        }
        if (!skip && strlen(token) > 1) {
            result = nc_strdup(token);
            break;
        }
        token = strtok_r(NULL, " \t\n", &saveptr);
    }
    free(copy);
    return result ? result : nc_strdup("myapp");
}

NCIntent *nc_parse_intent(const char *description) {
    if (!description || !*description) return NULL;

    NCIntent *intent = (NCIntent *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCIntent));
    if (!intent) return NULL;

    intent->description = nc_strdup(description);
    intent->features    = (char **)calloc(NC_MAX_FEATURES, sizeof(char *));
    intent->n_features  = 0;
    intent->theme       = nc_strdup("light");

    /* Work with a lowered copy */
    char *stripped = nc_strip_preamble(description);

    /* ── Detect template type ──────────────────────────── */
    intent->type = NC_TMPL_SERVICE;  /* default */

    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "full") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "complete") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "fullstack") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "full-stack") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "full stack")) {
        intent->type = NC_TMPL_FULL_APP;
    } else if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "page") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "website") ||
               nc_str_contains(stripped, "frontend") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "landing") ||
               nc_str_contains(stripped, "ui ") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "ncui")) {
        intent->type = NC_TMPL_NCUI_PAGE;
    } else if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "crud")) {
        intent->type = NC_TMPL_CRUD;
    } else if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "test") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "spec")) {
        intent->type = NC_TMPL_TEST;
    } else if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "middleware") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "proxy")) {
        intent->type = NC_TMPL_MIDDLEWARE;
    } else if ((nc_str_contains(stripped, "ai") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "bot") ||
                nc_str_contains(stripped, "chat") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "ml") ||
                nc_str_contains(stripped, "intelligence")) &&
               !nc_str_contains(stripped, "crud")) {
        intent->type = NC_TMPL_AI_SERVICE;
    }

    /* If it says "app" but not "full", it's still a full app */
    if (intent->type == NC_TMPL_SERVICE &&
        (nc_str_contains(stripped, " app") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "application"))) {
        intent->type = NC_TMPL_FULL_APP;
    }

    /* ── Detect features ───────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "auth") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "login") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "signup") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "sign up") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "register") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "password")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "auth");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "crud") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "create") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "update") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "delete") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "list")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "crud");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "ai") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "intelligence") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "ml") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "model") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "moderat")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "ai");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "chat") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "messag") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "realtime") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "real-time") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "websocket") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "socket")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "realtime");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "upload") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "file") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "image") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "photo") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "media")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "upload");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "search") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "filter") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "query")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "search");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "notif") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "alert") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "email") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "mail")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "notifications");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "pay") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "stripe") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "billing") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "subscript")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "payments");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "contact") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "form")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "contact_form");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "blog") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "post") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "article")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "blog");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "dashboard") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "analytics") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "chart") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "graph")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "dashboard");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "admin") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "manage")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "admin");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "cache") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "redis")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "cache");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "rate") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "limit") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "throttle")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "rate_limit");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "log") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "monitor")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "logging");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "todo") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "task")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "todo");
        if (!nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "crud"))
            nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "crud");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "user") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "profile") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "account")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "users");
    }
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "portfolio") || nc_str_contains(stripped, "showcase") ||
        nc_str_contains(stripped, "gallery")) {
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "portfolio");
    }

    /* ── Theme ─────────────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_str_contains(stripped, "dark")) {
        free(intent->theme);
        intent->theme = nc_strdup("dark");
    }

    /* ── Name extraction ───────────────────────────────── */
    intent->name = nc_extract_name(stripped);

    free(stripped);
    return intent;
}

void nc_intent_free(NCIntent *intent) {
    if (!intent) return;
    free(intent->name);
    free(intent->description);
    free(intent->theme);
    for (int i = 0; i < intent->n_features; i++)
        free(intent->features[i]);
    free(intent->features);
    free(intent);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template: Backend API service
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_template_service(NCIntent *intent) {
    NCBuf b = nc_buf_new();
    const char *name = intent->name ? intent->name : "myservice";
    char Name[128];
    nc_str_capitalize(Name, sizeof(Name), name);

    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// %s Service — generated by NC\n", Name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// %s\n\n", intent->description ? intent->description : "");
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "service \"%s\"\n", name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "version \"1.0.0\"\n\n");

    /* ── Auth behavior ─────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "auth")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "// Authentication\n"
            "to authenticate with token:\n"
            "    if token is empty:\n"
            "        respond with error \"No token provided\"\n"
            "    set user to verify_jwt(token)\n"
            "    if user is empty:\n"
            "        respond with error \"Invalid token\"\n"
            "    respond with user\n\n"
            "to login with credentials:\n"
            "    set username to credentials.username\n"
            "    set password to credentials.password\n"
            "    set user to load(\"users.json\", username)\n"
            "    if user is empty:\n"
            "        respond with error \"User not found\"\n"
            "    if user.password is not password:\n"
            "        respond with error \"Invalid password\"\n"
            "    set token to create_jwt(user)\n"
            "    respond with token\n\n"
            "to register with data:\n"
            "    set existing to load(\"users.json\", data.username)\n"
            "    if existing is not empty:\n"
            "        respond with error \"Username taken\"\n"
            "    set data.created_at to now()\n"
            "    save data to \"users.json\"\n"
            "    set token to create_jwt(data)\n"
            "    respond with token\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── CRUD behaviors ────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "crud") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "blog") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "todo")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "// CRUD operations\n"
            "to list_%ss:\n"
            "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
            "    respond with items\n\n"
            "to get_%s with id:\n"
            "    set item to load(\"%ss.json\", id)\n"
            "    if item is empty:\n"
            "        respond with error \"%s not found\"\n"
            "    respond with item\n\n"
            "to create_%s with data:\n"
            "    set data.id to generate_id()\n"
            "    set data.created_at to now()\n"
            "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
            "    add data to items\n"
            "    save items to \"%ss.json\"\n"
            "    respond with data\n\n"
            "to update_%s with id and data:\n"
            "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
            "    set index to find_index(items, id)\n"
            "    if index is -1:\n"
            "        respond with error \"%s not found\"\n"
            "    set data.updated_at to now()\n"
            "    set items[index] to data\n"
            "    save items to \"%ss.json\"\n"
            "    respond with data\n\n"
            "to delete_%s with id:\n"
            "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
            "    set index to find_index(items, id)\n"
            "    if index is -1:\n"
            "        respond with error \"%s not found\"\n"
            "    remove items[index]\n"
            "    save items to \"%ss.json\"\n"
            "    respond with success\n\n",
            name, name,
            name, name, Name,
            name, name, name,
            name, name, Name, name,
            name, name, Name, name
        );
    }

    /* ── AI behaviors ──────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "ai")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "// AI integration\n"
            "to analyze with text:\n"
            "    ask AI \"Analyze this %s content: \" + text\n"
            "    set result to AI said\n"
            "    respond with result\n\n"
            "to summarize with content:\n"
            "    ask AI \"Summarize the following %s: \" + content\n"
            "    set summary to AI said\n"
            "    respond with summary\n\n"
            "to moderate with content:\n"
            "    ask AI \"Is this content appropriate? Reply yes or no: \" + content\n"
            "    set verdict to AI said\n"
            "    if verdict contains \"no\":\n"
            "        respond with error \"Content flagged by moderation\"\n"
            "    respond with content\n\n",
            name, name
        );
    }

    /* ── Search behavior ───────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "search")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "// Search\n"
            "to search_%ss with query:\n"
            "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
            "    set results to filter(items, query)\n"
            "    respond with results\n\n",
            name, name
        );
    }

    /* ── Upload behavior ───────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "upload")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "// File upload\n"
            "to upload_file with file:\n"
            "    if file.size > 10485760:\n"
            "        respond with error \"File too large (max 10MB)\"\n"
            "    set path to save_file(file, \"uploads/\")\n"
            "    respond with path\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── Notifications ─────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "notifications")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "// Notifications\n"
            "to notify with user_id and message:\n"
            "    set notification to create_notification(user_id, message)\n"
            "    save notification to \"notifications.json\"\n"
            "    respond with notification\n\n"
            "to get_notifications with user_id:\n"
            "    set notifs to load(\"notifications.json\", user_id)\n"
            "    respond with notifs\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── Payments ──────────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "payments")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "// Payments\n"
            "to create_payment with amount and currency:\n"
            "    set payment to init_payment(amount, currency)\n"
            "    respond with payment\n\n"
            "to verify_payment with payment_id:\n"
            "    set status to check_payment(payment_id)\n"
            "    respond with status\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── API routes ────────────────────────────────────── */
    nc_buf_append(&b, "api:\n");

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "auth")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    POST /auth/login runs login\n"
            "    POST /auth/register runs register\n"
        );
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "crud") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "blog") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "todo")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "    GET  /%ss         runs list_%ss\n"
            "    GET  /%ss/:id     runs get_%s\n"
            "    POST /%ss         runs create_%s\n"
            "    PUT  /%ss/:id     runs update_%s\n"
            "    DELETE /%ss/:id   runs delete_%s\n",
            name, name, name, name, name, name,
            name, name, name, name
        );
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "ai")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "    POST /%s/analyze    runs analyze\n"
            "    POST /%s/summarize  runs summarize\n"
            "    POST /%s/moderate   runs moderate\n",
            name, name, name
        );
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "search")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "    GET  /%ss/search  runs search_%ss\n",
            name, name
        );
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "upload")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "    POST /upload       runs upload_file\n");
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "notifications")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    GET  /notifications/:user_id runs get_notifications\n"
            "    POST /notifications           runs notify\n"
        );
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "payments")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    POST /payments          runs create_payment\n"
            "    GET  /payments/:id      runs verify_payment\n"
        );
    }

    nc_buf_append(&b, "\n");

    /* ── Middleware ─────────────────────────────────────── */
    nc_buf_append(&b, "middleware:\n");
    nc_buf_append(&b, "    cors allow all\n");

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "rate_limit")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "    rate limit 100 per minute\n");
    } else {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "    rate limit 60 per minute\n");
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "auth")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "    auth jwt on /api/*\n");
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "logging")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "    log requests to \"access.log\"\n");
    }

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "cache")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "    cache ttl 300\n");
    }

    nc_buf_append(&b, "\n");

    return nc_buf_detach(&b);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template: NC UI page
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_template_ncui_page(NCIntent *intent) {
    NCBuf b = nc_buf_new();
    const char *name = intent->name ? intent->name : "mypage";
    char Name[128];
    nc_str_capitalize(Name, sizeof(Name), name);
    const char *theme  = intent->theme ? intent->theme : "light";
    const char *accent = (strcmp(theme, "dark") == 0) ? "#00d4ff" : "#2563eb";
    const char *bg     = (strcmp(theme, "dark") == 0) ? "#0f172a" : "#ffffff";
    const char *fg     = (strcmp(theme, "dark") == 0) ? "#e2e8f0" : "#1e293b";

    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// %s Page — generated by NC\n", Name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// %s\n\n", intent->description ? intent->description : "");
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "page \"%s\"\n", Name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "theme \"%s\"\n", theme);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "accent \"%s\"\n", accent);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "background \"%s\"\n", bg);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "foreground \"%s\"\n\n", fg);

    /* ── Navigation ────────────────────────────────────── */
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "nav:\n");
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "    brand \"%s\"\n", Name);
    nc_buf_append(&b, "    links:\n");
    nc_buf_append(&b, "        link \"Home\" to \"#home\"\n");

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "blog")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "        link \"Blog\" to \"#blog\"\n");
    }
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "portfolio")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "        link \"Work\" to \"#work\"\n");
    }
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "dashboard")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "        link \"Dashboard\" to \"#dashboard\"\n");
    }
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "contact_form")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b, "        link \"Contact\" to \"#contact\"\n");
    }

    nc_buf_append(&b, "        link \"About\" to \"#about\"\n\n");

    /* ── Hero section ──────────────────────────────────── */
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "section hero centered:\n");
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "    heading \"%s\" style \"gradient\"\n", Name);

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "portfolio")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    subheading \"Developer & Designer\"\n"
            "    text \"Welcome to my portfolio. I build modern web experiences.\"\n"
            "    button \"View Work\" to \"#work\" style \"primary\"\n"
            "    button \"Contact Me\" to \"#contact\" style \"outline\"\n\n"
        );
    } else if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "blog")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    subheading \"Thoughts, stories, and ideas\"\n"
            "    text \"A place for writing and sharing knowledge.\"\n"
            "    button \"Read Latest\" to \"#blog\" style \"primary\"\n\n"
        );
    } else if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "dashboard")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    subheading \"Your analytics at a glance\"\n"
            "    text \"Track metrics, monitor performance, and gain insights.\"\n"
            "    button \"View Dashboard\" to \"#dashboard\" style \"primary\"\n\n"
        );
    } else {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "    subheading \"Welcome to %s\"\n"
            "    text \"A modern, fast, and beautiful experience.\"\n"
            "    button \"Get Started\" to \"#main\" style \"primary\"\n\n",
            Name
        );
    }

    /* ── Portfolio section ─────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "portfolio")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "section work id \"work\":\n"
            "    heading \"My Work\"\n"
            "    grid columns 3 gap \"1.5rem\":\n"
            "        card:\n"
            "            image \"project1.png\"\n"
            "            heading \"Project One\"\n"
            "            text \"A description of the first project.\"\n"
            "            link \"View\" to \"/projects/1\"\n"
            "        card:\n"
            "            image \"project2.png\"\n"
            "            heading \"Project Two\"\n"
            "            text \"A description of the second project.\"\n"
            "            link \"View\" to \"/projects/2\"\n"
            "        card:\n"
            "            image \"project3.png\"\n"
            "            heading \"Project Three\"\n"
            "            text \"A description of the third project.\"\n"
            "            link \"View\" to \"/projects/3\"\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── Blog section ──────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "blog")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "section blog id \"blog\":\n"
            "    heading \"Latest Posts\"\n"
            "    grid columns 2 gap \"1.5rem\":\n"
            "        card:\n"
            "            tag \"New\"\n"
            "            heading \"First Post Title\"\n"
            "            text \"A preview of the blog post content...\"\n"
            "            meta \"March 2026 · 5 min read\"\n"
            "            link \"Read More\" to \"/blog/first-post\"\n"
            "        card:\n"
            "            heading \"Second Post Title\"\n"
            "            text \"Another interesting article preview...\"\n"
            "            meta \"March 2026 · 3 min read\"\n"
            "            link \"Read More\" to \"/blog/second-post\"\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── Dashboard section ─────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "dashboard")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "section dashboard id \"dashboard\":\n"
            "    heading \"Dashboard\"\n"
            "    grid columns 4 gap \"1rem\":\n"
            "        stat-card:\n"
            "            label \"Users\"\n"
            "            value \"1,234\"\n"
            "            trend \"+12%\"\n"
            "        stat-card:\n"
            "            label \"Revenue\"\n"
            "            value \"$5,678\"\n"
            "            trend \"+8%\"\n"
            "        stat-card:\n"
            "            label \"Orders\"\n"
            "            value \"456\"\n"
            "            trend \"+23%\"\n"
            "        stat-card:\n"
            "            label \"Growth\"\n"
            "            value \"15%\"\n"
            "            trend \"+5%\"\n"
            "    chart type \"line\" data \"analytics\" title \"Traffic Over Time\"\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── Contact form ──────────────────────────────────── */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "contact_form")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "section contact id \"contact\":\n"
            "    heading \"Get in Touch\"\n"
            "    text \"Have a question or want to work together?\"\n"
            "    form action \"/api/contact\":\n"
            "        input \"Name\" type \"text\" required\n"
            "        input \"Email\" type \"email\" required\n"
            "        input \"Subject\" type \"text\"\n"
            "        textarea \"Message\" rows 5 required\n"
            "        button \"Send Message\" type \"submit\" style \"primary\"\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* ── About section ─────────────────────────────────── */
    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "section about id \"about\":\n"
        "    heading \"About %s\"\n"
        "    text \"Built with the NC programming language.\"\n\n",
        Name
    );

    /* ── Footer ────────────────────────────────────────── */
    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "footer:\n"
        "    text \"Built with NC UI\"\n"
        "    text \"© 2026 %s. All rights reserved.\"\n"
        "    links:\n"
        "        link \"GitHub\" to \"https://github.com\"\n"
        "        link \"Twitter\" to \"https://twitter.com\"\n",
        Name
    );

    return nc_buf_detach(&b);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template: Full app (backend + frontend)
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_template_full_app(NCIntent *intent) {
    /*
     * Returns a combined output with both files separated by a marker.
     * The CLI handler splits them into <name>_service.nc and <name>.ncui.
     */
    NCBuf b = nc_buf_new();

    /* Ensure features common to full apps */
    if (!nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "crud"))
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "crud");
    if (!nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "auth"))
        nc_intent_add_feature(intent, "auth");

    /* Generate backend */
    char *backend = nc_template_service(intent);
    nc_buf_append(&b, backend);
    free(backend);

    nc_buf_append(&b, "\n// === NC_FILE_SEPARATOR ===\n\n");

    /* Generate frontend */
    char *frontend = nc_template_ncui_page(intent);
    nc_buf_append(&b, frontend);
    free(frontend);

    return nc_buf_detach(&b);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template: CRUD service
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_template_crud(NCIntent *intent) {
    NCBuf b = nc_buf_new();
    const char *name = intent->name ? intent->name : "item";
    char Name[128];
    nc_str_capitalize(Name, sizeof(Name), name);

    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// %s CRUD Service — generated by NC\n\n", Name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "service \"%s_crud\"\n", name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "version \"1.0.0\"\n\n");

    /* Data model as comment */
    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "// Data model for %s:\n"
        "//   id         - unique identifier\n"
        "//   name       - display name\n"
        "//   status     - active/inactive\n"
        "//   created_at - creation timestamp\n"
        "//   updated_at - last update timestamp\n\n",
        name
    );

    /* All CRUD behaviors */
    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "to list_%ss:\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    respond with items\n\n"
        "to list_%ss_paginated with page and limit:\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    set start to (page - 1) * limit\n"
        "    set result to slice(items, start, limit)\n"
        "    respond with result\n\n"
        "to get_%s with id:\n"
        "    set item to load(\"%ss.json\", id)\n"
        "    if item is empty:\n"
        "        respond with error \"%s not found\"\n"
        "    respond with item\n\n"
        "to create_%s with data:\n"
        "    set data.id to generate_id()\n"
        "    set data.status to \"active\"\n"
        "    set data.created_at to now()\n"
        "    set data.updated_at to now()\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    add data to items\n"
        "    save items to \"%ss.json\"\n"
        "    log \"Created %s: \" + data.id\n"
        "    respond with data\n\n"
        "to update_%s with id and data:\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    set index to find_index(items, id)\n"
        "    if index is -1:\n"
        "        respond with error \"%s not found\"\n"
        "    set data.id to id\n"
        "    set data.updated_at to now()\n"
        "    set items[index] to data\n"
        "    save items to \"%ss.json\"\n"
        "    log \"Updated %s: \" + id\n"
        "    respond with data\n\n"
        "to patch_%s with id and fields:\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    set index to find_index(items, id)\n"
        "    if index is -1:\n"
        "        respond with error \"%s not found\"\n"
        "    set item to items[index]\n"
        "    merge fields into item\n"
        "    set item.updated_at to now()\n"
        "    set items[index] to item\n"
        "    save items to \"%ss.json\"\n"
        "    respond with item\n\n"
        "to delete_%s with id:\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    set index to find_index(items, id)\n"
        "    if index is -1:\n"
        "        respond with error \"%s not found\"\n"
        "    set deleted to items[index]\n"
        "    remove items[index]\n"
        "    save items to \"%ss.json\"\n"
        "    log \"Deleted %s: \" + id\n"
        "    respond with deleted\n\n"
        "to count_%ss:\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    set total to length(items)\n"
        "    respond with total\n\n"
        "to search_%ss with query:\n"
        "    set items to load(\"%ss.json\")\n"
        "    set results to filter(items, query)\n"
        "    respond with results\n\n",
        name, name,
        name, name,
        name, name, Name,
        name, name, name, name,
        name, name, Name, name, name,
        name, name, Name, name,
        name, name, Name, name, name,
        name, name,
        name, name
    );

    /* API routes */
    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "api:\n"
        "    GET    /%ss           runs list_%ss\n"
        "    GET    /%ss/count     runs count_%ss\n"
        "    GET    /%ss/search    runs search_%ss\n"
        "    GET    /%ss/:id       runs get_%s\n"
        "    POST   /%ss           runs create_%s\n"
        "    PUT    /%ss/:id       runs update_%s\n"
        "    PATCH  /%ss/:id       runs patch_%s\n"
        "    DELETE /%ss/:id       runs delete_%s\n\n",
        name, name, name, name, name, name,
        name, name, name, name, name, name,
        name, name, name, name
    );

    nc_buf_append(&b,
        "middleware:\n"
        "    cors allow all\n"
        "    rate limit 120 per minute\n"
        "    log requests to \"crud.log\"\n"
    );

    return nc_buf_detach(&b);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template: AI-powered service
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_template_ai_service(NCIntent *intent) {
    NCBuf b = nc_buf_new();
    const char *name = intent->name ? intent->name : "ai_assistant";
    char Name[128];
    nc_str_capitalize(Name, sizeof(Name), name);

    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// %s AI Service — generated by NC\n\n", Name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "service \"%s\"\n", name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "version \"1.0.0\"\n\n");

    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "// AI configuration\n"
        "set ai_model to \"default\"\n"
        "set max_context to 4096\n"
        "set temperature to 0.7\n\n"

        "// Chat with AI\n"
        "to chat with message:\n"
        "    if message is empty:\n"
        "        respond with error \"Message cannot be empty\"\n"
        "    ask AI message\n"
        "    set response to AI said\n"
        "    set entry to create_entry(message, response)\n"
        "    save entry to \"conversations.json\"\n"
        "    respond with response\n\n"

        "// Chat with context (conversation history)\n"
        "to chat_with_context with session_id and message:\n"
        "    set history to load(\"conversations.json\", session_id)\n"
        "    set context to format_context(history)\n"
        "    set prompt to context + \"\\nUser: \" + message\n"
        "    ask AI prompt\n"
        "    set response to AI said\n"
        "    set entry to create_entry(message, response)\n"
        "    set entry.session_id to session_id\n"
        "    save entry to \"conversations.json\"\n"
        "    respond with response\n\n"

        "// Analyze text\n"
        "to analyze with text:\n"
        "    ask AI \"Analyze the following text and provide key insights:\\n\" + text\n"
        "    set analysis to AI said\n"
        "    respond with analysis\n\n"

        "// Summarize content\n"
        "to summarize with content:\n"
        "    ask AI \"Provide a concise summary of:\\n\" + content\n"
        "    set summary to AI said\n"
        "    respond with summary\n\n"

        "// Classify text into categories\n"
        "to classify with text and categories:\n"
        "    set prompt to \"Classify the following text into one of these categories: \"\n"
        "    set prompt to prompt + join(categories, \", \") + \"\\nText: \" + text\n"
        "    ask AI prompt\n"
        "    set category to AI said\n"
        "    respond with category\n\n"

        "// Generate content\n"
        "to generate_content with topic and style:\n"
        "    set prompt to \"Write a \" + style + \" about \" + topic\n"
        "    ask AI prompt\n"
        "    set content to AI said\n"
        "    respond with content\n\n"

        "// Translate text\n"
        "to translate with text and target_language:\n"
        "    set prompt to \"Translate the following to \" + target_language + \":\\n\" + text\n"
        "    ask AI prompt\n"
        "    set translated to AI said\n"
        "    respond with translated\n\n"

        "// Extract entities from text\n"
        "to extract_entities with text:\n"
        "    ask AI \"Extract all named entities (people, places, organizations) from:\\n\" + text\n"
        "    set entities to AI said\n"
        "    respond with entities\n\n"

        "// Sentiment analysis\n"
        "to sentiment with text:\n"
        "    ask AI \"Analyze the sentiment of this text (positive/negative/neutral):\\n\" + text\n"
        "    set result to AI said\n"
        "    respond with result\n\n"

        "// Content moderation\n"
        "to moderate with content:\n"
        "    ask AI \"Is this content safe and appropriate? Reply with: safe, warning, or blocked.\\n\" + content\n"
        "    set verdict to AI said\n"
        "    if verdict contains \"blocked\":\n"
        "        respond with error \"Content blocked by moderation\"\n"
        "    respond with verdict\n\n"
    );

    /* API */
    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "api:\n"
        "    POST /%s/chat             runs chat\n"
        "    POST /%s/chat/context     runs chat_with_context\n"
        "    POST /%s/analyze          runs analyze\n"
        "    POST /%s/summarize        runs summarize\n"
        "    POST /%s/classify         runs classify\n"
        "    POST /%s/generate         runs generate_content\n"
        "    POST /%s/translate        runs translate\n"
        "    POST /%s/entities         runs extract_entities\n"
        "    POST /%s/sentiment        runs sentiment\n"
        "    POST /%s/moderate         runs moderate\n\n",
        name, name, name, name, name,
        name, name, name, name, name
    );

    nc_buf_append(&b,
        "middleware:\n"
        "    cors allow all\n"
        "    rate limit 30 per minute\n"
        "    auth jwt on /api/*\n"
        "    log requests to \"ai_service.log\"\n"
    );

    return nc_buf_detach(&b);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template: Middleware configuration
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_template_middleware(NCIntent *intent) {
    NCBuf b = nc_buf_new();
    const char *name = intent->name ? intent->name : "gateway";
    char Name[128];
    nc_str_capitalize(Name, sizeof(Name), name);

    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// %s Middleware — generated by NC\n\n", Name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "service \"%s_middleware\"\n", name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "version \"1.0.0\"\n\n");

    nc_buf_append(&b,
        "// Request logging\n"
        "to log_request with request:\n"
        "    set entry to format_log(request.method, request.path, now())\n"
        "    append entry to \"access.log\"\n"
        "    pass request through\n\n"

        "// CORS handler\n"
        "to handle_cors with request:\n"
        "    set response.headers.access_control_allow_origin to \"*\"\n"
        "    set response.headers.access_control_allow_methods to \"GET,POST,PUT,DELETE,PATCH\"\n"
        "    set response.headers.access_control_allow_headers to \"Content-Type,Authorization\"\n"
        "    if request.method is \"OPTIONS\":\n"
        "        respond with status 204\n"
        "    pass request through\n\n"

        "// Rate limiting\n"
        "to rate_limit with request:\n"
        "    set key to request.ip\n"
        "    set count to increment_counter(key, 60)\n"
        "    if count > 100:\n"
        "        respond with error \"Rate limit exceeded\" status 429\n"
        "    set response.headers.x_rate_limit_remaining to 100 - count\n"
        "    pass request through\n\n"

        "// JWT authentication\n"
        "to authenticate with request:\n"
        "    set token to request.headers.authorization\n"
        "    if token is empty:\n"
        "        respond with error \"No authorization header\" status 401\n"
        "    set token to replace(token, \"Bearer \", \"\")\n"
        "    set user to verify_jwt(token)\n"
        "    if user is empty:\n"
        "        respond with error \"Invalid token\" status 401\n"
        "    set request.user to user\n"
        "    pass request through\n\n"

        "// Request validation\n"
        "to validate_json with request:\n"
        "    if request.content_type is not \"application/json\":\n"
        "        respond with error \"Content-Type must be application/json\" status 415\n"
        "    if request.body is empty:\n"
        "        respond with error \"Request body is required\" status 400\n"
        "    pass request through\n\n"

        "// Response compression\n"
        "to compress_response with response:\n"
        "    if response.size > 1024:\n"
        "        set response.body to gzip(response.body)\n"
        "        set response.headers.content_encoding to \"gzip\"\n"
        "    pass response through\n\n"

        "// Error handler\n"
        "to handle_error with error:\n"
        "    log \"Error: \" + error.message + \" at \" + error.path\n"
        "    set response.status to error.code\n"
        "    set response.body to format_error(error)\n"
        "    respond with response\n\n"
    );

    nc_buf_append(&b,
        "middleware:\n"
        "    use log_request on all\n"
        "    use handle_cors on all\n"
        "    use rate_limit on all\n"
        "    use authenticate on /api/*\n"
        "    use validate_json on POST,PUT,PATCH\n"
        "    use compress_response on all\n"
        "    use handle_error on all\n"
    );

    return nc_buf_detach(&b);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Template: Test file
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_template_test(NCIntent *intent) {
    NCBuf b = nc_buf_new();
    const char *name = intent->name ? intent->name : "myservice";
    char Name[128];
    nc_str_capitalize(Name, sizeof(Name), name);

    nc_buf_printf(&b, "// Tests for %s — generated by NC\n\n", Name);
    nc_buf_printf(&b, "test \"%s\"\n\n", name);

    /* Basic lifecycle tests */
    nc_buf_printf(&b,
        "// Health check\n"
        "to test_health:\n"
        "    set response to GET \"/health\"\n"
        "    assert response.status is 200\n"
        "    assert response.body.status is \"ok\"\n\n"
    );

    /* CRUD tests if applicable */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "crud") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "todo") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "blog")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "// Test create\n"
            "to test_create_%s:\n"
            "    set data to {\"name\": \"Test %s\"}\n"
            "    set response to POST \"/%ss\" with data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body.name is \"Test %s\"\n"
            "    assert response.body.id is not empty\n"
            "    set created_id to response.body.id\n\n"

            "// Test list\n"
            "to test_list_%ss:\n"
            "    set response to GET \"/%ss\"\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body is a list\n"
            "    assert length(response.body) > 0\n\n"

            "// Test get by id\n"
            "to test_get_%s:\n"
            "    set data to {\"name\": \"Fetch Test\"}\n"
            "    set create_res to POST \"/%ss\" with data\n"
            "    set id to create_res.body.id\n"
            "    set response to GET \"/%ss/\" + id\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body.name is \"Fetch Test\"\n\n"

            "// Test update\n"
            "to test_update_%s:\n"
            "    set data to {\"name\": \"Original\"}\n"
            "    set create_res to POST \"/%ss\" with data\n"
            "    set id to create_res.body.id\n"
            "    set update_data to {\"name\": \"Updated\"}\n"
            "    set response to PUT \"/%ss/\" + id with update_data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body.name is \"Updated\"\n\n"

            "// Test delete\n"
            "to test_delete_%s:\n"
            "    set data to {\"name\": \"To Delete\"}\n"
            "    set create_res to POST \"/%ss\" with data\n"
            "    set id to create_res.body.id\n"
            "    set response to DELETE \"/%ss/\" + id\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    set get_res to GET \"/%ss/\" + id\n"
            "    assert get_res.status is 404\n\n"

            "// Test not found\n"
            "to test_%s_not_found:\n"
            "    set response to GET \"/%ss/nonexistent_id\"\n"
            "    assert response.status is 404\n\n",
            name, Name, name, Name,
            name, name,
            name, name, name,
            name, name, name,
            name, name, name, name,
            name, name
        );
    }

    /* Auth tests */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "auth")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "// Test registration\n"
            "to test_register:\n"
            "    set data to {\"username\": \"testuser\", \"password\": \"secret123\"}\n"
            "    set response to POST \"/auth/register\" with data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body.token is not empty\n\n"

            "// Test login\n"
            "to test_login:\n"
            "    set data to {\"username\": \"testuser\", \"password\": \"secret123\"}\n"
            "    set response to POST \"/auth/login\" with data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body.token is not empty\n\n"

            "// Test invalid login\n"
            "to test_invalid_login:\n"
            "    set data to {\"username\": \"testuser\", \"password\": \"wrong\"}\n"
            "    set response to POST \"/auth/login\" with data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 401\n\n"

            "// Test protected endpoint without token\n"
            "to test_no_auth:\n"
            "    set response to GET \"/api/protected\"\n"
            "    assert response.status is 401\n\n"
        );
    }

    /* AI tests */
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "ai")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "// Test AI analysis\n"
            "to test_analyze:\n"
            "    set data to {\"text\": \"This is a test document for analysis.\"}\n"
            "    set response to POST \"/%s/analyze\" with data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body is not empty\n\n"

            "// Test AI summarize\n"
            "to test_summarize:\n"
            "    set data to {\"content\": \"A long piece of content that needs summarization.\"}\n"
            "    set response to POST \"/%s/summarize\" with data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 200\n"
            "    assert response.body is not empty\n\n"

            "// Test empty input\n"
            "to test_empty_input:\n"
            "    set data to {\"text\": \"\"}\n"
            "    set response to POST \"/%s/analyze\" with data\n"
            "    assert response.status is 400\n\n",
            name, name, name
        );
    }

    /* Run block */
    nc_buf_append(&b,
        "run:\n"
        "    run test_health\n"
    );

    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "crud") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "todo") ||
        nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "blog")) {
        nc_buf_printf(&b,
            "    run test_create_%s\n"
            "    run test_list_%ss\n"
            "    run test_get_%s\n"
            "    run test_update_%s\n"
            "    run test_delete_%s\n"
            "    run test_%s_not_found\n",
            name, name, name, name, name, name
        );
    }
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "auth")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    run test_register\n"
            "    run test_login\n"
            "    run test_invalid_login\n"
            "    run test_no_auth\n"
        );
    }
    if (nc_intent_has_feature(intent, "ai")) {
        nc_buf_append(&b,
            "    run test_analyze\n"
            "    run test_summarize\n"
            "    run test_empty_input\n"
        );
    }

    return nc_buf_detach(&b);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Code validation (stub — calls into NC compiler)
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

int nc_validate_generated(const char *code, const char *type) {
    if (!code || !*code) return 0;

    /*
     * Basic structural validation without requiring the full compiler
     * linkage. Checks that the generated code has the expected
     * top-level keywords for its type.
     */
    if (type && strcmp(type, "ncui") == 0) {
        if (!nc_str_contains(code, "page "))   return 0;
        if (!nc_str_contains(code, "nav:"))    return 0;
        if (!nc_str_contains(code, "section")) return 0;
        return 1;
    }

    /* .nc backend code */
    if (!nc_str_contains(code, "service ") && !nc_str_contains(code, "test "))
        return 0;
    if (!nc_str_contains(code, "to "))
        return 0;
    return 1;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Generator lifecycle
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

NCGenerator *nc_generator_create(void) {
    NCGenerator *gen = (NCGenerator *)calloc(1, sizeof(NCGenerator));
    if (!gen) return NULL;
    gen->config = nc_generate_default_config();
    gen->use_model = 0;

    /* Try to load model if it exists */
    char model_path[1024], tok_path[1024];
    nc_model_path(model_path, sizeof(model_path));
    nc_tokenizer_path(tok_path, sizeof(tok_path));

    if (nc_file_exists(model_path) && nc_file_exists(tok_path)) {
        gen->model = nc_model_load(model_path);
        gen->tokenizer = nc_tokenizer_load(tok_path);
        if (gen->model && gen->tokenizer) {
            gen->use_model = 1;
        }
    }
    return gen;
}

void nc_generator_free(NCGenerator *gen) {
    if (!gen) return;
    if (gen->model)     nc_model_free(gen->model);
    if (gen->tokenizer) nc_tokenizer_free(gen->tokenizer);
    free(gen);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Model-based generation
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static char *nc_generate_with_model(NCGenerator *gen, NCIntent *intent) {
    if (!gen->model || !gen->tokenizer) return NULL;

    /* Build the prompt */
    NCBuf prompt = nc_buf_new();
    nc_buf_append(&prompt, "<|begin|>\n");
    nc_buf_printf(&prompt, "// Description: %s\n",
                  intent->description ? intent->description : "");

    switch (intent->type) {
        case NC_TMPL_SERVICE:    nc_buf_append(&prompt, "// Type: service\nservice \""); break;
        case NC_TMPL_NCUI_PAGE:  nc_buf_append(&prompt, "// Type: page\npage \""); break;
        case NC_TMPL_FULL_APP:   nc_buf_append(&prompt, "// Type: full app\nservice \""); break;
        case NC_TMPL_CRUD:       nc_buf_append(&prompt, "// Type: crud\nservice \""); break;
        case NC_TMPL_AI_SERVICE: nc_buf_append(&prompt, "// Type: ai service\nservice \""); break;
        case NC_TMPL_MIDDLEWARE: nc_buf_append(&prompt, "// Type: middleware\nservice \""); break;
        case NC_TMPL_TEST:       nc_buf_append(&prompt, "// Type: test\ntest \""); break;
    }

    if (intent->name) nc_buf_append(&prompt, intent->name);
    nc_buf_append(&prompt, "\"\n");

    /* Tokenize the prompt */
    int prompt_tokens[512];
    int prompt_len = nc_tokenizer_encode(gen->tokenizer, prompt.data,
                                          prompt_tokens, 512);
    nc_buf_free(&prompt);

    if (prompt_len <= 0) {
        return NULL;
    }

    /* Generate tokens */
    int max_out = gen->config.max_tokens;
    int *output = (int *)malloc((size_t)(prompt_len + max_out) * sizeof(int));
    if (!output) { return NULL; }

    memcpy(output, prompt_tokens, (size_t)prompt_len * sizeof(int));
    int total = nc_model_generate(gen->model, prompt_tokens, prompt_len,
                                  max_out, gen->config.temperature, output);

    if (total <= 0) { free(output); return NULL; }

    /* Decode back to text */
    char code_buf[8192];
    nc_tokenizer_decode(gen->tokenizer, output, total, code_buf, 8192);
    char *code = nc_strdup(code_buf);
    free(output);

    /* Post-process: remove <|begin|> marker if present */
    if (code) {
        char *marker = strstr(code, "<|begin|>\n");
        if (marker == code) {
            char *shifted = nc_strdup(code + 10);
            free(code);
            code = shifted;
        }
    }

    return code;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  Top-level generation dispatch
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

char *nc_generate_from_intent(NCGenerator *gen, NCIntent *intent) {
    if (!gen || !intent) return NULL;

    /* Try neural model first */
    if (gen->use_model) {
        char *code = nc_generate_with_model(gen, intent);
        if (code) {
            /* Validate */
            const char *type = (intent->type == NC_TMPL_NCUI_PAGE) ? "ncui" : "nc";
            if (nc_validate_generated(code, type)) {
                return code;
            }
            /* Model output invalid — fall back to template */
            fprintf(stderr, "[nc] Model output failed validation, using template engine.\n");
            free(code);
        }
    }

    /* Template fallback */
    switch (intent->type) {
        case NC_TMPL_SERVICE:    return nc_template_service(intent);
        case NC_TMPL_NCUI_PAGE:  return nc_template_ncui_page(intent);
        case NC_TMPL_FULL_APP:   return nc_template_full_app(intent);
        case NC_TMPL_CRUD:       return nc_template_crud(intent);
        case NC_TMPL_AI_SERVICE: return nc_template_ai_service(intent);
        case NC_TMPL_MIDDLEWARE:  return nc_template_middleware(intent);
        case NC_TMPL_TEST:       return nc_template_test(intent);
    }
    return NULL;
}

char *nc_generate_code(NCGenerator *gen, const char *description) {
    NCIntent *intent = nc_parse_intent(description);
    if (!intent) return NULL;
    char *code = nc_generate_from_intent(gen, intent);
    nc_intent_free(intent);
    return code;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 *  CLI: nc generate
 * ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

static void nc_generate_usage(void) {
    fprintf(stderr,
        "Usage: nc generate [options] \"description\"\n\n"
        "Options:\n"
        "  --ui            Generate a NC UI page (.ncui)\n"
        "  --full          Generate full app (backend + frontend)\n"
        "  --type TYPE     Force template type: service, crud, ai, middleware, test\n"
        "  --name NAME     Override the generated service/page name\n"
        "  --theme THEME   Theme for UI pages: dark, light (default: light)\n"
        "  --output FILE   Write to specific file (default: auto-named)\n"
        "  --stdout        Print to stdout instead of file\n"
        "  --validate      Validate generated code (default: on)\n"
        "  --no-validate   Skip validation\n"
        "  --temperature T Set generation temperature (0.0-2.0, default 0.7)\n\n"
        "Examples:\n"
        "  nc generate \"a blog service with auth\"\n"
        "  nc generate --ui \"a dark portfolio page with contact form\"\n"
        "  nc generate --full \"a todo app with login\"\n"
        "  nc generate --type crud \"users\"\n"
        "  nc generate --type test \"blog service\"\n"
    );
}

int nc_cmd_generate(int argc, char **argv) {
    if (argc < 3) {
        nc_generate_usage();
        return 1;
    }

    /* Parse arguments */
    const char *description = NULL;
    const char *force_type  = NULL;
    const char *force_name  = NULL;
    const char *force_theme = NULL;
    const char *output_file = NULL;
    int to_stdout           = 0;
    int force_ui            = 0;
    int force_full          = 0;
    int validate            = 1;
    float temperature       = 0.7f;

    for (int i = 2; i < argc; i++) {
        if (strcmp(argv[i], "--help") == 0 || strcmp(argv[i], "-h") == 0) {
            nc_generate_usage();
            return 0;
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--ui") == 0) {
            force_ui = 1;
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--full") == 0) {
            force_full = 1;
        } else if (strcmp(argv[i], "--type") == 0 && i + 1 < argc) {
            force_type = argv[++i];
